sg_is_decreasing([_]).
sg_is_decreasing([A,B|R]) :- A > B, sg_is_decreasing([B|R]).

SG-SG-009 sg_is_nondecreasing([]).
sg_is_nondecreasing([_]).
sg_is_nondecreasing([A,B|R]) :- A =< B, sg_is_nondecreasing([B|R]).

SG-SG-010 sg_is_nonincreasing([]).
sg_is_nonincreasing([_]).
sg_is_nonincreasing([A,B|R]) :- A >= B, sg_is_nonincreasing([B|R]).

SG-SG-011 sg_threshold(List, T, AboveIdxs, BelowOrEqIdxs):
  N1 = length(List) - 1
  AboveIdxs = findall I where I in [0..N1], List[I] > T
  BelowOrEqIdxs = findall I where I in [0..N1], List[I] =< T

SG-SG-012 sg_row_profile(Grid, R, Values):
  Values = Grid[R]

SG-SG-013 sg_col_profile(Grid, C, Values):
  Values = map(Row -> Row[C], Grid)

SG-SG-014 sg_cross_profile(Grid, R, C, RowVals, ColVals):
  RowVals = sg_row_profile(Grid, R)
  ColVals = sg_col_profile(Grid, C)

END OF PART 120 PSEUDOCODE


PART 121 - HISTOGRAM PACK PSEUDOCODE (Layer 110)

Work Package 131: histogram pack (hi_* prefix, Layer 110).

HI-HI-001 hi_count(List, V, N):
  Matches = [X | X in List, X == V]
  N = length(Matches)

HI-HI-002 hi_freq(List, Pairs):
  Unique = sort(List)
  Pairs = [(V, hi_count(List,V)) | V in Unique]

HI-HI-003 hi_mode(List, V, N):
  [V-N | _] = hi_sorted_by_freq(List)

HI-HI-004 hi_rare(List, V, N):
  V-N = last(hi_sorted_by_freq(List))

HI-HI-005 hi_unique_vals(List, Vals):
  Vals = sort(List)

HI-HI-006 hi_unique_count(List, N):
  N = length(sort(List))

HI-HI-007 hi_sorted_by_freq(List, Pairs):
  FreqPairs = hi_freq(List)
  Keyed = [(-N)-V | V-N in FreqPairs]
  Sorted = keysort(Keyed)  // stable: preserves V-ascending for equal N
  Pairs = [V-N | (-N)-V in Sorted]

HI-HI-008 hi_top_n(List, N, TopN):
  Pairs = hi_sorted_by_freq(List)
  TopN = first N elements of Pairs

HI-HI-009 hi_has_value(List, V):
  memberchk(V, List)

HI-HI-010 hi_all_equal([H|T], H):
  forall X in T: X =:= H

HI-HI-011 hi_grid_freq(Grid, Pairs):
  Flat = flatten_one_level(Grid)
  Pairs = hi_freq(Flat)

HI-HI-012 hi_grid_mode(Grid, Color, Count):
  Flat = flatten_one_level(Grid)
  hi_mode(Flat, Color, Count)

HI-HI-013 hi_grid_rare(Grid, Color, Count):
  Flat = flatten_one_level(Grid)
  hi_rare(Flat, Color, Count)

HI-HI-014 hi_rank(List, V, Rank):
  Pairs = hi_sorted_by_freq(List)
  Rank = first I where Pairs[I-1] = V-_ (1-based), then cut

END OF PART 121 PSEUDOCODE


PART 122 - ZOOM PACK PSEUDOCODE (Layer 111)

Work Package 132: zoom pack (zm_* prefix, Layer 111).

ZM-ZM-001 zm_scale_up([], _, []).
zm_scale_up([Row|Rest], F, Big) :-
  ScaledRow = zm_scale_up_row(Row, F)
  Copies = [ScaledRow] * F  (F identical copies)
  BigRest = zm_scale_up(Rest, F)
  Big = append(Copies, BigRest)

ZM-ZM-002 zm_scale_down(Grid, F, Small):
  Small = [zm_scale_down_row(Grid[R], F) | R in 0..H-1, R mod F = 0]

ZM-ZM-003 zm_scale_up_row([], _, []).
zm_scale_up_row([V|Rest], F, BigRow) :-
  Copies = [V] * F
  BigRest = zm_scale_up_row(Rest, F)
  BigRow = append(Copies, BigRest)

ZM-ZM-004 zm_scale_down_row(Row, F, SmallRow):
  SmallRow = [Row[I] | I in 0..N-1, I mod F = 0]

ZM-ZM-005 zm_scale_factor(Small, Big, F):
  WS = width(Small)
  WB = width(Big)
  WB mod WS = 0
  F = WB // WS

ZM-ZM-006 zm_is_scaled_up(Small, Big, F):
  zm_scale_up(Small, F) = Big

ZM-ZM-007 zm_dims_up(H, W, F, BH, BW):
  BH = H * F, BW = W * F

ZM-ZM-008 zm_dims_down(H, W, F, SH, SW):
  SH = H // F, SW = W // F

ZM-ZM-009 zm_extract_block(Grid, F, BR, BC, Block):
  R0 = BR * F, C0 = BC * F, R1 = R0 + F - 1
  Block = [zm_take_cols(Grid[R], C0, F) | R in R0..R1]

ZM-ZM-010 zm_split_blocks(Grid, F, Blocks):
  NR, NC = zm_blocks_dims(Grid, F)
  Blocks = [zm_extract_block(Grid, F, BR, BC) | BR in 0..NR-1, BC in 0..NC-1]

ZM-ZM-011 zm_blocks_dims(Grid, F, NR, NC):
  NR = height(Grid) // F
  NC = width(Grid) // F

ZM-ZM-012 zm_block_color(Grid, F, BR, BC, Color):
  Block = zm_extract_block(Grid, F, BR, BC)
  Flat = flatten(Block)
  Color = Flat[0]
  forall V in Flat: V =:= Color

ZM-ZM-013 zm_scale_down_mode(Grid, F, Small):
  NR, NC = zm_blocks_dims(Grid, F)
  Small[BR][BC] = zm_mode(flatten(zm_extract_block(Grid, F, BR, BC)))
    for BR in 0..NR-1, BC in 0..NC-1
  zm_mode: most common value; tie broken by largest value

ZM-ZM-014 zm_tile_grid(Tile, NR, NC, Grid):
  TileBlockRow = [concat(Row, NC times) | Row in Tile]
  Grid = concat(TileBlockRow, NR times)

END OF PART 122 PSEUDOCODE


PART 123 - OFFSET PACK PSEUDOCODE (Layer 112)

Work Package 133: offset pack (od_* prefix, Layer 112).

OD-OD-001 od_shift_row(Row, N, Bg, Shifted):
  Keep = first (length(Row)-N) elements of Row
  BgCells = [Bg] * N
  Shifted = BgCells ++ Keep

OD-OD-002 od_shift_row_left(Row, N, Bg, Shifted):
  Skip first N elements; Keep = remaining
  BgCells = [Bg] * N
  Shifted = Keep ++ BgCells

OD-OD-003 od_roll_row(Row, N, Rolled):
  PN = N mod length(Row)
  Split = length(Row) - PN
  Prefix = Row[0..Split-1], Suffix = Row[Split..]
  Rolled = Suffix ++ Prefix

OD-OD-004 od_shift_right(Grid, N, Bg, Shifted):
  Shifted = map(Row -> od_shift_row(Row, N, Bg), Grid)

OD-OD-005 od_shift_left(Grid, N, Bg, Shifted):
  Shifted = map(Row -> od_shift_row_left(Row, N, Bg), Grid)

OD-OD-006 od_shift_down(Grid, N, Bg, Shifted):
  Keep = first (H-N) rows of Grid
  BgRows = [BgRow] * N  where BgRow = [Bg]*W
  Shifted = BgRows ++ Keep

OD-OD-007 od_shift_up(Grid, N, Bg, Shifted):
  Drop first N rows of Grid; Keep = remaining
  BgRows = [BgRow] * N
  Shifted = Keep ++ BgRows

OD-OD-008 od_shift_dir(Grid, Dir, N, Bg, Shifted):
  if Dir=right: od_shift_right
  elif Dir=left: od_shift_left
  elif Dir=down: od_shift_down
  elif Dir=up: od_shift_up

OD-OD-009 od_roll_right(Grid, N, Rolled):
  Rolled = map(Row -> od_roll_row(Row, N), Grid)

OD-OD-010 od_roll_left(Grid, N, Rolled):
  Rolled = map(Row -> od_roll_left_row(Row, N), Grid)
  od_roll_left_row: PN = N mod W; Prefix=first PN elements; Rolled=Suffix++Prefix

OD-OD-011 od_roll_down(Grid, N, Rolled):
  PN = N mod H; Split = H - PN
  Prefix = Grid[0..Split-1]; Suffix = Grid[Split..]
  Rolled = Suffix ++ Prefix

OD-OD-012 od_roll_up(Grid, N, Rolled):
  PN = N mod H
  Prefix = Grid[0..PN-1]; Suffix = Grid[PN..]
  Rolled = Suffix ++ Prefix

OD-OD-013 od_shift_color(Grid, Color, DR, DC, Bg, Result):
  for each (R, C):
    SR = R-DR, SC = C-DC
    if in_bounds(SR,SC) and Grid[SR][SC] = Color: Result[R][C] = Color
    elif Grid[R][C] = Color: Result[R][C] = Bg
    else: Result[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

OD-OD-014 od_infer_shift(GridA, GridB, Bg, DR, DC):
  for DR in [-(H-1)..H-1]:
    for DC in [-(W-1)..W-1]:
      if od_apply_shift(GridA, DR, DC, Bg) = GridB: return DR, DC

od_apply_shift_(Grid, DR, DC, Bg, Result):
  if DR>0: T = shift_down(Grid, DR, Bg)
  elif DR<0: T = shift_up(Grid, -DR, Bg)
  else: T = Grid
  if DC>0: Result = shift_right(T, DC, Bg)
  elif DC<0: Result = shift_left(T, -DC, Bg)
  else: Result = T

END OF PART 123 PSEUDOCODE


PART 124 PSEUDOCODE: INTERLEAVE PACK

IL-IL-001 il_rows(GridA, GridB, Result):
  if GridA=[] and GridB=[]: Result=[]
  else: Result = [GridA[0], GridB[0]] ++ il_rows(tail(GridA), tail(GridB))

IL-IL-002 il_cols(GridA, GridB, Result):
  for each pair (RowA, RowB) in zip(GridA, GridB):
    ResultRow = interleave_elements(RowA, RowB)
  Result = [ResultRow for each pair]

interleave_elements(RowA, RowB):
  if RowA=[] and RowB=[]: return []
  else: return [RowA[0], RowB[0]] ++ interleave(tail(RowA), tail(RowB))

IL-IL-003 il_derows(Grid, Even, Odd):
  for I=0 to length(Grid)-1:
    if I mod 2 = 0: append Grid[I] to Even
    else: append Grid[I] to Odd

IL-IL-004 il_decols(Grid, Even, Odd):
  for each Row in Grid:
    for J=0 to length(Row)-1:
      if J mod 2 = 0: append Row[J] to EvenRow
      else: append Row[J] to OddRow
    append EvenRow to Even; append OddRow to Odd

IL-IL-005 il_weave_rows(Grid, Bg, Woven):
  if Grid=[]: Woven=[]
  elif length(Grid)=1: Woven=Grid
  else:
    W = width(Grid[0])
    BgRow = [Bg]*W
    Woven = [Grid[0], BgRow] ++ il_weave_rows(tail(Grid), Bg)

IL-IL-006 il_weave_cols(Grid, Bg, Woven):
  for each Row in Grid:
    for each element V in Row:
      append V to WovenRow
      if not last element: append Bg to WovenRow
    append WovenRow to Woven

IL-IL-007 il_unweave_rows(Grid, Core):
  Core = il_derows(Grid).Even

IL-IL-008 il_unweave_cols(Grid, Core):
  Core = il_decols(Grid).Even

IL-IL-009 il_stride_rows(Grid, Step, Start0, SubGrid):
  H = length(Grid)
  SubGrid = [Grid[I] for I in [Start0, Start0+Step, ...] if I < H]

IL-IL-010 il_stride_cols(Grid, Step, Start0, SubGrid):
  if Grid=[]: SubGrid=[]
  else:
    W = width(Grid[0])
    ColIdxs = [I for I in [Start0, Start0+Step, ...] if I < W]
    SubGrid = [[Row[I] for I in ColIdxs] for each Row in Grid]

IL-IL-011 il_select_rows(Grid, Indices, SubGrid):
  SubGrid = [Grid[I] for I in Indices]

IL-IL-012 il_select_cols(Grid, Indices, SubGrid):
  SubGrid = [[Row[I] for I in Indices] for each Row in Grid]

IL-IL-013 il_rows_n(Grids, Result):
  if Grids=[]: Result=[]
  else:
    H = length(Grids[0])
    Result = [Grids[G][I] for I in 0..H-1 for G in 0..length(Grids)-1]

IL-IL-014 il_block_rows(Grid, N, Blocks):
  if Grid=[]: Blocks=[]
  else if length(Grid) >= N:
    Block = Grid[0..N-1]
    Blocks = [Block] ++ il_block_rows(Grid[N:], N)
  else:
    Blocks = [Grid]

END OF PART 124 PSEUDOCODE


PART 125 PSEUDOCODE: PANEL PACK

PN-PN-001 pn_is_divider_row(Grid, R, Bg):
  Row = Grid[R]
  forall V in Row: V == Bg

PN-PN-002 pn_is_divider_col(Grid, C, Bg):
  forall Row in Grid: Row[C] == Bg

PN-PN-003 pn_divider_rows(Grid, Bg, Rows):
  Rows = [R for R in 0..height(Grid)-1 if pn_is_divider_row(Grid, R, Bg)]

PN-PN-004 pn_divider_cols(Grid, Bg, Cols):
  Cols = [C for C in 0..width(Grid)-1 if pn_is_divider_col(Grid, C, Bg)]

PN-PN-005 pn_split_rows(Grid, RowIdxs, Parts):
  pn_split_rows_(Grid, RowIdxs, Start=0, End=height(Grid)):
    if RowIdxs=[]: Parts = [Grid[Start:End]]
    else let Div=RowIdxs[0]:
      Parts = [Grid[Start:Div]] ++ pn_split_rows_(Grid, RowIdxs[1:], Div+1, End)

PN-PN-006 pn_split_cols(Grid, ColIdxs, Parts):
  similar to pn_split_rows but on columns using pn_slice_row_

pn_slice_row_(C0, C1, Row, Sub):
  Skip = Row[0:C0]; Sub = Row[C0:C1]

PN-PN-007 pn_auto_split_rows(Grid, Bg, Parts):
  Divs = pn_divider_rows(Grid, Bg)
  Parts = pn_split_rows(Grid, Divs)

PN-PN-008 pn_auto_split_cols(Grid, Bg, Parts):
  Divs = pn_divider_cols(Grid, Bg)
  Parts = pn_split_cols(Grid, Divs)

PN-PN-009 pn_strip_rows(Grid, Bg, Stripped):
  Divs = pn_divider_rows(Grid, Bg)
  Stripped = [Grid[I] for I in 0..H-1 if I not in Divs]

PN-PN-010 pn_strip_cols(Grid, Bg, Stripped):
  Divs = pn_divider_cols(Grid, Bg)
  Kept = [C for C in 0..W-1 if C not in Divs]
  Stripped = [[Row[C] for C in Kept] for each Row in Grid]

PN-PN-011 pn_quadrants(Grid, TL, TR, BL, BR):
  MidR = H // 2; MidC = W // 2
  TL = Grid[0:MidR, 0:MidC]
  TR = Grid[0:MidR, MidC:W]
  BL = Grid[MidR:H, 0:MidC]
  BR = Grid[MidR:H, MidC:W]

PN-PN-012 pn_n_col_parts(Grid, N, Parts):
  StepW = W // N
  Parts = [Grid[:, K*StepW:(K+1)*StepW] for K in 0..N-1]

PN-PN-013 pn_col_slices(Grid, Widths, Parts):
  Ends = cumulative_sum(Widths)
  Parts = [Grid[:, End-Width:End] for each (Width, End) in zip(Widths, Ends)]

PN-PN-014 pn_has_dividers(Grid, Bg):
  if pn_divider_rows(Grid, Bg) != []: return true
  if pn_divider_cols(Grid, Bg) != []: return true
  return false

END OF PART 125 PSEUDOCODE


PART 126 PSEUDOCODE: SCAN PACK (Layer 115, sn_* prefix)

sn_row_major(Grid, Cells):
  H1 = height(Grid) - 1
  W1 = width(Grid) - 1  (0 if empty)
  Cells = [R-C-V | R in 0..H1, C in 0..W1, V = Grid[R][C]]

sn_col_major(Grid, Cells):
  H1 = height(Grid) - 1
  W1 = width(Grid) - 1
  Cells = [R-C-V | C in 0..W1, R in 0..H1, V = Grid[R][C]]

sn_cells_of(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = [R-C | R in 0..H1, C in 0..W1, Grid[R][C] == V]

sn_set_cell(Grid, R, C, V, New):
  New = [NewRow | Ri in 0..H1,
    if Ri == R: NewRow = sn_set_elem_(Grid[Ri], C, V)
    else:        NewRow = Grid[Ri]]

sn_set_elem_(Row, C, V, New):
  New = [Cell | Ci in 0..Len1,
    if Ci == C: Cell = V
    else:        Cell = Row[Ci]]

sn_map_cells(Grid, Goal, New):
  New = [[Goal(R, C, Grid[R][C]) | C in 0..W1] | R in 0..H1]

sn_filter_cells(Grid, Pred, Cells):
  Cells = [R-C-V | R in 0..H1, C in 0..W1, V = Grid[R][C], Pred(R, C, V)]

sn_update_cells(Grid, Updates, New):
  New = [[NV | C in 0..W1,
    if R-C-NV in Updates: use NV
    else:                  NV = Grid[R][C]] | R in 0..H1]

sn_zigzag(Grid, Cells):
  Cells = [R-C-V | R in 0..H1, Offset in 0..W1,
    if R mod 2 == 0: C = Offset
    else:             C = W1 - Offset,
    V = Grid[R][C]]

sn_spiral_in(Grid, Cells):
  call sn_spiral_(Grid, 0, H-1, 0, W-1, Cells)

sn_spiral_(Grid, T, B, L, R, Cells):
  if T > B or L > R: return []
  T1 = T+1, B1 = B-1, L1 = L+1, R1 = R-1
  TopC  = [T-C-V | C in L..R]
  RightC = [Ri-R-V | Ri in T1..B]
  if T < B:
    BotFwd = [B-C-V | C in L..R-1]
    BotC = reverse(BotFwd)
  else: BotC = []
  if T1 <= B1 and L < R:
    LeftFwd = [Ri-L-V | Ri in T1..B1]
    LeftC = reverse(LeftFwd)
  else: LeftC = []
  Rest = sn_spiral_(Grid, T1, B1, L1, R1)
  return TopC ++ RightC ++ BotC ++ LeftC ++ Rest

sn_border_traversal(Grid, Cells):
  TopC = [0-C-V | C in 0..W1]
  if H > 1:
    RightC = [Ri-W1-V | Ri in 1..H1]
    BotFwd = [H1-C-V | C in 0..W1-1]; BotC = reverse(BotFwd)
    if W > 1:
      LeftFwd = [Ri-0-V | Ri in 1..H1-1]; LeftC = reverse(LeftFwd)
    else: LeftC = []
  else: RightC = BotC = LeftC = []
  return TopC ++ RightC ++ BotC ++ LeftC

sn_diag_traversal_ne(Grid, Cells):
  MaxD = H1 + W1
  Cells = [R-C-V | D in 0..MaxD, R in 0..D,
    C = D - R, R <= H1, 0 <= C <= W1, V = Grid[R][C]]

sn_diag_traversal_se(Grid, Cells):
  MinD = -H1, MaxD = W1
  Cells = [R-C-V | D in MinD..MaxD, R in 0..H1,
    C = R + D, 0 <= C <= W1, V = Grid[R][C]]

sn_grid_from_cells(H, W, Cells, Bg, Grid):
  Grid = [[V | C in 0..W1,
    if R-C-V in Cells: use V
    else:               V = Bg] | R in 0..H1]

sn_index_of(Grid, V, R, C):
  find first R, C in row-major order where Grid[R][C] == V
  commit with cut

END OF PART 126 PSEUDOCODE


PART 127 PSEUDOCODE: BOUND PACK (Layer 116, bd_* prefix)

bd_bbox(Grid, Color, R0, C0, R1, C1):
  Cells = [R-C | R in 0..H1, C in 0..W1, Grid[R][C] == Color]
  if Cells is empty: fail
  R0 = min(R for R-C in Cells), R1 = max(R ...)
  C0 = min(C for R-C in Cells), C1 = max(C ...)

bd_bbox_h(R0, R1, H): H = R1 - R0 + 1
bd_bbox_w(C0, C1, W): W = C1 - C0 + 1

bd_crop_bbox(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Sub):
  Sub = [slice(Grid[R], C0, C1) | R in R0..R1]

bd_crop_color(Grid, Color, Sub):
  bbox = bd_bbox(Grid, Color)
  return bd_crop_bbox(Grid, bbox)

bd_trim(Grid, Bg, Trimmed):
  Cells = [R-C | R in 0..H1, C in 0..W1, Grid[R][C] != Bg]
  if Cells empty: return [[]]
  bbox = (min R, min C, max R, max C) of Cells
  return bd_crop_bbox(Grid, bbox)

bd_pad(Grid, N, Bg, Padded):
  BgRow = [Bg repeated W+2*N times]
  Padding = [BgRow repeated N times]
  PaddedRows = [LeftPad ++ Row ++ RightPad | Row in Grid]
  Padded = Padding ++ PaddedRows ++ Padding

bd_place(Canvas, Patch, R0, C0, _Bg, New):
  New[R][C] = Patch[R-R0][C-C0] if 0 <= R-R0 < PH and 0 <= C-C0 < PW
            = Canvas[R][C]       otherwise

bd_center(Grid, Color, CR, CC):
  R0, C0, R1, C1 = bd_bbox(Grid, Color)
  CR = (R0 + R1) // 2, CC = (C0 + C1) // 2

bd_bbox_contains(R0, C0, R1, C1, R, C):
  R0 <= R <= R1 and C0 <= C <= C1

bd_bbox_overlap(R0A, C0A, R1A, C1A, R0B, C0B, R1B, C1B):
  R1A >= R0B and R0A <= R1B and C1A >= C0B and C0A <= C1B

bd_bbox_union(R0A, C0A, R1A, C1A, R0B, C0B, R1B, C1B, R0, C0, R1, C1):
  R0 = min(R0A, R0B), C0 = min(C0A, C0B)
  R1 = max(R1A, R1B), C1 = max(C1A, C1B)

bd_expand(R0, C0, R1, C1, N, ER0, EC0, ER1, EC1):
  ER0 = R0 - N, EC0 = C0 - N, ER1 = R1 + N, EC1 = C1 + N

bd_fill_bbox(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Color, New):
  New[R][C] = Color if R0 <= R <= R1 and C0 <= C <= C1
            = Grid[R][C] otherwise

END OF PART 127 PSEUDOCODE


PART 128 PSEUDOCODE: CELLSET PACK (Layer 117, cs_* prefix)

cs_from_grid(Grid, Color, Cells):
  H = length(Grid), W = length(Grid[0])
  Unsorted = [R-C | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] == Color]
  Cells = sort(Unsorted)

cs_to_grid(Cells, H, W, Color, Bg, Grid):
  Grid = [ [Color if R-C in Cells else Bg | C in 0..W-1] | R in 0..H-1 ]

cs_union(A, B, Union):
  Union = sort(A ++ B)

cs_intersect(A, B, Inter):
  Inter = sort([RC | RC in A, RC in B])

cs_subtract(A, B, Diff):
  Diff = [RC | RC in A, RC not in B]

cs_translate(Cells, DR, DC, Shifted):
  Shifted = [(R+DR)-(C+DC) | R-C in Cells]

cs_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, R1, C1):
  if Cells empty: fail
  R0 = min(R | R-C in Cells), R1 = max(R ...)
  C0 = min(C | R-C in Cells), C1 = max(C ...)

cs_normalize([], [], 0, 0)
cs_normalize(Cells, Norm, DR, DC):
  R0, C0, _, _ = cs_bbox(Cells)
  DR = -R0, DC = -C0
  Norm = cs_translate(Cells, DR, DC)

cs_size(Cells, N): N = length(Cells)

cs_contains(Cells, R, C): R-C in Cells (deterministic)

cs_adjacent_bg(Cells, Adjacent):
  Neighbors = [NR-NC | R-C in Cells,
                        (DR,DC) in {(-1,0),(1,0),(0,-1),(0,1)},
                        NR = R+DR, NC = C+DC,
                        NR-NC not in Cells]
  Adjacent = sort(Neighbors)

cs_same_shape(A, B):
  if A = [] and B = []: succeed
  else: cs_normalize(A) == cs_normalize(B)

cs_rotate_90(Cells, H, Rotated):
  H1 = H - 1
  Rotated = sort([C-(H1-R) | R-C in Cells])

cs_mirror_h(Cells, W, Mirrored):
  W1 = W - 1
  Mirrored = sort([R-(W1-C) | R-C in Cells])

END OF PART 128 PSEUDOCODE


PART 129 PSEUDOCODE: LOCATE PACK (Layer 118, lc_* prefix)

lc_subgrid_at(Grid, Sub, R0, C0):
  for every (SR, SC) in 0..SH-1 x 0..SW-1:
    GR = R0 + SR, GC = C0 + SC
    assert Grid[GR][GC] == Sub[SR][SC]

lc_find_sub(Grid, Sub, R0, C0):
  MaxR = H - SH, MaxC = W - SW
  for R0 in 0..MaxR, C0 in 0..MaxC:
    if lc_subgrid_at(Grid, Sub, R0, C0): return (R0, C0)
  fail

lc_all_sub(Grid, Sub, Positions):
  Positions = [(R0, C0) | R0 in 0..MaxR, C0 in 0..MaxC,
                          lc_subgrid_at(Grid, Sub, R0, C0)]

lc_subgrid_count(Grid, Sub, N):
  N = length(lc_all_sub(Grid, Sub))

lc_row_pattern(Grid, Pattern, R):
  for R in 0..H-1:
    if Grid[R] == Pattern: return R
  fail

lc_all_row_pattern(Grid, Pattern, Rows):
  Rows = [R | R in 0..H-1, Grid[R] == Pattern]

lc_col_pattern(Grid, Pattern, C):
  for C in 0..W-1:
    ColVals = [Grid[R][C] | R in 0..H-1]
    if ColVals == Pattern: return C
  fail

lc_all_col_pattern(Grid, Pattern, Cols):
  Cols = [C | C in 0..W-1, [Grid[R][C] | R in 0..H-1] == Pattern]

lc_row_prefix(Grid, R, Prefix, Rest):
  Grid[R] = Prefix ++ Rest

lc_row_suffix(Grid, R, Suffix):
  exists Prefix: Prefix ++ Suffix = Grid[R]

lc_anchor(Grid, V, R, C):
  Cells = [(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] == V]
  require length(Cells) == 1; return Cells[0]

lc_row_count(Grid, V, Counts):
  Counts = [count(V in Grid[R]) | R in 0..H-1]

lc_row_contains(Grid, V, Rows):
  Rows = sort({R | R in 0..H-1, V in Grid[R]})

lc_col_contains(Grid, V, Cols):
  Cols = sort({C | C in 0..W-1, exists R: Grid[R][C] == V})

END OF PART 129 PSEUDOCODE


PART 130 PSEUDOCODE: EXTENDED CELL SELECTION BY VALUE COMPARISON (xsel)

xs_cells_lt(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] < V])

xs_cells_gt(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] > V])

xs_cells_le(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] <= V])

xs_cells_ge(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] >= V])

xs_cells_between(Grid, Lo, Hi, Cells):
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Lo <= Grid[R][C] <= Hi])

xs_cells_ne(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] != V])

xs_max_cells(Grid, Cells):
  AllVals = [Grid[R][C] | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1]
  MaxV = max(AllVals)
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] == MaxV])

xs_min_cells(Grid, Cells):
  AllVals = [Grid[R][C] | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1]
  MinV = min(AllVals)
  Cells = sort([(R,C) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C] == MinV])

xs_threshold(Grid, T, OnV, OffV, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = OnV if Grid[R][C] >= T else OffV, for all R, C

xs_replace_lt(Grid, V, New, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = New if Grid[R][C] < V else Grid[R][C], for all R, C

xs_replace_gt(Grid, V, New, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = New if Grid[R][C] > V else Grid[R][C], for all R, C

xs_rank_vals(Grid, Vals):
  Vals = sort(unique({Grid[R][C] | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1}))

xs_val_rank(Grid, V, Rank):
  Vals = xs_rank_vals(Grid)
  Rank = index of V in Vals

xs_rank_grid(Grid, RankGrid):
  Vals = xs_rank_vals(Grid)
  RankGrid[R][C] = index of Grid[R][C] in Vals, for all R, C

END OF PART 130 PSEUDOCODE


PART 131 PSEUDOCODE: CELLULAR AUTOMATON NEIGHBORHOOD AGGREGATION (autom)

at_count_nbrs_4(Grid, V, CGrid):
  CGrid[R][C] = |{D in 4-offsets | Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == V and in-bounds}|
  for all R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1

at_count_nbrs_8(Grid, V, CGrid):
  CGrid[R][C] = |{D in 8-offsets | Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == V and in-bounds}|
  for all R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1

at_count_same_4(Grid, CGrid):
  CGrid[R][C] = |{D in 4-offsets | Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == Grid[R][C] and in-bounds}|

at_count_same_8(Grid, CGrid):
  CGrid[R][C] = |{D in 8-offsets | Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == Grid[R][C] and in-bounds}|

at_any_nbr_4(Grid, V, BGrid):
  BGrid[R][C] = 1 if exists D in 4-offsets: Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == V and in-bounds
  BGrid[R][C] = 0 otherwise

at_all_nbrs_4(Grid, V, BGrid):
  BGrid[R][C] = 1 if forall D in 4-offsets, in-bounds: Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == V
  BGrid[R][C] = 0 otherwise

at_any_nbr_8(Grid, V, BGrid):
  BGrid[R][C] = 1 if exists D in 8-offsets: Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == V and in-bounds

at_all_nbrs_8(Grid, V, BGrid):
  BGrid[R][C] = 1 if forall D in 8-offsets, in-bounds: Grid[R+DR][C+DC] == V

at_isolated_4(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = sort({(R,C) | Grid[R][C] == V and no V-valued 4-neighbor})

at_isolated_8(Grid, V, Cells):
  Cells = sort({(R,C) | Grid[R][C] == V and no V-valued 8-neighbor})

at_birth_4(Grid, Dead, Live, N, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = Live if Grid[R][C] == Dead and count_4_nbrs(Grid,R,C,Live) == N
  Grid2[R][C] = Grid[R][C] otherwise

at_birth_8(Grid, Dead, Live, N, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = Live if Grid[R][C] == Dead and count_8_nbrs(Grid,R,C,Live) == N
  Grid2[R][C] = Grid[R][C] otherwise

at_majority_4(Grid, Bg, Grid2):
  Vals = {Grid[R][C]} union {in-bounds 4-nbr values}
  Grid2[R][C] = unique_mode(Vals) if unique; else Bg

at_step_gol(Grid, Grid2):
  N = count of alive (1-valued) in-bounds 8-neighbors of (R,C)
  Grid2[R][C] = 1 if Grid[R][C]=1 and (N=2 or N=3)  [survival]
  Grid2[R][C] = 1 if Grid[R][C]=0 and N=3             [birth]
  Grid2[R][C] = 0 otherwise                            [death/quiescence]

END OF PART 131 PSEUDOCODE


PART 132 PSEUDOCODE: CROSS PACK

cx_row(Grid, R, Row):
  Row = Grid[R]   (direct nth0 lookup)

cx_col(Grid, C, Col):
  Col = [Grid[0][C], Grid[1][C], ..., Grid[H-1][C]]

cx_diag(Grid, Diag):
  Diag = [Grid[R][R] for R in 0..min(H,W)-1]

cx_antidiag(Grid, Diag):
  Diag = [Grid[R][W-1-R] for R in 0..H-1 where W-1-R >= 0]

cx_row_sum(Grid, R, Sum):
  Sum = sum(Grid[R])

cx_col_sum(Grid, C, Sum):
  Col = cx_col(Grid, C)
  Sum = sum(Col)

cx_row_count(Grid, R, V, N):
  N = count of V in Grid[R]

cx_col_count(Grid, C, V, N):
  Col = cx_col(Grid, C)
  N = count of V in Col

cx_rows_with(Grid, V, Rows):
  Rows = sorted {R | V in Grid[R]}

cx_cols_with(Grid, V, Cols):
  Cols = sorted {C | exists R such that Grid[R][C] = V}

cx_row_uniq(Grid, R, Vals):
  Vals = sorted_set(Grid[R])

cx_col_uniq(Grid, C, Vals):
  Col = cx_col(Grid, C)
  Vals = sorted_set(Col)

cx_row_mode(Grid, R, Bg, Mode):
  Mode = cx_mode_(Grid[R], Bg)

cx_col_mode(Grid, C, Bg, Mode):
  Col = cx_col(Grid, C)
  Mode = cx_mode_(Col, Bg)

cx_mode_(Vals, Bg, Mode):
  Freqs = {V: count(V, Vals) for V in unique(Vals)}
  MaxN = max(values(Freqs))
  Winners = {V | Freqs[V] = MaxN}
  Mode = Winners[0] if |Winners| = 1 else Bg

END OF PART 132 PSEUDOCODE


PART 133 PSEUDOCODE: MASK PACK

mk_from_val(Grid, V, Mask):
  Mask[R][C] = 1 if Grid[R][C] = V else 0

mk_from_bg(Grid, Bg, Mask):
  Mask[R][C] = 0 if Grid[R][C] = Bg else 1

mk_invert(Mask, Mask2):
  Mask2[R][C] = 0 if Mask[R][C] = 1 else 1

mk_and(MaskA, MaskB, MaskC):
  MaskC[R][C] = 1 if MaskA[R][C] = 1 and MaskB[R][C] = 1 else 0

mk_or(MaskA, MaskB, MaskC):
  MaskC[R][C] = 0 if MaskA[R][C] = 0 and MaskB[R][C] = 0 else 1

mk_xor(MaskA, MaskB, MaskC):
  MaskC[R][C] = (MaskA[R][C] + MaskB[R][C]) mod 2

mk_apply(Grid, Mask, Bg, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = Grid[R][C] if Mask[R][C] = 1 else Bg

mk_fill(Grid, Mask, V, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = V if Mask[R][C] = 1 else Grid[R][C]

mk_overlay(GridA, GridB, Mask, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = GridB[R][C] if Mask[R][C] = 1 else GridA[R][C]

mk_where(Mask, Cells):
  Cells = sorted {R-C | Mask[R][C] = 1}

mk_count(Mask, N):
  N = |{(R,C) | Mask[R][C] = 1}|

mk_any(Mask):
  true iff exists (R,C) such that Mask[R][C] = 1

mk_all(Mask):
  true iff forall (R,C): Mask[R][C] = 1

mk_extract(Grid, Mask, Vals):
  Vals = sorted_set {Grid[R][C] | Mask[R][C] = 1}

END OF PART 133 PSEUDOCODE


PART 134 PSEUDOCODE: TABLE PACK

tb_transpose(Grid, TGrid):
  TGrid[C] = [Grid[R][C] for R in 0..H-1]  for C in 0..W-1

tb_sort_rows(Grid, C, Sorted):
  Pairs = [(Grid[R][C], Grid[R]) for R in 0..H-1]
  Sorted = [Row for (_, Row) in keysort(Pairs)]

tb_filter_rows(Grid, C, V, Filtered):
  Filtered = [Row | Row in Grid, Row[C] = V]

tb_group_by(Grid, C, Groups):
  UniqueVs = sorted {Grid[R][C] | R in 0..H-1}
  Groups = [(V, [Row | Row in Grid, Row[C]=V]) | V in UniqueVs]

tb_count_by(Grid, C, Counts):
  Groups = tb_group_by(Grid, C)
  Counts = [(V, |Rows|) | (V, Rows) in Groups]

tb_unique_rows(Grid, UniqueGrid):
  UniqueGrid = first occurrence of each row in Grid (in document order)

tb_select_cols(Grid, ColIdxs, SubGrid):
  SubGrid[R] = [Grid[R][C] for C in ColIdxs]

tb_drop_col(Grid, C, Grid2):
  Grid2[R] = [Grid[R][Ci] for Ci in 0..W-1, Ci != C]

tb_add_col(Grid, NewCol, Grid2):
  Grid2[R] = Grid[R] ++ [NewCol[R]]

tb_insert_row(Grid, Row, R, Grid2):
  Grid2 = Grid[0..R-1] ++ [Row] ++ Grid[R..H-1]

tb_delete_row(Grid, R, Grid2):
  Grid2 = [Grid[I] for I in 0..H-1, I != R]

tb_swap_rows(Grid, R1, R2, Grid2):
  Grid2[R1] = Grid[R2]; Grid2[R2] = Grid[R1]; Grid2[I] = Grid[I] otherwise

tb_col_max_row(Grid, C, R):
  MaxV = max {Grid[I][C] | I in 0..H-1}
  R = first I such that Grid[I][C] = MaxV

tb_col_min_row(Grid, C, R):
  MinV = min {Grid[I][C] | I in 0..H-1}
  R = first I such that Grid[I][C] = MinV

END OF PART 134 PSEUDOCODE


PART 135: NUMSEQ PACK PSEUDOCODE (WP 145)

nr_diff(List, Diffs):
  if List = [] or List = [_]: Diffs = []
  else List = [A,B|T]:
    D = B - A
    Diffs = [D | nr_diff([B|T])]

nr_cumsum(List, Sums):
  if List = []: Sums = []
  if List = [H|T]:
    Sums = [H | nr_cumsum_helper(T, H)]

nr_cumsum_helper([], Acc): []
nr_cumsum_helper([H|T], Acc):
  S = Acc + H
  [S | nr_cumsum_helper(T, S)]

nr_running_max(List, Maxs):
  if List = []: Maxs = []
  if List = [H|T]: Maxs = [H | nr_running_max_helper(T, H)]

nr_running_max_helper([], Max0): []
nr_running_max_helper([H|T], Max0):
  Max1 = max(H, Max0)
  [Max1 | nr_running_max_helper(T, Max1)]

nr_running_min(List, Mins): symmetric to nr_running_max with min.

nr_zip_add(A, B, C): C[I] = A[I] + B[I] for all I.
nr_zip_sub(A, B, C): C[I] = A[I] - B[I] for all I.
nr_zip_mul(A, B, C): C[I] = A[I] * B[I] for all I.
nr_zip_max(A, B, C): C[I] = max(A[I], B[I]) for all I.
nr_zip_min(A, B, C): C[I] = min(A[I], B[I]) for all I.

nr_scale(List, K, Scaled): Scaled[I] = List[I] * K for all I.
nr_offset(List, D, Shifted): Shifted[I] = List[I] + D for all I.

nr_is_sorted(List):
  for each consecutive pair (A, B) in List: A =< B

nr_is_arith(List):
  if |List| < 2: true
  D = List[1] - List[0]
  for each consecutive pair (B, C) in List[1:]: C - B =:= D

nr_period(List, MaxP, P):
  Len = length(List)
  P = smallest value in 1..MaxP such that:
    Len mod P = 0
    and for all I in 0..(Len-P-1): List[I] = List[I+P]

END OF PART 135 PSEUDOCODE


PART 136: GRIDMATH PACK PSEUDOCODE (WP 146)

gm_add(GridA, GridB, GridC):
  for each row pair (RA, RB) in zip(GridA, GridB):
    RC[I] = RA[I] + RB[I] for all I
  GridC = list of RC rows

gm_sub(GridA, GridB, GridC): RC[I] = RA[I] - RB[I]
gm_mul(GridA, GridB, GridC): RC[I] = RA[I] * RB[I]
gm_max(GridA, GridB, GridC): RC[I] = max(RA[I], RB[I])
gm_min(GridA, GridB, GridC): RC[I] = min(RA[I], RB[I])

gm_scale(Grid, K, Grid2):
  for each Row in Grid:
    Row2[I] = Row[I] * K for all I

gm_offset(Grid, D, Grid2):
  for each Row in Grid:
    Row2[I] = Row[I] + D for all I

gm_abs(Grid, Grid2):
  for each Row in Grid:
    Row2[I] = abs(Row[I]) for all I

gm_eq_mask(GridA, GridB, Mask):
  Mask[R][C] = 1 if GridA[R][C] = GridB[R][C] else 0

gm_diff_mask(GridA, GridB, Mask):
  Mask[R][C] = 0 if GridA[R][C] = GridB[R][C] else 1

gm_clamp(Grid, Lo, Hi, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = max(Lo, min(Hi, Grid[R][C]))

gm_modulo(Grid, M, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = Grid[R][C] mod M

gm_sum(Grid, Sum):
  Vs = [V | V in Grid[R][C] for all R, C]
  Sum = sum(Vs)

gm_product(Grid, Prod):
  Vs = [V | V in Grid[R][C] for all R, C]
  Prod = product(Vs)

END OF PART 136 PSEUDOCODE


PART 137: COLORMAP PACK PSEUDOCODE (WP 147)

cm_apply(Map, Grid, Grid2):
  for each cell V in Grid:
    if V-V2 in Map: Grid2[cell] = V2
    else: Grid2[cell] = V

cm_apply_default(Map, Bg, Grid, Grid2):
  for each cell V in Grid:
    if V-V2 in Map: Grid2[cell] = V2
    else: Grid2[cell] = Bg

cm_invert(Map, Grid, Grid2):
  InvMap = [N-O | O-N in Map]
  Grid2 = cm_apply(InvMap, Grid)

cm_compose(MapA, MapB, MapAB):
  for each K-V1 in MapA:
    if V1-V2 in MapB: MapAB += [K-V2]
    else: MapAB += [K-V1]

cm_from_grids(GridA, GridB, Map):
  Pairs = {VA-VB | same position in GridA and GridB}
  Map = sort(Pairs)

cm_identity(Palette, Map): Map = [V-V | V in Palette]

cm_remap(OldVals, NewVals, Map):
  Map = [OldVals[I]-NewVals[I] | I in 0..len-1]

cm_remap_list(Map, List, List2):
  for each V in List:
    if V-V2 in Map: List2[I] = V2
    else: List2[I] = V

cm_palette(Map, Palette): Palette = sort({K | K-_ in Map})
cm_used(Grid, UsedVals): UsedVals = sort({V | V in any cell of Grid})
cm_has_key(Map, K): K-_ in Map
cm_lookup(Map, K, V): K-V in Map (first match)

cm_restrict(Map, Keys, Map2):
  Map2 = [K-V | K-V in Map, K in Keys]

cm_expand(Map, Bg, Palette, Map2):
  NewEntries = [K-Bg | K in Palette, K-_ not in Map]
  Map2 = Map ++ NewEntries

END OF PART 137 PSEUDOCODE


PART 138: BLOCK PACK PSEUDOCODE (WP 148)

bk_extract(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Block):
  Block = [[Grid[R][C] | C in C0..C1] | R in R0..R1]

bk_dims(Grid, BH, BW, NR, NC):
  NR = H // BH where H = length(Grid)
  NC = W // BW where W = length(Grid[0])

bk_split_h(Grid, BH, Strips):
  NS = H // BH
  for Si in 0..NS-1:
    R0 = Si * BH, R1 = R0 + BH - 1
    Strip = [Grid[R] | R in R0..R1]

bk_split_v(Grid, BW, Strips):
  NS = W // BW
  for Si in 0..NS-1:
    C0 = Si * BW, C1 = C0 + BW - 1
    Strip = [[Grid[R][C] | C in C0..C1] | R in 0..H-1]

bk_tile_h(Grid, N, Tiled):
  Tiled = [Row | _ in 1..N, Row in Grid]

bk_tile_v(Grid, N, Tiled):
  Tiled = [[V | _ in 1..N, V in Row] | Row in Grid]

bk_count_h(Grid, BH, N): N = H // BH
bk_count_v(Grid, BW, N): N = W // BW

bk_map(Blocks, Goal, Blocks2): maplist(Goal, Blocks, Blocks2)

bk_uniform(Grid, R, C, V): V = Grid[R][C]

bk_mode_color(Grid, R0, C0, V):
  Cells = {Grid[R][C] | R in R0..R0+1, C in C0..C0+1}
  V = most_frequent(Cells), tie-break to lowest value

bk_border_color(Grid, R0, C0, Bg):
  BorderCells = in-bounds cells in 3x3 neighborhood of (R0,C0) minus center
  Bg = most_frequent(BorderCells), tie-break to lowest value

bk_is_solid(Grid, Color, Bool):
  Bool = 1 if all cells in Grid equal Color, else 0

bk_is_border(Grid, R, C, Bool):
  Bool = 1 if R=0 or R=H-1 or C=0 or C=W-1, else 0

END OF PART 138 PSEUDOCODE


PART 139 PSEUDOCODE: EDGE DETECTION AND BOUNDARY ANALYSIS PACK

ed_h_edges(Grid, Edges):
  H = length(Grid), H2 = H - 2
  W = length(Grid[0])
  Edges = findall R-C where
    R in 0..H2, R1 = R+1
    C in 0..W-1
    Grid[R][C] != Grid[R1][C]

ed_v_edges(Grid, Edges):
  H = length(Grid)
  W = length(Grid[0]), W2 = W - 2
  Edges = findall R-C where
    R in 0..H-1
    C in 0..W2, C1 = C+1
    Grid[R][C] != Grid[R][C1]

ed_h_edge(Grid, R, C, Bool):
  R1 = R + 1
  VA = Grid[R][C], VB = Grid[R1][C]
  Bool = 1 if VA != VB else 0

ed_v_edge(Grid, R, C, Bool):
  C1 = C + 1
  VA = Grid[R][C], VB = Grid[R][C1]
  Bool = 1 if VA != VB else 0

ed_all_edges(Grid, Edges):
  HEdges = ed_h_edges(Grid)
  VEdges = ed_v_edges(Grid)
  HTerms = findall h-R-C for each R-C in HEdges
  VTerms = findall v-R-C for each R-C in VEdges
  Edges = sort(HTerms ++ VTerms)

ed_boundary_cells(Grid, Val, Cells):
  H = length(Grid), W = length(Grid[0])
  Cells = sort(findall R-C where
    R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1
    Grid[R][C] = Val
    exists 4-neighbor at (R2,C2) with Grid[R2][C2] != Val)

ed_outer_boundary(Grid, Cells):
  H = length(Grid), W = length(Grid[0])
  Cells = sort(findall R-C where
    R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1
    R=0 or R=H-1 or C=0 or C=W-1)

ed_inner_cells(Grid, Val, Cells):
  Boundary = ed_boundary_cells(Grid, Val)
  H = length(Grid), W = length(Grid[0])
  Cells = sort(findall R-C where
    R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1
    Grid[R][C] = Val
    R-C not in Boundary)

ed_edge_count(Grid, N):
  HEdges = ed_h_edges(Grid)
  VEdges = ed_v_edges(Grid)
  N = length(HEdges) + length(VEdges)

ed_is_smooth(Grid):
  ed_edge_count(Grid, 0)

ed_label_edges(Grid, Bg, Grid2):
  H = length(Grid), W = length(Grid[0])
  Grid2 = findall Row2 for R in 0..H-1 where
    Row2 = findall Label for C in 0..W-1 where
      Label = 1 if ed_has_diff_nbr_(Grid,R,C,V,H-1,W-1) else Bg

ed_has_edge(Grid, R, C, Bool):
  H = length(Grid), W = length(Grid[0])
  V = Grid[R][C]
  Bool = 1 if ed_has_diff_nbr_(Grid,R,C,V,H-1,W-1) else 0

ed_corners(Grid, Corners):
  H = length(Grid), W = length(Grid[0])
  Corners = sort(findall R-C where
    R in 0..H-2, R1 = R+1
    C in 0..W-2, C1 = C+1
    not all of Grid[R][C], Grid[R][C1], Grid[R1][C], Grid[R1][C1] are equal)

ed_corner_count(Grid, N):
  Corners = ed_corners(Grid)
  N = length(Corners)

END OF PART 139 PSEUDOCODE


PART 140 PSEUDOCODE: CELL DISTANCE AND PROXIMITY COMPUTATION PACK

dt_manhattan(R1, C1, R2, C2, D):
  D = abs(R2-R1) + abs(C2-C1)

dt_chebyshev(R1, C1, R2, C2, D):
  D = max(abs(R2-R1), abs(C2-C1))

dt_euclidean_sq(R1, C1, R2, C2, DSq):
  DR = R2-R1, DC = C2-C1
  DSq = DR*DR + DC*DC

dt_nearest(Grid, Val, R0-C0, R-C):
  Pairs = findall D-R2-C2 where Grid[R2][C2]=Val, D=dt_manhattan(R0,C0,R2,C2)
  R-C = cell from element with minimum D in Pairs

dt_farthest(Grid, Val, R0-C0, R-C):
  Pairs = findall D-R2-C2 where Grid[R2][C2]=Val, D=dt_manhattan(R0,C0,R2,C2)
  R-C = cell from element with maximum D in Pairs

dt_all_at(Grid, Val, R0-C0, D, Cells):
  Cells = sort(findall R2-C2 where Grid[R2][C2]=Val,
    dt_manhattan(R0,C0,R2,C2)=D)

dt_within_manhattan(Grid, R0, C0, D, Cells):
  Cells = sort(findall R2-C2 where dt_manhattan(R0,C0,R2,C2) <= D)

dt_within_chebyshev(Grid, R0, C0, D, Cells):
  Cells = sort(findall R2-C2 where dt_chebyshev(R0,C0,R2,C2) <= D)

dt_map_manhattan(Grid, Val, MapGrid):
  ValCells = all R-C positions where Grid[R][C]=Val
  MapGrid = for each R: for each C:
    Ds = [dt_manhattan(R,C,VR,VC) for each VR-VC in ValCells]
    min(Ds), or -1 if Ds empty

dt_map_chebyshev(Grid, Val, MapGrid):
  ValCells = all R-C positions where Grid[R][C]=Val
  MapGrid = for each R: for each C:
    Ds = [dt_chebyshev(R,C,VR,VC) for each VR-VC in ValCells]
    min(Ds), or -1 if Ds empty

dt_ring_manhattan(Grid, R0, C0, D, Cells):
  Cells = sort(findall R2-C2 where dt_manhattan(R0,C0,R2,C2)=D, in-bounds)

dt_centroid(Grid, Val, CR-CC):
  Cells = all R-C where Grid[R][C]=Val
  N = length(Cells)
  CR = floor(sum(R for R-_ in Cells) / N)
  CC = floor(sum(C for _-C in Cells) / N)

dt_diameter_manhattan(Cells, D1-D2, Diam):
  Triples = findall Dist-A-B where A,B in Cells, A<B, Dist=dt_manhattan(A,B)
  Diam-D1-D2 = element with maximum Dist

dt_diameter_chebyshev(Cells, D1-D2, Diam):
  Triples = findall Dist-A-B where A,B in Cells, A<B, Dist=dt_chebyshev(A,B)
  Diam-D1-D2 = element with maximum Dist

END OF PART 140 PSEUDOCODE


PART 141 PSEUDOCODE: GRID TOPOLOGY AND CONNECTED COMPONENT ANALYSIS PACK

tp_component(Grid, Val, Seed, Cells):
  verify Grid[Seed.R][Seed.C] = Val
  Cells = sort(BFS(Grid, Val, [Seed]))

tp_all_components(Grid, Val, Components):
  AllCells = sort(findall R-C where Grid[R][C]=Val)
  Components = tp_split_cells_(Grid, Val, AllCells)

tp_component_count(Grid, Val, N):
  N = length(tp_all_components(Grid, Val))

tp_component_size(Grid, Val, Seed, N):
  N = length(tp_component(Grid, Val, Seed))

tp_largest_component(Grid, Val, Cells):
  Comps = tp_all_components(Grid, Val)
  Tagged = [(length(C), C) for C in Comps]
  Cells = C from element with maximum length

tp_reachable(Grid, Val, Src, Dst, Bool):
  verify Grid[Src.R][Src.C] = Val
  Visited = BFS(Grid, Val, [Src])
  Bool = 1 if Dst in Visited else 0

tp_enclosed(Grid, Val, Bg, Enclosed):
  BorderBg = all border cells of value Bg
  Reachable = BFS(Grid, Bg, BorderBg)
  Enclosed = sort(all Bg cells not in Reachable)

tp_has_hole(Grid, Val, Bg, Bool):
  Enclosed = tp_enclosed(Grid, Val, Bg)
  Bool = 1 if Enclosed != [] else 0

tp_hole_count(Grid, Val, Bg, N):
  Enclosed = tp_enclosed(Grid, Val, Bg)
  N = length(tp_split_cells_plain_(Enclosed))

tp_fill_holes(Grid, Val, Bg, Grid2):
  Enclosed = tp_enclosed(Grid, Val, Bg)
  Grid2 = Grid with all Enclosed cells set to Val

tp_border_components(Grid, Val, Components):
  All = tp_all_components(Grid, Val)
  Components = [C for C in All if once(exists R-CC in C where R=0 or R=H1 or CC=0 or CC=W1)]

tp_interior_components(Grid, Val, Components):
  All = tp_all_components(Grid, Val)
  Components = [C for C in All if not(exists R-CC in C where border)]

tp_label_components(Grid, Val, LabelGrid):
  Comps = tp_all_components(Grid, Val)
  LabelMap = flat list of R-C-N triples (N = 1-based component index)
  LabelGrid = for each R,C: lookup label in LabelMap or 0

tp_same_component(Grid, Val, P1, P2, Bool):
  Bool = tp_reachable(Grid, Val, P1, P2)

Private BFS tp_grow_(Grid, Val, Queue, Visited, Result):
  if Queue = []: Result = Visited
  elif head H is in Visited: recurse on tail
  else: expand H -> find Val 4-neighbors not yet queued; add to queue; recurse

END OF PART 141 PSEUDOCODE


PART 142 PSEUDOCODE: ROW AND COLUMN PROJECTION AND PROFILE ANALYSIS (pj_*)

pj_row_sums(Grid, Sums):
  Sums = [sum(Row) for Row in Grid]
  implemented via maplist(sum_list, Grid, Sums)

pj_col_sums(Grid, Sums):
  W = width of Grid
  Sums = [sum(col(Grid, C)) for C in 0..W-1]

pj_row_counts(Grid, Val, Counts):
  Counts = [count(Val, Row) for Row in Grid]
  count via include(=(Val), Row, Occ), length(Occ, N)

pj_col_counts(Grid, Val, Counts):
  W = width of Grid
  Counts = [count(Val, col(Grid, C)) for C in 0..W-1]

pj_row_maxes(Grid, Maxes):
  Maxes = [max(Row) for Row in Grid]
  implemented via maplist(max_list, Grid, Maxes)

pj_col_maxes(Grid, Maxes):
  W = width of Grid
  Maxes = [max(col(Grid, C)) for C in 0..W-1]

pj_row_uniq(Grid, ValLists):
  ValLists = [sort(Row) for Row in Grid]

pj_col_uniq(Grid, ValLists):
  W = width of Grid
  ValLists = [sort(col(Grid, C)) for C in 0..W-1]

pj_shadow_h(Grid, Val, ColIndices):
  W = width of Grid
  Unsorted = [C for C in 0..W-1, Row in Grid, if Grid[Row][C] = Val]
  ColIndices = sort(Unsorted)

pj_shadow_v(Grid, Val, RowIndices):
  H = height of Grid
  Unsorted = [R for R in 0..H-1 if Val in Grid[R]]
  RowIndices = sort(Unsorted)

pj_h_profile(Grid, Val, Profile):
  Profile = [longest_run(Row, Val) for Row in Grid]

pj_v_profile(Grid, Val, Profile):
  W = width of Grid
  Profile = [longest_run(col(Grid, C), Val) for C in 0..W-1]

pj_row_modes(Grid, Modes):
  Modes = [mode(Row) for Row in Grid]

pj_col_modes(Grid, Modes):
  W = width of Grid
  Modes = [mode(col(Grid, C)) for C in 0..W-1]

Private pj_col_(Grid, C, Col):
  Col = [Grid[R][C] for R in 0..H-1]
  implemented via findall(V, member(Row,Grid), nth0(C,Row,V))

Private pj_longest_run_(List, Val, N):
  scan List with cur=0, max=0
  if element = Val: cur += 1; max = max(cur, max)
  else: max = max(cur, max); cur = 0
  N = max

Private pj_mode_(List, Mode):
  Unique = sort(List)
  Pairs = [(count(V, List), V) for V in Unique]
  (BestN, Mode) = pair with maximum count; on tie smallest V wins

END OF PART 142 PSEUDOCODE


PART 143 PSEUDOCODE: ROW AND COLUMN GRADIENT AND PROGRESSION ANALYSIS (gr_*)

gr_h_diffs(Grid, DiffGrid):
  DiffGrid = [adj_diffs(Row) for Row in Grid]
  adj_diffs([]) = []
  adj_diffs([_]) = []
  adj_diffs([A,B|T]) = [B-A | adj_diffs([B|T])]

gr_v_diffs(Grid, DiffGrid):
  pair up (Grid[i], Grid[i+1]) for i in 0..H-2
  DiffGrid[i] = [Grid[i+1][C] - Grid[i][C] for C in 0..W-1]

gr_h_mono(Grid, Flags):
  Flags = [mono(Row) for Row in Grid]
  mono(List):
    if is_nondec(List): return 1
    elif is_noninc(List): return -1
    else: return 0

gr_v_mono(Grid, Flags):
  Flags = [mono(col(Grid, C)) for C in 0..W-1]

gr_h_range(Grid, Ranges):
  Ranges = [max(Row) - min(Row) for Row in Grid]

gr_v_range(Grid, Ranges):
  Ranges = [max(col(Grid,C)) - min(col(Grid,C)) for C in 0..W-1]

gr_h_slope(Grid, Slopes):
  Slopes = [last(Row) - first(Row) for Row in Grid]

gr_v_slope(Grid, Slopes):
  Slopes = [last(col(Grid,C)) - first(col(Grid,C)) for C in 0..W-1]

gr_h_const(Grid, Bools):
  Bools = [1 if all_equal(Row) else 0 for Row in Grid]

gr_v_const(Grid, Bools):
  Bools = [1 if all_equal(col(Grid,C)) else 0 for C in 0..W-1]

gr_h_cum(Grid, CumGrid):
  CumGrid = [cumsum(Row) for Row in Grid]
  cumsum([]) = []
  cumsum([H|T]) = running sum: [H, H+T[0], H+T[0]+T[1], ...]

gr_v_cum(Grid, CumGrid):
  CumGrid[0] = Grid[0]
  CumGrid[i] = CumGrid[i-1] + Grid[i]  (element-wise addition)

gr_h_second(Grid, D2Grid):
  D2Grid = [adj_diffs(adj_diffs(Row)) for Row in Grid]

gr_v_second(Grid, D2Grid):
  D1 = gr_v_diffs(Grid)
  D2Grid = gr_v_diffs(D1)

Private gr_col_(Grid, C, Col):
  Col = [Grid[R][C] for R in 0..H-1]

Private gr_adj_diffs_(List, Diffs):
  base cases: [] -> [], [_] -> []
  recursive: [A,B|T] -> [B-A | adj_diffs_([B|T])]

Private gr_pair_diffs_(L1, L2, Diffs):
  Diffs[i] = L2[i] - L1[i]

Private gr_mono_(List, F):
  if gr_is_nondec_(List): F=1
  elif gr_is_noninc_(List): F=-1
  else: F=0

Private gr_is_nondec_, gr_is_noninc_: scan adjacent pairs with >= / =< guard

Private gr_all_equal_(List): scan adjacent pairs with =:= guard

Private gr_cumsum_(List, Cum): running sum via gr_cumsum_acc_ with Acc=0

Private gr_row_add_(L1, L2, L3): L3[i] = L1[i] + L2[i]

Private gr_v_cum_acc_(Grid, Prev, CumGrid):
  first row: CumRow = Row; subsequent rows: CumRow = row_add(Prev, Row)

END OF PART 143 PSEUDOCODE


PART 144 PSEUDOCODE: 2D GRID EXTREMA, LOCAL PEAKS, AND THRESHOLD FILTERING (ex_*)

ex_max_val(Grid, Val):
  Vals = [v for row in Grid, v in row]
  Val = max(Vals)

ex_min_val(Grid, Val):
  Vals = [v for row in Grid, v in row]
  Val = min(Vals)

ex_max_cells(Grid, Cells):
  Val = ex_max_val(Grid)
  Cells = sorted [(R,C) for R,C in grid if Grid[R][C] = Val]

ex_min_cells(Grid, Cells):
  Val = ex_min_val(Grid)
  Cells = sorted [(R,C) for R,C in grid if Grid[R][C] = Val]

ex_row_argmax(Grid, R):
  Pairs = [(sum(Grid[I]), I) for I in 0..H-1]
  R = I of pair with maximum sum; first on tie

ex_col_argmax(Grid, C):
  Pairs = [(sum(col(Grid,I)), I) for I in 0..W-1]
  C = I of pair with maximum sum; first on tie

ex_row_argmin(Grid, R):
  Pairs = [(sum(Grid[I]), I) for I in 0..H-1]
  R = I of pair with minimum sum; first on tie

ex_col_argmin(Grid, C):
  Pairs = [(sum(col(Grid,I)), I) for I in 0..W-1]
  C = I of pair with minimum sum; first on tie

ex_local_max4(Grid, Cells):
  Cells = sorted [(R,C) for R,C where Grid[R][C] > all in-bounds 4-neighbors]

ex_local_min4(Grid, Cells):
  Cells = sorted [(R,C) for R,C where Grid[R][C] < all in-bounds 4-neighbors]

ex_above(Grid, Thresh, Cells):
  Cells = sorted [(R,C) for R,C where Grid[R][C] > Thresh]

ex_below(Grid, Thresh, Cells):
  Cells = sorted [(R,C) for R,C where Grid[R][C] < Thresh]

ex_range(Grid, Range):
  Range = max(all vals) - min(all vals)

ex_nonzero(Grid, Cells):
  Cells = sorted [(R,C) for R,C where Grid[R][C] != 0]

Private ex_flat_vals_(Grid, Vals):
  Vals = findall(V, member(Row,Grid), member(V,Row))

Private ex_col_sum_(Grid, C, Sum):
  Vals = findall(V, member(Row,Grid), nth0(C,Row,V))
  Sum = sum(Vals)

Private ex_argmax_idx_([S-I|Rest], Best):
  ex_argmax_acc_(Rest, S, I, Best)

Private ex_argmax_acc_([], _, I, I).
Private ex_argmax_acc_([S2-I2|Rest], BestS, BestI, Final):
  if S2 > BestS: recurse with S2, I2
  else: recurse with BestS, BestI

Private ex_argmin_idx_ / ex_argmin_acc_: symmetric with < instead of >

Private ex_all_nbr4_lt_(Grid, H, W, R, C, V):
  compute RU, RD, CL, CR offsets
  for each: if in bounds, require Grid[NR][NC] < V; else succeed

Private ex_all_nbr4_gt_: symmetric with >

Private ex_check_nbr_lt_(Grid, H, W, NR, NC, V):
  if in bounds: Grid[NR][NC] < V; else succeed

Private ex_check_nbr_gt_: symmetric

END OF PART 144 PSEUDOCODE


PART 145 PSEUDOCODE: PER-CELL NEIGHBORHOOD VALUE AGGREGATION PACK

Private helper na_nbr4_vals_(Grid, H, W, R, C, Vals):
  Vals = findall(V, for each DR-DC in [-1-0, 1-0, 0-(-1), 0-1]:
    NR = R+DR, NC = C+DC; if NR in [0,H) and NC in [0,W): Grid[NR][NC])

Private helper na_nbr8_vals_(Grid, H, W, R, C, Vals):
  Vals = findall(V, for each DR-DC in the 8 diagonal and orthogonal offsets:
    NR = R+DR, NC = C+DC; if NR in [0,H) and NC in [0,W): Grid[NR][NC])

All 14 predicates use the same outer structure:
  compute H, W; H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  SumGrid = findall(Row, for each R in [0,H1]:
    Row = findall(V, for each C in [0,W1]:
      Vals = na_nbr4_vals_ (or na_nbr8_vals_);
      V = aggregate(Vals)))

na_sum4 / na_sum8: V = sum_list(Vals)  (sum_list([],0) handles empty)

na_max4 / na_max8: if Vals=[] then V=0 else V=max_list(Vals)

na_min4 / na_min8: if Vals=[] then V=0 else V=min_list(Vals)

na_mean4 / na_mean8:
  if Vals=[] then V=0
  else S=sum_list(Vals), N=length(Vals), V = S // N  (integer floor)

na_range4 / na_range8:
  N = length(Vals)
  if N < 2 then V=0 else V = max_list(Vals) - min_list(Vals)

na_spread4 / na_spread8:
  Uniq = sort(Vals)  (sort/2 removes duplicates)
  V = length(Uniq)  (0 for empty neighborhood)

na_diff4 / na_diff8:
  CV = Grid[R][C]
  Total = length(Vals)
  Same = findall(_, member(NV,Vals), NV =:= CV)
  SC = length(Same)
  V = Total - SC

END OF PART 145 PSEUDOCODE


PART 146 PSEUDOCODE: INTEGER MEDIAN COMPUTATION PACK

Private md_median_(List, M):
  msort(List, Sorted)
  N = length(Sorted)
  MI = (N - 1) // 2
  M = Sorted[MI]  (0-based nth0)

md_median(List, M): delegates to md_median_(List, M)

md_row(Grid, R, M):
  Row = nth0(R, Grid)
  md_median(Row, M)

md_col(Grid, C, M):
  ColVals = findall(V, for each Row in Grid: nth0(C, Row, V))
  md_median(ColVals, M)

md_row_medians(Grid, Ms):
  Ms = findall(M, for each Row in Grid: md_median(Row, M))

md_col_medians(Grid, Ms):
  W = width of Grid; W1 = W - 1
  Ms = findall(M, for each C in [0,W1]: md_col(Grid, C, M))

md_grid(Grid, M):
  Vals = findall(V, for each Row in Grid, each V in Row: V)
  md_median(Vals, M)

md_filter4(Grid, OutGrid):
  H = height(Grid); W = width(Grid)
  OutGrid = findall(Row, for each R in [0,H-1]:
    Row = findall(M, for each C in [0,W-1]:
      V = Grid[R][C]
      NbrVals = findall(NV, for each DR-DC in 4 offsets,
        NR=R+DR, NC=C+DC in bounds: Grid[NR][NC])
      M = md_median([V|NbrVals])))

md_filter8: same as md_filter4 with 8 direction offsets

md_above(Grid, Cells):
  Median = md_grid(Grid)
  Cells = findall(R-C, for each R,C: Grid[R][C] > Median)

md_below(Grid, Cells):
  Median = md_grid(Grid)
  Cells = findall(R-C, for each R,C: Grid[R][C] < Median)

md_row_above(Grid, R, Cells):
  Median = md_row(Grid, R)
  Row = nth0(R, Grid)
  Cells = findall(R-C, for each C in row: Row[C] > Median)

md_row_below: symmetric with Row[C] < Median

md_col_above(Grid, C, Cells):
  Median = md_col(Grid, C)
  Cells = findall(R-C, for each R: Grid[R][C] > Median)

md_col_below: symmetric with Grid[R][C] < Median

END OF PART 146 PSEUDOCODE

Part 147: Neighborhood Mode Filter Pseudocode (nm_* prefix, Layer 136)

nm_mode(List, M):
  msort(List, Sorted)
  nm_freq_pairs_(Sorted, Pairs)       % build Value-Count pairs
  extract counts from Pairs -> Counts
  max_list(Counts, MaxCount)
  collect V where V-MaxCount in Pairs -> Candidates
  sort(Candidates, [M|_])             % smallest tied value first

nm_mode_all(List, Ms):
  same as nm_mode but sort(Candidates, Ms)  % all tied values

nm_mode_count(List, M, Count):
  compute as nm_mode; Count = MaxCount

nm_row(Grid, R, M):
  nth0(R, Grid, Row); nm_mode(Row, M)

nm_col(Grid, C, M):
  findall(V, (member(Row, Grid), nth0(C, Row, V)), ColVals)
  nm_mode(ColVals, M)

nm_row_modes(Grid, Ms):
  findall(M, (member(Row, Grid), nm_mode(Row, M)), Ms)

nm_col_modes(Grid, Ms):
  W = width(Grid); W1 = W-1
  findall(M, (between(0, W1, C), nm_col(Grid, C, M)), Ms)

nm_grid(Grid, M):
  findall(V, (member(Row, Grid), member(V, Row)), Vals)
  nm_mode(Vals, M)

nm_filter4(Grid, OutGrid):
  H = height; W = width
  findall(Row,
    (between(0,H-1,R),
     findall(M,
       (between(0,W-1,C),
        V = Grid[R][C],
        NbrVals = in-bounds 4-neighbor values,
        nm_mode([V|NbrVals], M)),
       Row)),
    OutGrid)

nm_filter8: same with 8-directional offsets

nm_uniform4(Grid, Cells):
  findall(R-C,
    (between(0,H-1,R), between(0,W-1,C),
     NbrVals = 4-neighbor values,
     NbrVals not empty,
     sort(NbrVals) has exactly 1 element),
    Cells)

nm_uniform8: same with 8-neighbor values

nm_outlier4(Grid, Cells):
  findall(R-C,
    (between(0,H-1,R), between(0,W-1,C),
     V = Grid[R][C],
     NbrVals = 4-neighbor values (cell excluded),
     NbrVals not empty,
     nm_mode(NbrVals, NbrMode),
     V =\= NbrMode),
    Cells)

nm_outlier8: same with 8-neighbor values

nm_freq_pairs_(Sorted, Pairs):
  group consecutive equal elements; produce Val-Count pairs

nm_count_prefix_(Val, List, Count, Rest):
  count leading Val occurrences in List; Rest is the unmatched tail
  clause 1 (empty list) has cut to prevent clause 3 from matching

END OF PART 147

Part 148: Dense Ranking Pseudocode (rk_* prefix, Layer 137)

rk_rank_of(List, V, R):
  sort(List, Uniq)       % remove duplicates, ascending
  rk_pos1_(Uniq, V, R)  % 1-based position of V in Uniq

rk_dense(List, Ranks):
  sort(List, Uniq)
  findall(R, (member(V, List), rk_pos1_(Uniq, V, R)), Ranks)

rk_argsort_asc(List, Indices):
  numlist(0, N-1, Idxs)
  rk_zip_(List, Idxs, Pairs)   % V-I pairs
  msort(Pairs, Sorted)          % stable ascending sort by V
  findall(I, member(_-I, Sorted), Indices)

rk_argsort_desc(List, Indices):
  same as asc but negate V before msort, then extract I

rk_row_dense(Grid, RankGrid):
  findall(Ranks, (member(Row, Grid), rk_dense(Row, Ranks)), RankGrid)

rk_col_dense(Grid, RankGrid):
  for each row R:
    for each col C:
      collect ColVals = all Grid[r][C] for r in rows
      sort unique, find rank of Grid[R][C]
  return as row-first nested list

rk_grid_dense(Grid, RankGrid):
  flatten all values -> Vals
  sort(Vals, Uniq)
  for each Row: findall(R, member(V,Row), rk_pos1_(Uniq,V,R))

rk_row_rank_of(Grid, R, C, Rank):
  nth0(R, Grid, Row); nth0(C, Row, V)
  sort(Row, Uniq); rk_pos1_(Uniq, V, Rank)

rk_col_rank_of(Grid, R, C, Rank):
  findall column values; sort unique; get cell value; find its rank

rk_grid_rank_of(Grid, R, C, Rank):
  flatten; sort unique; get cell value; find its rank

rk_top_n(Grid, N, Cells):
  get sorted unique values; take last N (largest)
  findall R-C where Grid[R][C] is in TopVals

rk_bottom_n: same but take first N smallest

rk_above_rank(Grid, K, Cells):
  get unique; for each cell, compute rank; keep rank > K

rk_below_rank: same but keep rank < K

rk_pos1_: walks sorted unique list from position 1, succeeds when value matches

END OF PART 148

Part 149: Mean, Sum, and Deviation Statistics for Integer Lists and 2D Grids (vt_* prefix, Layer 138)

vt_sum(List, Sum):
  Delegate to sum_list(List, Sum).

vt_mean_floor(List, Mean):
  sum_list(List, Sum), length(List, N), N > 0, Mean is Sum // N.

vt_mean_round(List, Mean):
  sum_list(List, Sum), length(List, N), N > 0,
  Mean is round(float(Sum) / float(N)).

vt_deviation(List, Devs):
  vt_mean_floor(List, Mean),
  findall(D, (member(V, List), D is V - Mean), Devs).

vt_abs_deviation(List, AbsDevs):
  vt_mean_floor(List, Mean),
  findall(D, (member(V, List), D is abs(V - Mean)), AbsDevs).

vt_row_sums(Grid, Sums):
  findall(S, (member(Row, Grid), sum_list(Row, S)), Sums).

vt_col_sums(Grid, Sums):
  determine W from first row,
  findall(S, (between(0, W-1, C),
    findall(V, (member(Row, Grid), nth0(C, Row, V)), ColVals),
    sum_list(ColVals, S)), Sums).

vt_row_means(Grid, Means):
  findall(M, (member(Row, Grid), vt_mean_floor(Row, M)), Means).

vt_col_means(Grid, Means):
  determine W from first row,
  findall(M, (between(0, W-1, C),
    findall(V, (member(Row, Grid), nth0(C, Row, V)), ColVals),
    vt_mean_floor(ColVals, M)), Means).

vt_global_mean(Grid, Mean):
  findall(V, (member(Row, Grid), member(V, Row)), Vals),
  vt_mean_floor(Vals, Mean).

vt_above_mean(Grid, Cells):
  vt_global_mean(Grid, Mean), get H and W,
  findall(R-C, (between(0,H-1,R), between(0,W-1,C),
    nth0(R,Grid,Row), nth0(C,Row,V), V > Mean), Cells).

vt_below_mean(Grid, Cells):
  vt_global_mean(Grid, Mean), get H and W,
  findall(R-C, (between(0,H-1,R), between(0,W-1,C),
    nth0(R,Grid,Row), nth0(C,Row,V), V < Mean), Cells).

vt_row_above_mean(Grid, Cells):
  get H and W,
  findall(R-C, (between(0,H-1,R), nth0(R,Grid,Row),
    vt_mean_floor(Row, RowMean),
    between(0,W-1,C), nth0(C,Row,V), V > RowMean), Cells).

vt_col_above_mean(Grid, Cells):
  get H and W,
  findall(R-C, (between(0,H-1,R), between(0,W-1,C),
    findall(CV, (member(Row2,Grid), nth0(C,Row2,CV)), ColVals),
    vt_mean_floor(ColVals, ColMean),
    nth0(R,Grid,Row), nth0(C,Row,V), V > ColMean), Cells).

END OF PART 149

Part 150: Value Co-Occurrence and Adjacency Analysis in 2D Grids (co_* prefix, Layer 139)

co_h_pairs(Grid, Pairs):
  findall(A-B, (member(Row, Grid), co_row_adj_(Row, A, B)), Pairs).

co_v_pairs(Grid, Pairs):
  determine W from first row,
  findall(A-B, (between(0, W-1, C), co_col_adj_(Grid, C, A, B)), Pairs).

co_d_pairs_dr(Grid, Pairs):
  get H and W,
  findall(A-B, (between(0,H-1,R), between(0,W-1,C),
    R1=R+1, C1=C+1, R1=<H-1, C1=<W-1,
    nth0(R,Grid,Row), nth0(C,Row,A),
    nth0(R1,Grid,Row1), nth0(C1,Row1,B)), Pairs).

co_d_pairs_dl(Grid, Pairs):
  same but R1=R+1, C1=C-1, C1>=0.

co_count_h(Grid, V1, V2, N):
  co_h_pairs(Grid, Pairs), include(=(V1-V2), Pairs, M), length(M, N).

co_count_v(Grid, V1, V2, N):
  co_v_pairs(Grid, Pairs), include(=(V1-V2), Pairs, M), length(M, N).

co_count_adj4(Grid, V1, V2, N):
  co_h_pairs+co_v_pairs -> All,
  include(=(V1-V2), All, M1), N1 = |M1|,
  if V1==V2: N=N1, else include(=(V2-V1), All, M2), N=N1+|M2|.

co_always_adj4(Grid, V1, V2):
  \+ co_has_nonadj4_(Grid, V1, V2).

co_has_nonadj4_(Grid, V1, V2):
  exists (R,C) with value V1 where no in-bounds 4-neighbor has value V2.

co_never_adj4(Grid, V1, V2):
  \+ co_shared_border(Grid, V1, V2).

co_isolated4(Grid, V, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (V cell at (R,C) and no V in-bounds 4-neighbor), Cells).

co_border_vals(Grid, V, Vals):
  collect all NV for V cells' in-bounds 4-neighbors where NV \= V,
  sort to remove duplicates.

co_shared_border(Grid, V1, V2):
  find one V1 cell with an in-bounds 4-neighbor of value V2, cut.

co_row_transitions(Grid, Triples):
  co_h_pairs->Pairs, sort->UniqPairs,
  for each A-B in UniqPairs: count occurrences N; build N-A-B,
  msort ascending, reverse for descending,
  convert N-A-B to A-B-N.

co_most_common_adj4(Grid, V, W):
  co_border_vals->BVals (fail if empty),
  for each X in BVals: co_count_adj4(Grid,V,X,N), build N-X,
  msort, last -> _-W.

Private helpers:
  co_row_adj_: backtracks over consecutive element pairs in a list.
  co_col_adj_: backtracks over column-C values in adjacent row pairs.
  co_has_nonadj4_: true if some V1 cell has no V2 4-neighbor.

END OF PART 150

PART 151: ROWSIG PACK PSEUDOCODE (rs_* prefix, Layer 140)

rs_col_at(Grid, C, Col):
  Col <- findall(V | Row in Grid, V = Grid[Row][C])

rs_all_cols(Grid, Cols):
  W <- width of Grid (0 if empty)
  Cols <- findall(Col | C in 0..W-1, Col = rs_col_at(Grid, C))

rs_row_freq(Grid, Freqs):
  UniqRows <- sort(Grid)          // deduplicate and sort
  Raw <- findall(N-Row | Row in UniqRows,
           N = count(row=Row in Grid))
  Sorted <- msort(Raw)            // ascending by N then Row
  Rev <- reverse(Sorted)
  Freqs <- findall(Row-N | N-Row in Rev)

rs_col_freq(Grid, Freqs):
  Cols <- rs_all_cols(Grid)
  UniqCols <- sort(Cols)
  Raw <- findall(N-Col | Col in UniqCols,
           N = count(col=Col in Cols))
  Sorted <- msort(Raw)
  Rev <- reverse(Sorted)
  Freqs <- findall(Col-N | N-Col in Rev)

rs_modal_row(Grid, Row):
  UniqRows <- sort(Grid)
  Raw <- findall(N-Row2 | Row2 in UniqRows,
           N = count(row=Row2 in Grid))
  Sorted <- msort(Raw)
  Row <- last(Sorted).second      // highest N, largest row on tie

rs_modal_col(Grid, Col):
  Cols <- rs_all_cols(Grid)
  UniqCols <- sort(Cols)
  Raw <- findall(N-Col2 | Col2 in UniqCols,
           N = count(col=Col2 in Cols))
  Sorted <- msort(Raw)
  Col <- last(Sorted).second

rs_uniq_rows(Grid, Pairs):
  Pairs <- findall(R-Row | R in 0..H-1,
             Row = Grid[R],
             count(row=Row in Grid) = 1)

rs_uniq_cols(Grid, Pairs):
  Cols <- rs_all_cols(Grid)
  Pairs <- findall(C-Col | C in 0..W-1,
             Col = Cols[C],
             count(col=Col in Cols) = 1)

rs_dup_row_pairs(Grid, Pairs):
  Pairs <- findall(R1-R2 | R1 in 0..H-1, R2 in 0..H-1,
             R1 < R2, Grid[R1] = Grid[R2])

rs_dup_col_pairs(Grid, Pairs):
  Cols <- rs_all_cols(Grid)
  Pairs <- findall(C1-C2 | C1 in 0..W-1, C2 in 0..W-1,
             C1 < C2, Cols[C1] = Cols[C2])

rs_row_palindrome(Grid, R):
  Row <- Grid[R]
  succeed iff reverse(Row) = Row

rs_col_palindrome(Grid, C):
  Col <- rs_col_at(Grid, C)
  succeed iff reverse(Col) = Col

rs_rows_anagram(Grid, R1, R2):
  Row1 <- Grid[R1], Row2 <- Grid[R2]
  succeed iff msort(Row1) = msort(Row2)

rs_cols_anagram(Grid, C1, C2):
  Col1 <- rs_col_at(Grid, C1), Col2 <- rs_col_at(Grid, C2)
  succeed iff msort(Col1) = msort(Col2)

END OF PART 151

PART 152: GRIDOPS PACK PSEUDOCODE (go_* prefix, Layer 141)

go_always(Grids, V, Cells):
  NR,NC <- dims of first grid
  Cells <- findall(R-C | R in 0..NR-1, C in 0..NC-1,
             forall(Grid in Grids, Grid[R][C] = V))

go_never(Grids, V, Cells):
  NR,NC <- dims of first grid
  Cells <- findall(R-C | R in 0..NR-1, C in 0..NC-1,
             not_exists(Grid in Grids | Grid[R][C] = V))

go_sometimes(Grids, V, Cells):
  NR,NC <- dims of first grid
  Raw <- findall(R-C | R in 0..NR-1, C in 0..NC-1,
           exists(Grid in Grids | Grid[R][C]=V),
           not forall(G2 in Grids | G2[R][C]=V))
  Cells <- sort(Raw)    // deduplicate

go_count_v(Grids, V, CountGrid):
  NR,NC <- dims of first grid
  CountGrid <- matrix(NR, NC) where CountGrid[R][C] =
    count(Grid in Grids | Grid[R][C] = V)

go_modal(Grids, ModalGrid):
  NR,NC <- dims of first grid
  ModalGrid <- matrix(NR, NC) where ModalGrid[R][C] =
    mode(Grid[R][C] for Grid in Grids)   // smallest wins ties

go_stable(Grids, Triples):
  NR,NC <- dims of first grid
  V0 <- Grids[0][R][C]
  Triples <- findall(R-C-V0 | R in 0..NR-1, C in 0..NC-1,
               forall(Grid in Grids[1..] | Grid[R][C] = V0))

go_unstable(Grids, Cells):
  Stable <- go_stable(Grids)
  Cells <- findall(R-C | R,C in dims, R-C-_ not in Stable)

go_eq(G1, G2):
  succeed iff G1 = G2   // structural unification

go_add(G1, G2, G):
  G[R][C] = G1[R][C] + G2[R][C] for all R,C

go_sub(G1, G2, G):
  G[R][C] = G1[R][C] - G2[R][C] for all R,C

go_emax(G1, G2, G):
  G[R][C] = max(G1[R][C], G2[R][C]) for all R,C

go_emin(G1, G2, G):
  G[R][C] = min(G1[R][C], G2[R][C]) for all R,C

go_overlay(Grids, Bg, G):
  G[R][C] = first non-Bg value at (R,C) scanning Grids in order; Bg if all Bg

go_intersect(Grids, Bg, G):
  G[R][C] = V if all Grids have same non-Bg value V at (R,C); else Bg

go_mode_(Vals, Mode):
  count each distinct value; find max count; return smallest value at max count

END OF PART 152

PART 153: INDEX PACK PSEUDOCODE (ix_* prefix, Layer 142)

ix_row_grid(H, W, Grid):
  H1 = H - 1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1, findall(R, _ in 1..W, Row))

ix_col_grid(H, W, Grid):
  W1 = W - 1
  Grid = findall(Row, _ in 1..H, findall(C, C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_sum_grid(H, W, Grid):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1, findall(R+C, C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_diff_grid(H, W, Grid):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1, findall(R-C, C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_prod_grid(H, W, Grid):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1, findall(R*C, C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_manhattan_grid(H, W, R0, C0, Grid):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1,
           findall(abs(R-R0)+abs(C-C0), C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_chebyshev_grid(H, W, R0, C0, Grid):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1,
           findall(max(abs(R-R0),abs(C-C0)), C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_mod_grid(H, W, N, Grid):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1,
           findall((R+C) mod N, C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_row_mod_grid(H, W, N, Grid):
  H1 = H-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1,
           M = R mod N, findall(M, _ in 1..W, Row))

ix_col_mod_grid(H, W, N, Grid):
  W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, _ in 1..H,
           findall(C mod N, C in 0..W1, Row))

ix_mask_rows(Grid, Is, Bg, Grid2):
  H = length(Grid), H1 = H-1
  Grid2 = findall(Row, R in 0..H1,
            OrigRow = Grid[R],
            if R in Is then Row = OrigRow
            else Row = findall(Bg, _ in OrigRow, _))

ix_mask_cols(Grid, Js, Bg, Grid2):
  H = length(Grid), H1 = H-1
  W = length(Grid[0]), W1 = W-1
  Grid2 = findall(MRow, R in 0..H1,
            GRow = Grid[R],
            MRow = findall(V, C in 0..W1,
                     GV = GRow[C],
                     if C in Js then V=GV else V=Bg))

ix_apply(IxGrid, Op, Grid, Out):
  H = length(IxGrid), H1 = H-1
  W = length(IxGrid[0]), W1 = W-1
  Out = findall(OutRow, R in 0..H1,
          IxRow = IxGrid[R], GRow = Grid[R],
          OutRow = findall(V, C in 0..W1,
                    IX = IxRow[C], GV = GRow[C],
                    V = apply_op(Op, IX, GV)))
  apply_op(add, IX, GV) = GV + IX
  apply_op(sub, IX, GV) = GV - IX
  apply_op(mul, IX, GV) = GV * IX
  apply_op(max_op, IX, GV) = max(GV, IX)
  apply_op(min_op, IX, GV) = min(GV, IX)

ix_from(H, W, R0, C0, Grid):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1
  Grid = findall(Row, R in 0..H1,
           findall((R-R0)*W+(C-C0), C in 0..W1, Row))

END OF PART 153


PART 154: FOLD PACK PSEUDOCODE

Module: fold. Prefix: fd_*. Layer 143. Work Package 164.

fd_split_h(Grid, R, Top, Bottom):
    R1 = R + 1
    length(Top, R1)           % creates unbound list of length R+1
    append(Top, Bottom, Grid) % splits Grid at the R+1 prefix

fd_split_row_(C1, Row, LeftRow, RightRow):
    length(LeftRow, C1)
    append(LeftRow, RightRow, Row)

fd_split_v(Grid, C, Left, Right):
    C1 = C + 1
    maplist(fd_split_row_(C1), Grid, Left, Right)

fd_overlay_cell_(Bg, VA, _VB, VA):
    if VA \= Bg then VA wins (cut)
fd_overlay_cell_(_Bg, _VA, VB, VB):
    fallback: B cell used when A is background

fd_overlay_row_(Bg, RowA, RowB, RowOut):
    maplist(fd_overlay_cell_(Bg), RowA, RowB, RowOut)

fd_overlay(A, B, Bg, Out):
    maplist(fd_overlay_row_(Bg), A, B, Out)

fd_fold_h(Grid, R, Bg, Out):
    fd_split_h(Grid, R, Top, Bottom)
    HB = length(Bottom)
    HT = length(Top); HT1 = HT - 1
    Out = findall(OutRow, between(0, HT1, I):
        TopRow = Top[I]
        K = R - I
        if K >= 0 and K < HB:
            BotRow = Bottom[K]
            OutRow = fd_overlay_row_(Bg, TopRow, BotRow)
        else:
            OutRow = TopRow
    )

fd_fold_row_v_(WL, WR, C, Bg, LRow, RRow, OutRow):
    WL1 = WL - 1
    OutRow = findall(V, between(0, WL1, I):
        LV = LRow[I]
        K = C - I
        if K >= 0 and K < WR:
            RV = RRow[K]
            V = fd_overlay_cell_(Bg, LV, RV)
        else:
            V = LV
    )

fd_fold_v(Grid, C, Bg, Out):
    fd_split_v(Grid, C, Left, Right)
    WR = length(Right[0])  (or 0 if Right empty)
    WL = length(Left[0])   (or 0 if Left empty)
    maplist(fd_fold_row_v_(WL, WR, C, Bg), Left, Right, Out)

fd_unfold_h(Half, Grid):
    RevHalf = reverse(Half)
    Grid = append(Half, RevHalf)

fd_mirror_row_(LeftRow, FullRow):
    RevRow = reverse(LeftRow)
    FullRow = append(LeftRow, RevRow)

fd_unfold_v(Half, Grid):
    maplist(fd_mirror_row_, Half, Grid)

fd_sym_h(Grid, R):
    H = length(Grid); H1 = H - 1
    forall between(0, H1, I):
        IR = 2*R + 1 - I
        if IR >= 0 and IR <= H1:
            Grid[I] must equal Grid[IR]
        else: skip

fd_sym_v(Grid, C):
    H = length(Grid); H1 = H - 1
    W = length(Grid[0]); W1 = W - 1
    forall between(0, H1, R) and between(0, W1, J):
        JC = 2*C + 1 - J
        if JC >= 0 and JC <= W1:
            Grid[R][J] must equal Grid[R][JC]
        else: skip

fd_find_fold_h(Grid, R):
    H = length(Grid); H1 = H - 1
    between(0, H1, R), fd_sym_h(Grid, R), cut

fd_find_fold_v(Grid, C):
    W = length(Grid[0]); W1 = W - 1
    between(0, W1, C), fd_sym_v(Grid, C), cut

fd_mark_row(Grid, V, R):
    H = length(Grid); H1 = H - 1
    between(0, H1, R)
    Row = Grid[R]
    forall member(Cell, Row): Cell == V
    cut

fd_mark_col(Grid, V, C):
    W = length(Grid[0]); W1 = W - 1
    between(0, W1, C)
    forall member(Row, Grid): Grid[Row][C] == V
    cut

fd_fold_both(Grid, R, C, Bg, Out):
    FoldedH = fd_fold_h(Grid, R, Bg)
    Out = fd_fold_v(FoldedH, C, Bg)

END OF PART 154


PART 155: ROTATION PACK PSEUDOCODE

Module: rotation. Prefix: ro_*. Layer 144. Work Package 165.

ro_rot90(Grid, Out):
    H = length(Grid); H1 = H - 1
    W = length(Grid[0]); W1 = W - 1
    Out = findall(NewRow, between(0, W1, C):
        NewRow = findall(V, between(0, H1, R):
            R2 = H1 - R
            GRow = Grid[R2]
            V = GRow[C]
    )

ro_rot180(Grid, Out):
    Temp = maplist(reverse, Grid)   % reverse each row
    Out = reverse(Temp)             % reverse row order

ro_rot270(Grid, Out):
    H = length(Grid); H1 = H - 1
    W = length(Grid[0]); W1 = W - 1
    Out = findall(NewRow, between(0, W1, C):
        C2 = W1 - C
        NewRow = findall(V, between(0, H1, R):
            GRow = Grid[R]
            V = GRow[C2]
    )

ro_rot_n(Grid, 0, Grid) :- cut
ro_rot_n(Grid, 1, Out) :- cut, ro_rot90(Grid, Out)
ro_rot_n(Grid, 2, Out) :- cut, ro_rot180(Grid, Out)
ro_rot_n(Grid, 3, Out) :- ro_rot270(Grid, Out)

ro_all(Grid, [Grid, G90, G180, G270]):
    G90 = ro_rot90(Grid)
    G180 = ro_rot180(Grid)
    G270 = ro_rot270(Grid)

ro_canonical(Grid, Canon):
    Rots = ro_all(Grid)
    [Canon|_] = msort(Rots)

ro_is_rot2(Grid):
    Grid180 = ro_rot180(Grid)
    Grid == Grid180

ro_is_rot4(Grid):
    Grid90 = ro_rot90(Grid)
    Grid == Grid90

ro_sym_order(Grid, 4) :- ro_is_rot4(Grid), cut
ro_sym_order(Grid, 2) :- ro_is_rot2(Grid), cut
ro_sym_order(_, 1).

ro_apply_cell_(0, R, C, _, _, R, C).
ro_apply_cell_(1, R, C, H1, _, C, H1-R).
ro_apply_cell_(2, R, C, H1, W1, H1-R, W1-C).
ro_apply_cell_(3, R, C, _, W1, W1-C, R).

ro_rotate_cells(Cells, H, W, N, Out):
    H1 = H - 1; W1 = W - 1
    Out = findall(NR-NC, member(R-C, Cells):
        ro_apply_cell_(N, R, C, H1, W1, NR, NC)
    )

ro_overlay_bg_(Bg, VA, _VB, VA) :- VA \= Bg, cut
ro_overlay_bg_(_Bg, _VA, VB, VB).

ro_overlay_rows_([], [], _, []).
ro_overlay_rows_([VA|RestA], [VB|RestB], Bg, [V|RestOut]):
    ro_overlay_bg_(Bg, VA, VB, V)
    ro_overlay_rows_(RestA, RestB, Bg, RestOut)

ro_overlay_grids_([], [], _, []).
ro_overlay_grids_([RowA|RestA], [RowB|RestB], Bg, [RowOut|RestOut]):
    ro_overlay_rows_(RowA, RowB, Bg, RowOut)
    ro_overlay_grids_(RestA, RestB, Bg, RestOut)

ro_spin2(Grid, Bg, Out):
    Grid180 = ro_rot180(Grid)
    Out = ro_overlay_grids_(Grid, Grid180, Bg)

ro_spin4(Grid, Bg, Out):
    G90 = ro_rot90(Grid)
    G180 = ro_rot180(Grid)
    G270 = ro_rot270(Grid)
    Step1 = ro_overlay_grids_(Grid, G90, Bg)
    Step2 = ro_overlay_grids_(Step1, G180, Bg)
    Out = ro_overlay_grids_(Step2, G270, Bg)

ro_match_rotation(GridA, GridB, N):
    between(0, 3, N)
    ro_rot_n(GridA, N, GridB)
    cut

ro_equiv_rotation(GridA, GridB):
    ro_match_rotation(GridA, GridB, _)

END OF PART 155

PART 156: WARP PACK PSEUDOCODE

wr_dims_(Grid, H, W):
    H = length(Grid)
    if H > 0: W = length(Grid[0]) else W = 0

wr_shift_linear_(Row, N, Bg, Out):
    W = length(Row)
    Out = [Row[C-N] if (C-N in [0,W-1]) else Bg | C in 0..W-1]

wr_replace_nth_(0, [_|T], V, [V|T]): cut
wr_replace_nth_(I, [H|T], V, [H|T2]): I>0, wr_replace_nth_(I-1, T, V, T2)

wr_get_col_(Grid, C, ColVals):
    ColVals = [Row[C] | Row in Grid]

wr_put_col_([], _, [], [])
wr_put_col_([Row|Rows], C, [V|Vs], [NewRow|Rest]):
    replace position C in Row with V -> NewRow
    wr_put_col_(Rows, C, Vs, Rest)

wr_cyclic_row_(Row, N, Out):
    W = length(Row)
    Out = [Row[(C-N) mod W] | C in 0..W-1]

wr_shift_row(Grid, R, N, Bg, Out):
    Out = [shift_linear(Row, N, Bg) if I==R else Row | (I, Row) in enumerate(Grid)]

wr_shift_col(Grid, C, N, Bg, Out):
    ColVals = wr_get_col_(Grid, C)
    ShiftedCol = wr_shift_linear_(ColVals, N, Bg)
    Out = wr_put_col_(Grid, C, ShiftedCol)

wr_shear_h(Grid, Step, Bg, Out):
    Out = [shift_linear(Grid[I], I*Step, Bg) | I in 0..H-1]

wr_shear_v(Grid, Step, Bg, Out):
    Out[R][J] = Grid[R - J*Step][J] if (R - J*Step) in [0,H-1], else Bg

wr_unshear_h(Grid, Step, Bg, Out): wr_shear_h(Grid, -Step, Bg, Out)
wr_unshear_v(Grid, Step, Bg, Out): wr_shear_v(Grid, -Step, Bg, Out)

wr_cyclic_h(Grid, N, Out):
    Out = [cyclic_row(Row, N) | Row in Grid]

wr_cyclic_v(Grid, N, Out):
    Out[R][C] = Grid[(R-N) mod H][C]

wr_cyclic_shear_h(Grid, Step, Out):
    Out = [cyclic_row(Grid[I], I*Step) | I in 0..H-1]

wr_cyclic_shear_v(Grid, Step, Out):
    Out[R][J] = Grid[(R - J*Step) mod H][J]

wr_skew_offsets(Grid, Offsets, Bg, Out):
    Out = [shift_linear(Grid[I], Offsets[I], Bg) | I in 0..H-1]

wr_transpose_anti(Grid, Out):
    (H, W) = dims(Grid)
    Out[J][I] = Grid[H-1-I][W-1-J]   for J in 0..W-1, I in 0..H-1

wr_find_shear_h(GridA, GridB, Bg, Step):
    for K in 0..2*(W-1):
        Step = K - (W-1)
        Candidate = wr_shear_h(GridA, Step, Bg)
        if Candidate == GridB: return Step
    fail

wr_find_shear_v(GridA, GridB, Bg, Step):
    for K in 0..2*(H-1):
        Step = K - (H-1)
        Candidate = wr_shear_v(GridA, Step, Bg)
        if Candidate == GridB: return Step
    fail

END OF PART 156

PART 157: BORDER PACK PSEUDOCODE

br_dims_(Grid, H, W):
    H = length(Grid)
    if H > 0: W = length(Grid[0]) else W = 0

br_ring_depth_(H, W, R, C, D):
    DR1 = R; DR2 = H - 1 - R; DC1 = C; DC2 = W - 1 - C
    D = min(DR1, min(DR2, min(DC1, DC2)))

br_ring_cells(Grid, N, Cells):
    (H, W) = dims(Grid)
    H1 = H - 1; W1 = W - 1
    Cells = [R-C | R in 0..H1, C in 0..W1, br_ring_depth_(H,W,R,C) == N]

br_ring_vals(Grid, N, Vals):
    Cells = br_ring_cells(Grid, N)
    Vals = [Grid[R][C] | R-C in Cells]

br_ring_color(Grid, N, Color):
    Vals = br_ring_vals(Grid, N)
    Vals != []
    sort(Vals) == [Color]

br_is_uniform_ring(Grid, N): br_ring_color(Grid, N, _)

br_add_border_(Row, V, NewRow): NewRow = [V] ++ Row ++ [V]

br_add_border(Grid, V, Out):
    W = width(Grid); NewW = W + 2
    TopBot = list of NewW copies of V
    MiddleRows = [V ++ Row ++ [V] | Row in Grid]
    Out = [TopBot] ++ MiddleRows ++ [TopBot]

br_strip_border(Grid, Inner):
    (H, W) = dims(Grid); H2 = H - 2; W2 = W - 2
    if H2 > 0 and W2 > 0:
        Inner = [[Grid[R][C] | C in 1..W2] | R in 1..H2]
    else: Inner = []

br_inner_n(Grid, 0, Grid): return (identity)
br_inner_n(Grid, N, Inner):
    Stripped = br_strip_border(Grid)
    Inner = br_inner_n(Stripped, N - 1)

br_outer_color(Grid, V): br_ring_color(Grid, 0, V)
br_is_uniform_outer(Grid): br_outer_color(Grid, _)

br_ring_colors_(_, N, MaxN, []): N > MaxN   (base case: past max ring)
br_ring_colors_(Grid, N, MaxN, [C|Rest]):
    C = br_ring_color(Grid, N)   (ring N is uniform)
    Rest = br_ring_colors_(Grid, N+1, MaxN)
br_ring_colors_(_, _, _, [])   (ring N is non-uniform: stop)

br_ring_colors(Grid, Colors):
    MaxN = br_max_ring(Grid)
    Colors = br_ring_colors_(Grid, 0, MaxN)

br_max_ring(Grid, N):
    (H, W) = dims(Grid); N = (min(H, W) - 1) // 2

br_is_nested(Grid):
    MaxN = br_max_ring(Grid)
    forall N in 0..MaxN: br_is_uniform_ring(Grid, N)

br_depth_map(Grid, DepthGrid):
    (H, W) = dims(Grid); H1 = H - 1; W1 = W - 1
    DepthGrid = [[br_ring_depth_(H,W,R,C) | C in 0..W1] | R in 0..H1]

br_replace_cell_if_(H, W, N, V, R, C, _OldV, V):
    br_ring_depth_(H, W, R, C) == N
br_replace_cell_if_(_, _, _, _, _, _, OldV, OldV)

br_fill_ring(Grid, N, V, Out):
    (H, W) = dims(Grid); H1 = H - 1; W1 = W - 1
    Out = [[replace_if_at_ring_N(R, C) | C in 0..W1] | R in 0..H1]
    where replace_if_at_ring_N(R,C) = V if ring_depth(R,C)==N else Grid[R][C]

END OF PART 157


PART 158 — SPLICE PACK PSEUDOCODE (sp_* prefix, Layer 147)

sp_insert_row(Grid, R, NewRow, Out):
  Split Grid at position R into Prefix (first R rows) and Suffix (remaining rows)
    using length(Prefix, R) and append(Prefix, Suffix, Grid).
  Re-assemble as append(Prefix, [NewRow|Suffix], Out).

sp_delete_row(Grid, R, Out):
  Split Grid at position R using length(Prefix, R) and
    append(Prefix, [_|Suffix], Grid) to discard row R.
  Re-assemble as append(Prefix, Suffix, Out).

sp_insert_col_row_(C, V, Row, NewRow) [private]:
  Split Row at column C into Prefix and Suffix.
  Re-assemble as append(Prefix, [V|Suffix], NewRow).

sp_insert_col(Grid, C, V, Out):
  Apply sp_insert_col_row_(C, V) to each row of Grid via maplist.

sp_delete_col_row_(C, Row, NewRow) [private]:
  Split Row at column C; discard the cell at C with [_|Suffix].
  Re-assemble as append(Prefix, Suffix, NewRow).

sp_delete_col(Grid, C, Out):
  Apply sp_delete_col_row_(C) to each row of Grid via maplist.

sp_swap_rows(Grid, R1, R2, Out):
  Fetch Row1 = nth0(R1, Grid) and Row2 = nth0(R2, Grid).
  Compute H1 = H - 1.
  Enumerate each index I from 0 to H1 via between.
  When I = R1 output Row2; when I = R2 output Row1; otherwise output the original row.
  Collect all outputs via findall.

sp_swap_in_row_(C1, C2, Row, NewRow) [private]:
  Fetch V1 = nth0(C1, Row) and V2 = nth0(C2, Row).
  Compute W1 = W - 1.
  Enumerate each column index C from 0 to W1 via between.
  When C = C1 output V2; when C = C2 output V1; otherwise output the original value.
  Collect all outputs via findall.

sp_swap_cols(Grid, C1, C2, Out):
  Apply sp_swap_in_row_(C1, C2) to each row of Grid via maplist.

sp_reverse_rows(Grid, Out):
  Out = reverse(Grid).

sp_reverse_cols(Grid, Out):
  Apply reverse to each row of Grid via maplist(reverse, Grid, Out).

sp_rotate_rows(Grid, K, Out):
  Compute K1 = K mod H.
  Split Grid at K1 into Prefix and Suffix using length and append.
  Out = append(Suffix, Prefix).

sp_rotate_row_cols_(K, Row, RotRow) [private]:
  Compute K1 = K mod W.
  Split Row at K1 into Prefix and Suffix.
  RotRow = append(Suffix, Prefix).

sp_rotate_cols(Grid, K, Out):
  Apply sp_rotate_row_cols_(K) to each row of Grid via maplist.

sp_replicate_row(Grid, R, N, Out):
  Fetch Row = nth0(R, Grid).
  Split Grid at R into Prefix and [Row|Suffix].
  Build Copies = list of N elements each equal to Row via length and maplist(=(Row)).
  Out = append([Prefix, Copies, Suffix]).

sp_replicate_col_in_row_(C, N, Row, NewRow) [private]:
  Split Row at C into Prefix and [V|Suffix].
  Build Copies = list of N elements each equal to V via length and maplist(=(V)).
  NewRow = append([Prefix, Copies, Suffix]).

sp_replicate_col(Grid, C, N, Out):
  Apply sp_replicate_col_in_row_(C, N) to each row of Grid via maplist.

sp_select_rows(Grid, Indices, Out):
  Out = findall(Row, member(I, Indices) and nth0(I, Grid, Row)).

sp_select_col_from_row_(Indices, Row, NewRow) [private]:
  NewRow = findall(V, member(C, Indices) and nth0(C, Row, V)).

sp_select_cols(Grid, Indices, Out):
  Apply sp_select_col_from_row_(Indices) to each row of Grid via maplist.

END OF PART 158


PART 159 — OBJOP PACK PSEUDOCODE (oo_* prefix, Layer 148)

oo_dims_(Grid, H, W) [private]:
  H = length(Grid).
  W = length(first row) if H > 0, else 0.

oo_cells_of(Grid, V, Cells):
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1.
  Unsorted = findall(R-C, between(0,H1,R) and between(0,W1,C)
                           and nth0(R,Grid,Row) and nth0(C,Row,V)).
  Cells = sort(Unsorted).

oo_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, R1, C1):
  Rs = findall(R, member(R-_, Cells)).
  Cs = findall(C, member(_-C, Cells)).
  R0 = min_list(Rs), R1 = max_list(Rs).
  C0 = min_list(Cs), C1 = max_list(Cs).

oo_count(Grid, V, N):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  N = length(Cells).

oo_size(Grid, V, H, W):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  oo_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, R1, C1).
  H = R1-R0+1, W = C1-C0+1.

oo_center(Grid, V, R, C):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  oo_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, R1, C1).
  R = (R0+R1) // 2, C = (C0+C1) // 2.

oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, Val, Out) [private]:
  For each row R (via between): for each col C (via between):
    if memberchk(R-C, Cells) then NewV = Val else NewV = original.
  Collect all NewRows; Out = collected grid.

oo_erase(Grid, V, Bg, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, Bg).

oo_repaint(Grid, V, NewV, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, NewV).

oo_swap(Grid, V1, V2, Out):
  Cells1 = oo_cells_of(Grid, V1).
  Cells2 = oo_cells_of(Grid, V2).
  Grid1 = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells1, V2).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid1, Cells2, V1).

oo_move(Grid, V, DR, DC, Bg, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  Grid1 = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, Bg).
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1.
  NewCells = findall(NewR-NewC, member(R-C, Cells) and
                     NewR is R+DR and NewC is C+DC and
                     between(0,H1,NewR) and between(0,W1,NewC)).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid1, NewCells, V).

oo_copy(Grid, V, DR, DC, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  H1 = H-1, W1 = W-1.
  NewCells = findall(NewR-NewC, member(R-C, Cells) and
                     NewR is R+DR and NewC is C+DC and
                     between(0,H1,NewR) and between(0,W1,NewC)).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid, NewCells, V).

oo_rotate90_cells_(Cells, R0, C0, H1, NewCells) [private]:
  For each R-C in Cells: Nr = R-R0, Nc = C-C0.
  NewR = R0+Nc, NewC = C0+H1-Nr.

oo_rotate90(Grid, V, Bg, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  oo_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, R1, _).
  H = R1-R0+1, H1 = H-1.
  NewCells = oo_rotate90_cells_(Cells, R0, C0, H1).
  Grid1 = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, Bg).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid1, NewCells, V).

oo_rotate180_cells_(Cells, R0, C0, H1, W1, NewCells) [private]:
  For each R-C in Cells: Nr = R-R0, Nc = C-C0.
  NewR = R0+H1-Nr, NewC = C0+W1-Nc.

oo_rotate180(Grid, V, Bg, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  oo_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, R1, C1).
  H1 = R1-R0, W1 = C1-C0.
  NewCells = oo_rotate180_cells_(Cells, R0, C0, H1, W1).
  Grid1 = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, Bg).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid1, NewCells, V).

oo_mirror_h_cells_(Cells, _R0, C0, W1, NewCells) [private]:
  For each R-C in Cells: Nc = C-C0.
  NewR = R (unchanged), NewC = C0+W1-Nc.

oo_mirror_h(Grid, V, Bg, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  oo_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, _R1, C1).
  W1 = C1-C0.
  NewCells = oo_mirror_h_cells_(Cells, R0, C0, W1).
  Grid1 = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, Bg).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid1, NewCells, V).
