    obj(Color, [r(R+DR, C+DC) | r(R,C) in Cells])

PROCEDURE sx_to_origin(Scene, Scene2)
  IF Scene == [] THEN Scene2 = []
  ELSE
    MinR = min([R | obj(_, Cells) in Scene, r(R,_) in Cells])
    MinC = min([C | obj(_, Cells) in Scene, r(_,C) in Cells])
    Scene2 = sx_shift(Scene, -MinR, -MinC)

PROCEDURE sx_reflect_h(Scene, Width, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [reflect_h_obj(Width, O) | O in Scene]
  WHERE reflect_h_obj(W, obj(Color, Cells)) =
    obj(Color, [r(R, W-1-C) | r(R,C) in Cells])

PROCEDURE sx_reflect_v(Scene, Height, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [reflect_v_obj(Height, O) | O in Scene]
  WHERE reflect_v_obj(H, obj(Color, Cells)) =
    obj(Color, [r(H-1-R, C) | r(R,C) in Cells])

PROCEDURE sx_remove_color(Scene, Color, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [O | O in Scene, color(O) != Color]

PROCEDURE sx_keep_color(Scene, Color, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [O | O in Scene, color(O) == Color]

PROCEDURE sx_sort_size_desc(Scene, Sorted)
  Keyed = [(-size(O), O) | O in Scene]
  Sorted = [O | (_, O) in msort(Keyed)]

PROCEDURE sx_sort_size_asc(Scene, Sorted)
  Keyed = [(size(O), O) | O in Scene]
  Sorted = [O | (_, O) in msort(Keyed)]

PROCEDURE sx_sort_pos(Scene, Sorted)
  Keyed = [(topleft(O), O) | O in Scene]
  Sorted = [O | (_, O) in msort(Keyed)]
  WHERE topleft(obj(_, Cells)) = r(min_row(Cells), min_col(Cells))

PROCEDURE sx_top_n(Scene, N, TopN)
  Sorted = sx_sort_size_desc(Scene)
  IF length(Sorted) >= N THEN TopN = first_n(N, Sorted)
  ELSE TopN = Sorted

PROCEDURE sx_dedup_form(Scene, Deduped)
  dedup_acc(Scene, [], Deduped)

PROCEDURE dedup_acc([], _, [])
PROCEDURE dedup_acc([H|T], Seen, [H|Rest])
  IF norm(H) not_in Seen
    dedup_acc(T, [norm(H)|Seen], Rest)
PROCEDURE dedup_acc([_|T], Seen, Rest)
  dedup_acc(T, Seen, Rest)
WHERE norm(Obj) = translate_to_origin_and_sort_cells(Obj)

Part 196: ruleinfer Pack — Scene-Level Transformation Rule Inference (ri_*, Layer 185)

PROCEDURE ri_infer_recolor(Before, After, Old, New)
  CB = distinct_colors(Before)
  CA = distinct_colors(After)
  [Old] = subtract(CB, CA)
  [New] = subtract(CA, CB)
  ASSERT count(Before, Old) == count(After, New)

PROCEDURE ri_infer_recolor_all(Before, After, New)
  ASSERT Before != [], After != []
  [New] = distinct_colors(After)

PROCEDURE ri_infer_color_map(Before, After, Map)
  ASSERT length(Before) == length(After)
  Map = [(CB-CA) | (B,A) in zip(Before,After), color(B)=CB, color(A)=CA, CB != CA]
  (deduplicated; existing pairs not re-added)

PROCEDURE ri_infer_keep_color(Before, After, Color)
  ASSERT After != []
  [Color] = distinct_colors(After)
  NA = count(Before, Color)
  ASSERT NA < length(Before)
  ASSERT count(After, Color) == NA

PROCEDURE ri_infer_remove_color(Before, After, Color)
  CB = distinct_colors(Before)
  CA = distinct_colors(After)
  [Color] = subtract(CB, CA)

PROCEDURE ri_infer_shift(Before, After, DR, DC)
  FirstB = head(Before)
  r(R1,C1) = topleft(FirstB)
  Color = color(FirstB), Norm = norm(FirstB)
  FirstA = member A of After WHERE color(A)==Color AND norm(A)==Norm
  r(R2,C2) = topleft(FirstA)
  DR = R2 - R1, DC = C2 - C1
  ASSERT msort(shift(Before, DR, DC)) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ri_infer_to_origin(Before, After)
  ASSERT Before != []
  r(MinR, MinC) = scene_bbox(Before)
  ASSERT msort(shift(Before, -MinR, -MinC)) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ri_consistent_recolor(Old, New, Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
    ASSERT msort(apply_recolor(Old, New, Before)) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ri_consistent_color_map(Map, Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
    ASSERT msort(apply_color_map(Map, Before)) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ri_consistent_keep_color(Color, Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
    ASSERT msort([O | O in Before, color(O)==Color]) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ri_consistent_remove_color(Color, Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
    ASSERT msort([O | O in Before, color(O)!=Color]) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ri_consistent_shift(DR, DC, Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
    ASSERT msort(shift(Before, DR, DC)) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ri_all_same_n_objs(Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
    ASSERT length(Before) == length(After)

PROCEDURE ri_all_same_colors(Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
    ASSERT distinct_colors(Before) == distinct_colors(After)

Part 197: sceneapply Pack — Scene-Level Rule Term Evaluation Engine (sa_*, Layer 186)

RULE TERMS: recolor(Old,New) | recolor_all(New) | color_map(Map)
            | shift(DR,DC) | to_origin | reflect_h(Width) | reflect_v(Height)
            | remove_color(Color) | keep_color(Color)
            | sort_size_desc | sort_size_asc | sort_pos | top_n(N) | dedup_form

PROCEDURE sa_apply(Rule, Scene, Scene2)
  DISPATCH on Rule:
    recolor(Old, New)    -> maplist(recolor_if_match(Old, New), Scene, Scene2)
    recolor_all(New)     -> maplist(set_color(New), Scene, Scene2)
    color_map(Map)       -> maplist(apply_map(Map), Scene, Scene2)
    shift(DR, DC)        -> maplist(shift_obj(DR, DC), Scene, Scene2)
    to_origin            -> IF Scene=[] THEN Scene2=[] ELSE
                            (MinR,MinC)=scene_bbox(Scene); shift(-MinR,-MinC)
    reflect_h(Width)     -> maplist(reflect_h_obj(Width), Scene, Scene2)
    reflect_v(Height)    -> maplist(reflect_v_obj(Height), Scene, Scene2)
    remove_color(Color)  -> include(color != Color, Scene, Scene2)
    keep_color(Color)    -> include(color == Color, Scene, Scene2)
    sort_size_desc       -> msort by -size
    sort_size_asc        -> msort by size
    sort_pos             -> msort by topleft r(R,C)
    top_n(N)             -> sort_size_desc, take first N (or all if N>length)
    dedup_form           -> accumulator keeping first of each norm

PROCEDURE sa_apply_seq([], Scene, Scene)
PROCEDURE sa_apply_seq([Rule|Rules], Scene, Scene2)
  Mid = sa_apply(Rule, Scene)
  Scene2 = sa_apply_seq(Rules, Mid)

PROCEDURE sa_verify(Rule, Before, After)
  Result = sa_apply(Rule, Before)
  ASSERT msort(Result) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE sa_verify_seq(Rules, Before, After)
  Result = sa_apply_seq(Rules, Before)
  ASSERT msort(Result) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE sa_verify_all(Rule, Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs: ASSERT sa_verify(Rule, Before, After)

PROCEDURE sa_verify_seq_all(Rules, Pairs)
  FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs: ASSERT sa_verify_seq(Rules, Before, After)

PROCEDURE sa_rule_type(Rule, Type)
  recolor/recolor_all/color_map -> color
  shift/to_origin/reflect_h/reflect_v -> spatial
  remove_color/keep_color/top_n -> filter
  sort_size_desc/sort_size_asc/sort_pos -> order
  dedup_form -> dedup

PROCEDURE sa_colors_affected(Rule, Colors)
  recolor(Old,New) -> [Old,New]
  recolor_all(New) -> [New]
  color_map(Map) -> sort(all Old and New atoms in Map)
  remove_color/keep_color -> [Color]
  spatial/order/dedup rules -> []

PROCEDURE sa_compose(Rule1, Rule2, Seq)
  Seq = [Rule1, Rule2]

PROCEDURE sa_rule_invertible(Rule)
  SUCCEED IF Rule in {recolor(_,_), shift(_,_), reflect_h(_), reflect_v(_)}

PSEUDOCODE: condxf Pack (xc_*, Layer 187, WP 208)

INPUT TYPES
  Scene := list of obj(Color, Cells)
  Color, C1, C2, NewColor, MatchColor := atom
  N := integer (cell count threshold)
  DR, DC := integer (row/column delta)
  Cmp := one of: gt | lt | eq | ge | le

PROCEDURE xc_split_color(Scene, Color, Match, NoMatch)
  Match   = [O | O in Scene, xc_color_(O) == Color]
  NoMatch = [O | O in Scene, xc_color_(O) \== Color]

PROCEDURE xc_merge(Group1, Group2, Scene2)
  Scene2 = append(Group1, Group2)

PROCEDURE xc_recolor_matching(Scene, MatchColor, NewColor, Scene2)
  Scene2 = maplist(xc_recolor_if_match_(MatchColor, NewColor), Scene)
  WHERE xc_recolor_if_match_(M, N, obj(M, Cells)) = obj(N, Cells)
        xc_recolor_if_match_(M, _, obj(C, Cells)) = obj(C, Cells)   [C \== M]

PROCEDURE xc_shift_color(Scene, Color, DR, DC, Scene2)
  Scene2 = maplist(xc_shift_if_color_(Color, DR, DC), Scene)
  WHERE xc_shift_if_color_(C, DR, DC, obj(C, Cells)) =
          obj(C, [r(R+DR, CF+DC) | r(R,CF) in Cells])
        xc_shift_if_color_(C, _, _, obj(C2, Cells)) = obj(C2, Cells)  [C2 \== C]

PROCEDURE xc_swap_colors(Scene, C1, C2, Scene2)
  Scene2 = maplist(xc_swap_one_(C1, C2), Scene)
  WHERE xc_swap_one_(C1, C2, obj(C, Cells)):
    IF C == C1 THEN obj(C2, Cells)
    ELSE IF C == C2 THEN obj(C1, Cells)
    ELSE obj(C, Cells)

PROCEDURE xc_recolor_by_size(Scene, N, Cmp, NewColor, Scene2)
  Scene2 = maplist(xc_recolor_if_size_(N, Cmp, NewColor), Scene)
  WHERE xc_recolor_if_size_(N, Cmp, New, obj(_, Cells)):
    S = length(Cells)
    IF xc_size_cmp_(Cmp, S, N) THEN obj(New, Cells)
    ELSE obj(_, Cells) [unchanged]

PROCEDURE xc_move_color(Scene, Color, DR, DC, Scene2)
  = xc_shift_color(Scene, Color, DR, DC, Scene2)

PROCEDURE xc_largest(Scene, Obj)
  Keyed = [(-N)-O | O in Scene, N = length(cells(O))]
  msort(Keyed, [_-Obj | _])

PROCEDURE xc_smallest(Scene, Obj)
  Keyed = [N-O | O in Scene, N = length(cells(O))]
  msort(Keyed, [_-Obj | _])

PROCEDURE xc_recolor_largest(Scene, NewColor, Scene2)
  Largest = xc_largest(Scene)
  Scene2 = maplist(xc_recolor_if_obj_(Largest, NewColor), Scene)
  WHERE xc_recolor_if_obj_(T, N, obj(_,Cells)) = obj(N,Cells)  [Obj==T]
        xc_recolor_if_obj_(_, _, Obj) = Obj                    [otherwise]

PROCEDURE xc_recolor_smallest(Scene, NewColor, Scene2)
  Smallest = xc_smallest(Scene)
  Scene2 = maplist(xc_recolor_if_obj_(Smallest, NewColor), Scene)

PROCEDURE xc_unique_size(Scene, Obj)
  FOR EACH Obj IN Scene:
    S = length(cells(Obj))
    SameSize = [O2 | O2 in Scene, length(cells(O2)) == S]
    IF length(SameSize) == 1 THEN YIELD Obj

PROCEDURE xc_recolor_unique_size(Scene, NewColor, Scene2)
  Unique = xc_unique_size(Scene)
  Scene2 = maplist(xc_recolor_if_obj_(Unique, NewColor), Scene)

PROCEDURE xc_split_size(Scene, N, Cmp, Match, NoMatch)
  Match   = [O | O in Scene, xc_size_cmp_(Cmp, length(cells(O)), N)]
  NoMatch = [O | O in Scene, NOT xc_size_cmp_(Cmp, length(cells(O)), N)]

HELPER xc_size_cmp_(gt, S, N): S > N
HELPER xc_size_cmp_(lt, S, N): S < N
HELPER xc_size_cmp_(eq, S, N): S =:= N
HELPER xc_size_cmp_(ge, S, N): S >= N
HELPER xc_size_cmp_(le, S, N): S =< N

PSEUDOCODE: scenepair Pack (ps_*, Layer 188, WP 209)

INPUT TYPES
  Before, After := list of obj(Color, Cells)
  Color          := atom
  N              := integer

PROCEDURE ps_same_n_objs(Before, After)
  ASSERT length(Before) == length(After)

PROCEDURE ps_added_objs(Before, After, Added)
  Added = [O | O in After, NOT ps_match_(O, Before)]
  WHERE ps_match_(O, List): exists C in List such that
    color(O)==color(C) AND norm(O)==norm(C)
    norm: translate min-row/col to 0, msort cells

PROCEDURE ps_removed_objs(Before, After, Removed)
  Removed = [O | O in Before, NOT ps_match_(O, After)]

PROCEDURE ps_n_added(Before, After, N)
  N = length(ps_added_objs(Before, After))

PROCEDURE ps_n_removed(Before, After, N)
  N = length(ps_removed_objs(Before, After))

PROCEDURE ps_color_set_before(Before, Colors)
  Colors = sorted_dedup([color(O) | O in Before])

PROCEDURE ps_color_set_after(After, Colors)
  Colors = sorted_dedup([color(O) | O in After])

PROCEDURE ps_same_color_set(Before, After)
  CB = ps_color_set_before(Before)
  CA = ps_color_set_after(After)
  ASSERT CB == CA

PROCEDURE ps_color_delta(Before, After, Delta)
  IF length(Before) != length(After) THEN Delta = []
  ELSE Delta = ps_color_delta_acc_(Before, After)
  WHERE ps_color_delta_acc_:
    FOR EACH (B, A) positional pair:
      IF color(B) != color(A): add color(B)-color(A) to Delta if not already present

PROCEDURE ps_is_recolor(Before, After)
  ASSERT ps_same_n_objs(Before, After)
  CB = sorted_distinct_colors(Before)
  CA = sorted_distinct_colors(After)
  ASSERT subtract(CB, CA) == [_OldColor]
  ASSERT subtract(CA, CB) == [_NewColor]

PROCEDURE ps_is_recolor_all(Before, After)
  ASSERT Before != []
  ASSERT After != []
  ASSERT sorted_distinct_colors(After) == [_SingleColor]

PROCEDURE ps_is_shift(Before, After, DR, DC)
  ASSERT ps_same_n_objs(Before, After)
  (R1,C1) = topleft(first(Before))
  Find FirstA in After with same color and norm as first(Before)
  (R2,C2) = topleft(FirstA)
  DR = R2-R1, DC = C2-C1
  Shifted = [shift(DR,DC,O) | O in Before]
  ASSERT msort(Shifted) == msort(After)
  CUT

PROCEDURE ps_is_to_origin(Before, After)
  ASSERT Before != []
  (MinR,_,MinC,_) = scene_bbox(Before)
  DR = -MinR, DC = -MinC
  Shifted = [shift(DR,DC,O) | O in Before]
  ASSERT msort(Shifted) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE ps_size_preserved(Before, After)
  ASSERT ps_same_n_objs(Before, After)
  FOR EACH positional pair (B,A): ASSERT size(B) == size(A)

PSEUDOCODE: scenerank Pack (rk_*, Layer 189, WP 210)

INPUT TYPES
  Pairs   := list of Before-After terms, where Before and After are obj(Color,Cells) lists
  Rules   := list of rule terms (same vocabulary as sceneapply)
  Rule    := rule term
  N, MinN := integer

PROCEDURE rk_pair_ok_(Rule, Before-After)  [private]
  Result = rk_apply_(Rule, Before)
  ASSERT msort(Result) == msort(After)

PROCEDURE rk_apply_(Rule, Scene, Scene2)  [private]
  DISPATCH on Rule (same vocabulary as sceneapply):
    recolor(Old, New)    -> maplist(recolor_atom_(Old,New), Scene, Scene2)
    recolor_all(New)     -> maplist(set_color_(New), Scene, Scene2)
    color_map(Map)       -> maplist(apply_map_(Map), Scene, Scene2)
    shift(DR, DC)        -> maplist(shift_obj_(DR,DC), Scene, Scene2)
    to_origin            -> Scene=[] -> Scene2=[]; else bbox MinR/MinC; shift(-MinR,-MinC)
    reflect_h(Width)     -> maplist(reflect_h_(Width), Scene, Scene2)
    reflect_v(Height)    -> maplist(reflect_v_(Height), Scene, Scene2)
    remove_color(Color)  -> findall(O, O in Scene AND color(O) \== Color, Scene2)
    keep_color(Color)    -> findall(O, O in Scene AND color(O) == Color, Scene2)
    sort_size_desc       -> keyed msort by -N; extract values
    sort_size_asc        -> keyed msort by N; extract values
    top_n(N)             -> sort_size_desc; take Prefix of length N (or all)

PROCEDURE rk_n_pairs(Pairs, N)
  N = length(Pairs)

PROCEDURE rk_coverage_pairs(Rule, Pairs, Covered)
  Covered = include(rk_pair_ok_(Rule), Pairs)

PROCEDURE rk_coverage(Rule, Pairs, N)
  Covered = rk_coverage_pairs(Rule, Pairs)
  N = length(Covered)

PROCEDURE rk_consistent(Rule, Pairs)
  maplist(rk_pair_ok_(Rule), Pairs)

PROCEDURE rk_inconsistent_pairs(Rule, Pairs, Bad)
  Bad = [P | P in Pairs, NOT rk_pair_ok_(Rule, P)]

PROCEDURE rk_rule_score(Rule, Pairs, N)
  = rk_coverage(Rule, Pairs, N)

PROCEDURE rk_rank_rules(Rules, Pairs, Ranked)
  Keyed = [(-N)-Rule | Rule in Rules, N = rk_coverage(Rule, Pairs)]
  msort(Keyed, Sorted)
  Ranked = values(Sorted)

PROCEDURE rk_rank_candidates(Rules, Pairs, CovRulePairs)
  Keyed = [(-N)-N-Rule | Rule in Rules, N = rk_coverage(Rule, Pairs)]
  msort(Keyed, Sorted)
  CovRulePairs = [N-Rule | _-N-Rule in Sorted]

PROCEDURE rk_best_rule(Rules, Pairs, Best)
  rk_rank_rules(Rules, Pairs, [Best | _])

PROCEDURE rk_all_consistent(Rules, Pairs, Consistent)
  Consistent = include(rk_consistent_check_(Pairs), Rules)

PROCEDURE rk_filter_min_coverage(Rules, Pairs, MinN, Filtered)
  Filtered = include(rk_coverage_ge_(Pairs, MinN), Rules)

PROCEDURE rk_perfect_rules(Rules, Pairs, Perfect)
  Total = rk_n_pairs(Pairs)
  Perfect = rk_filter_min_coverage(Rules, Pairs, Total)

PROCEDURE rk_coverage_ratio(Rule, Pairs, Num/Den)
  Den = rk_n_pairs(Pairs)
  Num = rk_coverage(Rule, Pairs)

PROCEDURE rk_top_n_rules(Rules, Pairs, N, TopN)
  All = rk_rank_candidates(Rules, Pairs)
  TopN = first N elements of All (or all if fewer than N)

Part 201: Color Substitution Table Learning and Application (colortable Pack, WP 211)

Motivation: many ARC-AGI-2 tasks apply a consistent color permutation across
all objects. To solve them, the solver must learn what color maps to what by
examining training pairs, then apply the learned table to a new input.

ct_infer_from_pair(Before, After, Map):
    collect_pairs(Before, After, Pairs)  % positional: n-th B object vs n-th A
    list_to_set(Pairs, Map)
    consistent_map(Map)

collect_pairs([], [], []).
collect_pairs([obj(CB,_)|RestB], [obj(CA,_)|RestA], Pairs):
    collect_pairs(RestB, RestA, RestPairs)
    if CB == CA then Pairs = RestPairs
    else Pairs = [CB-CA | RestPairs]

ct_consistent_map(Map):
    not( member(From-To1, Map), member(From-To2, Map), To1 \== To2 )

ct_merge_maps(Map1, Map2, Merged):
    append(Map1, Map2, Combined)
    list_to_set(Combined, Merged)
    ct_consistent_map(Merged)

ct_learn_map(Pairs, Map, Inconsistent):
    accumulate over Pairs:
        infer PairMap from each pair
        if merge(Acc, PairMap) succeeds -> update Acc
        else -> add pair to Inconsistent

ct_apply_to_scene(Map, Scene, MappedScene):
    maplist(ct_apply_map(Map), Scene, MappedScene)

ct_complete_map(Map, Scene, Complete):
    find all colors in Scene not in Map keys
    add identity entries for those colors
    append to Map

ct_invert_map(Map, Inverted):
    swap each From-To to To-From
    verify consistency of Inverted

Part 202: End-to-End Scene Puzzle Solver (gridsolve Pack, WP 212)

Motivation: individual inference, ranking, and application packs each do one
step. gridsolve combines them into a single solve(Pairs, TestInput, Output)
predicate, hiding the pipeline internals.

gs_apply(Rule, Scene, Result):
    dispatch on Rule functor: recolor, recolor_all, color_map, shift,
    to_origin, reflect_h, reflect_v, remove_color, keep_color, sort_size_desc,
    sort_size_asc, top_n, identity
    (self-contained engine, no cross-pack dependency)

gs_coverage(Rule, Pairs, N):
    include(gs_pair_ok_(Rule), Pairs, Covered), length(Covered, N)

gs_consistent(Rule, Pairs):
    maplist(gs_pair_ok_(Rule), Pairs)

gs_rank_rules(Rules, Pairs, Ranked):
    findall(-N-Rule per Rule where N=coverage; msort; extract values

gs_infer_candidates(Pairs, Candidates):
    findall over gs_infer_one_ (backtracking over patterns)
    patterns: recolor(Old,New) from single-color set difference,
              recolor_all(New) if After has one color,
              color_map(Map) from positional color pairs,
              shift(DR,DC) from first-object topleft match,
              to_origin if scene bbox not at origin,
              remove_color from After colors

gs_default_candidates(Cands):
    static list covering recolor (r/b/g/y/p variants), recolor_all,
    shift (8 directions), to_origin, remove_color, sort, top_n, identity

gs_solve(Pairs, TestInput, Output):
    infer_candidates + default_candidates -> union
    best_rule from union
    apply best_rule to TestInput

gs_solve_n(Pairs, N, TopRules, BestRule):
    rank all candidates; take top N; BestRule = head of TopRules

gs_explain(Pairs, BestRule, Coverage):
    solve + coverage count for best rule

Part 203: Systematic Generation of Scene Transformation Rule Candidates (transformgen Pack, WP 213)

Motivation: rule inference heuristics (ruleinfer, gridsolve) catch the most
common patterns but may miss unusual rules. transformgen generates ALL rules
derivable from the scene data within a bounded search space, so a
filter-then-rank pipeline can find the right rule even without a direct
inference heuristic.

tg_scene_colors(Scene, Colors):
    findall C where member(obj(C,_), Scene); sort

tg_recolor_candidates(Scene, Cands):
    tg_scene_colors -> Colors
    findall recolor(Old,New) where Old\==New; both in Colors

tg_shift_candidates(MaxDR, MaxDC, Cands):
    findall shift(DR,DC) where DR in [-MaxDR..MaxDR], DC in [-MaxDC..MaxDC],
    not(DR=0, DC=0)

tg_color_map_candidate(Before, After, color_map(Map)):
    same length; nth1 positional pairs; collect CB-CA where CB\==CA;
    list_to_set; fails if empty

tg_from_scenes(Before, After, Candidates):
    union of: recolor(Before), recolor_all(After), remove(Before),
    keep(After), color_map(Before,After), shift(3,3), sorting, identity

tg_from_pairs(Pairs, Candidates):
    union of tg_from_scenes over all pairs + top_n variants

tg_filter_consistent(Rules, Pairs, Consistent):
    include(tg_rule_consistent_(Pairs)): maplist(tg_pair_ok_(Rule), Pairs)

tg_all_scene_candidates(Scene, MaxShift, Candidates):
    union of all generator predicates with given scene and MaxShift bound

Part 204: Multi-Color Scene Analysis (multicolor Pack, WP 214)

mc_color_counts(Scene, Counts):
    sort distinct colors; findall C-N per color; count matching objects

mc_dominant_color(Scene, Color):
    color_counts -> findall -N-C keyed; msort; head

mc_rarest_color(Scene, Color):
    color_counts -> findall N-C keyed; msort; head

mc_singleton_colors(Scene, Colors):
    color_counts -> findall C where count==1

mc_unique_color(Scene, Color):
    color_counts -> member C-1 (backtrackable)

mc_color_freq_rank(Scene, N, Color):
    color_counts -> findall -N-C keyed; msort; extract colors; nth1(N)

mc_color_partition(Scene, Groups):
    sort distinct colors; findall C-Objs per color

mc_pair_colors(Scene, Pairs):
    sort distinct colors; findall C1-C2 where C1 @< C2

mc_equal_count_pairs(Scene, Pairs):
    color_counts; findall C1-C2 where count(C1)==count(C2) and C1 @< C2

mc_majority_color(Scene, Color):
    length(Scene, Total); Half is Total/2;
    member Color-N where N > Half; cut


Part 205: sceneinv Pack Pseudocode (si_*, Layer 194)

FUNCTION si_n_before(Pair, N):
    Pair = Before-_
    N = length(Before)

FUNCTION si_n_after(Pair, N):
    Pair = _-After
    N = length(After)

FUNCTION si_all_n_before(Pairs, Ns):
    Ns = [si_n_before(P) for P in Pairs]

FUNCTION si_all_n_after(Pairs, Ns):
    Ns = [si_n_after(P) for P in Pairs]

FUNCTION si_const_n_before(Pairs, N):
    REQUIRE Pairs is not empty
    Ns = si_all_n_before(Pairs)
    SET = unique(Ns)
    REQUIRE SET = [N]

FUNCTION si_const_n_after(Pairs, N):
    REQUIRE Pairs is not empty
    Ns = si_all_n_after(Pairs)
    SET = unique(Ns)
    REQUIRE SET = [N]

FUNCTION si_n_preserved(Pairs):
    FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
        REQUIRE length(Before) == length(After)

FUNCTION si_colors_before(Pair, Colors):
    Pair = Before-_
    Colors = sorted(distinct(colors of Before))

FUNCTION si_colors_after(Pair, Colors):
    Pair = _-After
    Colors = sorted(distinct(colors of After))

FUNCTION si_const_colors_before(Pairs, Colors):
    REQUIRE Pairs is not empty
    AllColors = [si_colors_before(P) for P in Pairs]
    REQUIRE unique(AllColors) = [Colors]

FUNCTION si_const_colors_after(Pairs, Colors):
    REQUIRE Pairs is not empty
    AllColors = [si_colors_after(P) for P in Pairs]
    REQUIRE unique(AllColors) = [Colors]

FUNCTION si_colors_preserved(Pairs):
    FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
        REQUIRE sorted(distinct_colors(Before)) == sorted(distinct_colors(After))

FUNCTION si_total_cells_before(Pair, N):
    Pair = Before-_
    Lens = [length(Cells) for obj(_, Cells) in Before]
    N = sum(Lens)

FUNCTION si_cells_preserved(Pairs):
    FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs:
        N_B = sum of cell lengths in Before
        N_A = sum of cell lengths in After
        REQUIRE N_B == N_A


Part 206: seqinfer Pack Pseudocode (sq_*, Layer 195)

FUNCTION sq_apply(Rules, Scene, Result):
    IF Rules is empty: Result = Scene
    ELSE:
        Intermediate = sq_apply_one_(head(Rules), Scene)
        Result = sq_apply(tail(Rules), Intermediate)

FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(identity, Scene): return Scene
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(recolor(C1,C2), Scene): recolor all C1 objects to C2
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(recolor_all(C), Scene): recolor all objects to C
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(shift(DR,DC), Scene): translate all cells by (DR,DC)
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(to_origin, Scene): translate each object to start at (0,0)
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(reflect_h, Scene): reflect each object's cells within its bbox horizontally
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(reflect_v, Scene): reflect each object's cells within its bbox vertically
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(remove_color(C), Scene): filter out all objects of color C
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(keep_color(C), Scene): retain only objects of color C
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(sort_size_desc, Scene): sort objects by cell count descending
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(sort_size_asc, Scene): sort objects by cell count ascending
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(top_n(N), Scene): sort_size_desc, then take first N
FUNCTION sq_apply_one_(color_map(Map), Scene): apply first matching entry per object; identity if no match

FUNCTION sq_verify(Rules, Before, After):
    Result = sq_apply(Rules, Before)
    RETURN msort(Result) == msort(After)

FUNCTION sq_consistent(Rules, Pairs):
    FOR EACH Before-After IN Pairs: REQUIRE sq_verify(Rules, Before, After)

FUNCTION sq_coverage(Rules, Pairs, N):
    N = count of Pairs where sq_verify(Rules, Before, After) succeeds

FUNCTION sq_infer_2step(Candidates, Pairs, BestSeq):
    All = {(Cov, [R1,R2]) : R1 in Candidates, R2 in Candidates,
           Cov = sq_coverage([R1,R2], Pairs), Cov > 0}
    REQUIRE All is not empty
    BestSeq = sequence with maximum Cov in All

FUNCTION sq_infer_3step(Candidates, Pairs, BestSeq): same as 2step but for triples

FUNCTION sq_solve(Pairs, Candidates, BestSeq):
    IF 2-step sequence with full coverage exists: return it
    ELSE: return single-step rule with highest coverage


Part 207: gridquery Pack Pseudocode (gq_*, Layer 196)

FUNCTION gq_size(Grid, H, W):
    H = length(Grid)
    IF H > 0: W = length(Grid[0]) ELSE W = 0

FUNCTION gq_at(Grid, R, C, Color):
    Color = Grid[R][C]  (via nth0/3)

FUNCTION gq_row(Grid, R, Row):
    Row = Grid[R]  (via nth0/3)

FUNCTION gq_col(Grid, C, Col):
    Col = [Grid[R][C] for R in 0..H-1]

FUNCTION gq_colors(Grid, Colors):
    Colors = sorted(distinct(all cells in Grid))

FUNCTION gq_n_cells(Grid, Color, N):
    N = count of cells == Color across all rows

FUNCTION gq_most_freq_color(Grid, Color):
    counts = {C: gq_n_cells(Grid,C) for C in gq_colors(Grid)}
    Color = argmax(counts) with term-order tie-breaking

FUNCTION gq_region(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, SubGrid):
    FOR R in R0..R1: SubGrid[R-R0] = Grid[R][C0..C1]

FUNCTION gq_diff(Grid1, Grid2, Cells):
    Cells = {r(R,C) : Grid1[R][C] != Grid2[R][C]}

FUNCTION gq_n_diff(Grid1, Grid2, N):
    N = length(gq_diff(Grid1, Grid2))

FUNCTION gq_same_size(Grid1, Grid2):
    gq_size(Grid1) == gq_size(Grid2)

FUNCTION gq_transpose(Grid, Transposed):
    IF empty: Transposed = []
    ELSE: Transposed = [gq_col(Grid, C) for C in 0..W-1]

FUNCTION gq_replace(Grid, R, C, Color, NewGrid):
    NewGrid = Grid with Grid[R][C] = Color

FUNCTION gq_fill_region(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Color, NewGrid):
    NewGrid = Grid with all (R,C) in [R0..R1]x[C0..C1] set to Color


Part 208: gridparse Pack Pseudocode (gp_*, Layer 197)

FUNCTION gp_bg_color(Grid, BgColor):
    All = flatten(Grid)
    Colors = distinct(All)
    BgColor = argmax(count(All, C) for C in Colors), term-order tie-break

FUNCTION gp_grid_cells(Grid, Color, Cells):
    Cells = [(R,C) for R,C where Grid[R][C] == Color], row-major order

FUNCTION gp_color_components(Grid, Color, Components):
    Available = gp_grid_cells(Grid, Color)
    Components = []
    WHILE Available is not empty:
        Seed = head(Available)
        Comp, Remaining = BFS(Seed, Available)
        Components.append(Comp)
        Available = Remaining

FUNCTION BFS(Seed, Available):
    Queue = [Seed]; Visited = []
    WHILE Queue is not empty:
        Cell = dequeue(Queue)
        Neighbors = 4-adjacent(Cell) intersect Available
        Available = Available - Neighbors
        Queue.extend(Neighbors)
        Visited.append(Cell)
    RETURN Visited, Available

FUNCTION gp_grid_to_scene(Grid, BgColor, Scene):
    ObjColors = gp_object_colors(Grid, BgColor)
    Scene = [obj(C, Cells) for C in ObjColors
                             for Cells in gp_color_components(Grid, C)]

FUNCTION gp_scene_to_grid(Scene, H, W, BgColor, Grid):
    Blank = H x W grid filled with BgColor
    Grid = paint each obj in Scene onto Blank

FUNCTION gp_grid_from_rows(H, W, Color, Grid):
    Grid = [[Color]*W]*H

FUNCTION gp_paint_obj(Grid, obj(Color, Cells), NewGrid):
    FOR EACH r(R,C) IN Cells: Grid[R][C] = Color
    RETURN Grid


Part 209: gridtask Pack Pseudocode (gt_*, Layer 198)

WP-219-PSEUDO-001: gt_diff_cells(Before, After, Cells)
  Get H,W from Before dimensions.
  Findall r(R,C) over all 0-indexed positions where Before[R][C] != After[R][C].
  Bind to Cells.

WP-219-PSEUDO-002: gt_n_changed(Before, After, N)
  Call gt_diff_cells(Before, After, Cells).
  N = length(Cells).

WP-219-PSEUDO-003: gt_unchanged_cells(Before, After, Cells)
  Findall r(R,C) over all positions where Before[R][C] == After[R][C].

WP-219-PSEUDO-004: gt_bg_color(Grid, BgColor)
  Flatten Grid to list of all cell values.
  For each distinct color C, count occurrences.
  Key each as NegN-C where NegN = -count.
  msort keys. Head gives most frequent color = BgColor.

WP-219-PSEUDO-005: gt_infer_color_map(Before, After, Map)
  Findall BV-AV for every aligned cell pair (same R,C).
  list_to_set to deduplicate.
  Fail if any key K maps to two different values V1 != V2.

WP-219-PSEUDO-006: gt_apply_color_map(Map, Grid, NewGrid)
  maplist apply_row over Grid rows.
  Each row: maplist apply_cell where apply_cell looks up Map entry; keeps V if not found.

WP-219-PSEUDO-007: gt_color_map_pairs(Pairs, Map)
  Findall BV-AV across all cells of all pairs in one pass.
  list_to_set. Consistency check.

WP-219-PSEUDO-008: gt_is_color_sub(Pairs)
  gt_color_map_pairs(Pairs, Map) must succeed.
  maplist gt_test_color_map over all pairs must succeed.

WP-219-PSEUDO-009: gt_is_scale(Before, After, N)
  Get BH,BW from Before; AH,AW from After.
  Require BH>0, BW>0, AH mod BH = 0, AW mod BW = 0.
  N = AH // BH. Require N = AW // BW and N > 1.
  forall R in 0..BH-1, C in 0..BW-1:
    V = Before[R][C].
    forall DR in 0..N-1, DC in 0..N-1: After[R*N+DR][C*N+DC] == V.

WP-219-PSEUDO-010: gt_infer_shift(Before, After, Bg, dr(DR,DC))
  Collect non-Bg cells in Before; take first cell r(R1,C1,V1).
  Collect positions in After with color V1.
  For each candidate r(R2,C2): DR=R2-R1, DC=C2-C1.
  Apply shift to Before with Bg fill; compare to After.
  Succeed on first match.

WP-219-PSEUDO-011: gt_pair_score(Rule, Before, After, Score)
  Apply Rule to Before to get Predicted.
  Count changed cells between Predicted and After = Wrong.
  Score = (H*W - Wrong) / (H*W); 1.0 if H*W = 0.

WP-219-PSEUDO-012: gt_solve(Pairs, TestBefore, TestAfter, Rule)
  Try identity: if all pairs satisfy Before==After, Rule=identity, TestAfter=TestBefore.
  Try color_map: if gt_color_map_pairs and all pairs verify, apply map to TestBefore.
  Try scale: if first pair satisfies gt_is_scale(N) and all pairs verify, scale TestBefore.
  Try shift: detect Bg from first Before grid; infer shift from first pair; verify all pairs.
  Fallback: Rule=identity, TestAfter=TestBefore.


Part 210: gridnbr Pack Pseudocode (Layer 199)

gn_nbr4(Grid, R, C, Vals):
  dims(Grid, H, W)
  Vals = [V | for each delta in {(-1,0),(1,0),(0,-1),(0,1)}:
              R2=R+DR, C2=C+DC
              if 0<=R2<H and 0<=C2<W: V = Grid[R2][C2]]

gn_nbr8(Grid, R, C, Vals):
  Like gn_nbr4 but deltas = all 8 directions including diagonals.

gn_count4(Grid, R, C, Color, N):
  gn_nbr4(Grid, R, C, Vals)
  N = count(Color in Vals)

gn_count8(Grid, R, C, Color, N):
  gn_nbr8(Grid, R, C, Vals)
  N = count(Color in Vals)

gn_count4_grid(Grid, Color, CountGrid):
  dims(Grid, H, W)
  CountGrid[R][C] = gn_count4(Grid, R, C, Color, N) for each (R,C)

gn_count8_grid(Grid, Color, CountGrid):
  dims(Grid, H, W)
  CountGrid[R][C] = gn_count8(Grid, R, C, Color, N) for each (R,C)

gn_any4(Grid, R, C, Color):
  gn_nbr4(Grid, R, C, Vals)
  memberchk(Color, Vals)   // deterministic, no choicepoint

gn_all4(Grid, R, C, Color):
  gn_nbr4(Grid, R, C, Vals)
  Vals not empty
  no V in Vals where V != Color

gn_mark_border(Grid, Bg, MarkedGrid):
  for each (R,C):
    V = Grid[R][C]
    if V != Bg and gn_any4(Grid, R, C, Bg):
      MarkedGrid[R][C] = border
    else:
      MarkedGrid[R][C] = V

gn_mark_isolated(Grid, Bg, MarkedGrid):
  for each (R,C):
    V = Grid[R][C]
    if V != Bg and not gn_any4(Grid, R, C, V):
      MarkedGrid[R][C] = isolated
    else:
      MarkedGrid[R][C] = V

gn_expand_color(Grid, Color, Expanded):
  Bg = most_frequent_color(Grid)   // keyed-msort on negative counts
  for each (R,C):
    V = Grid[R][C]
    if V = Bg and gn_any4(Grid, R, C, Color):
      Expanded[R][C] = Color
    else:
      Expanded[R][C] = V

gn_shrink_color(Grid, Color, Shrunk):
  Bg = most_frequent_color(Grid)
  for each (R,C):
    V = Grid[R][C]
    if V = Color and exists neighbor N of (R,C) where N != Color:
      Shrunk[R][C] = Bg
    else:
      Shrunk[R][C] = V

gn_majority_nbr4(Grid, R, C, Maj):
  gn_nbr4(Grid, R, C, Vals)
  Vals not empty
  Maj = most_frequent(Vals)   // keyed-msort on negative counts

gn_conway_step(Grid, Color, N, NewGrid):
  Bg = most_frequent_color(Grid)
  for each (R,C):
    V = Grid[R][C]
    if V = Color and gn_count4(Grid, R, C, Color, CN) and CN = N:
      NewGrid[R][C] = Bg
    else:
      NewGrid[R][C] = V


PART 211 - WORK PACKAGE 221 PSEUDOCODE: griddist (Layer 200, gd_*)

gd_manhattan(R1, C1, R2, C2, D):
  D = abs(R1 - R2) + abs(C1 - C2)

gd_chebyshev(R1, C1, R2, C2, D):
  D = max(abs(R1 - R2), abs(C1 - C2))

gd_dist_map(Grid, Color, DistGrid):
  Seeds = {(SR,SC) | Grid[SR][SC] == Color}
  for each (R,C):
    DistGrid[R][C] = min over all (SR,SC) in Seeds of (abs(R-SR) + abs(C-SC))
                     or 9999 if Seeds is empty

gd_dist_map8(Grid, Color, DistGrid):
  Seeds = {(SR,SC) | Grid[SR][SC] == Color}
  for each (R,C):
    DistGrid[R][C] = min over Seeds of max(abs(R-SR), abs(C-SC))
                     or 9999 if empty

gd_nearest_coord(Grid, R, C, Color, [R2,C2]):
  Candidates = {(D,NR,NC) | Grid[NR][NC]==Color, D = abs(R-NR)+abs(C-NC)}
  fail if Candidates empty
  [R2,C2] = (NR,NC) with minimum D, tie-broken by standard term order

gd_zone(Grid, Color, N, ZoneGrid):
  DMap = gd_dist_map(Grid, Color)
  for each (R,C):
    if Grid[R][C] == Color: ZoneGrid[R][C] = Color
    else if DMap[R][C] <= N: ZoneGrid[R][C] = zone
    else: ZoneGrid[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

gd_ring(Grid, R0, C0, D, Coords):
  Coords = {[R,C] | in-bounds(R,C), abs(R-R0)+abs(C-C0) == D}

gd_voronoi(Grid, VGrid):
  Bg = most_frequent_color(Grid)
  FgCells = {(FR,FC,V) | Grid[FR][FC] != Bg}
  for each (R,C):
    if Grid[R][C] == Bg and FgCells non-empty:
      VGrid[R][C] = color of nearest (FR,FC,V) in FgCells by Manhattan distance
    else:
      VGrid[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

gd_bfs_flood(Grid, R0, C0, Wall, DistGrid):
  fail if Grid[R0][C0] == Wall
  BFS from (R0,C0) with 4-connected neighbors, skipping Wall cells
  DistGrid[R][C] = BFS distance from (R0,C0), or 9999 if unreachable

gd_recolor_by_dist(Grid, Color, Palette, NewGrid):
  Bg = most_frequent_color(Grid)
  DMap = gd_dist_map(Grid, Bg)
  PLen = length(Palette)
  for each (R,C):
    if Grid[R][C] == Color:
      D = DMap[R][C]
      if D <= PLen: NewGrid[R][C] = Palette[D]
      else: NewGrid[R][C] = Color
    else: NewGrid[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

gd_expand_n(Grid, Color, N, Expanded):
  if N == 0: Expanded = Grid
  else:
    DMap = gd_dist_map(Grid, Color)
    for each (R,C):
      if DMap[R][C] <= N: Expanded[R][C] = Color
      else: Expanded[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

gd_shrink_n(Grid, Color, N, Shrunk):
  if N == 0: Shrunk = Grid
  else:
    Bg = most_frequent_color(Grid)
    DMap = gd_dist_map(Grid, Bg)
    for each (R,C):
      if Grid[R][C] == Color and DMap[R][C] <= N: Shrunk[R][C] = Bg
      else: Shrunk[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

gd_equidistant(Grid, ColorA, ColorB, EqGrid):
  DMapA = gd_dist_map(Grid, ColorA)
  DMapB = gd_dist_map(Grid, ColorB)
  for each (R,C):
    if DMapA[R][C] == DMapB[R][C]: EqGrid[R][C] = equidist
    else: EqGrid[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

gd_max_dist(Grid, Color, R, C):
  DMap = gd_dist_map(Grid, Color)
  Dists = {DMap[R2][C2] | DMap[R2][C2] < 9999}
  fail if Dists empty
  MaxD = max(Dists)
  (R,C) = first cell in row-major order where DMap[R][C] == MaxD


PART 212 - WORK PACKAGE 222 PSEUDOCODE: gridperiod (Layer 201, gper_*)

gper_is_row_periodic(Grid, P):
  for all r in 0..H-1 where r+P < H:
    assert Grid[r] == Grid[r+P]
  // fails if any pair differs; vacuously true if no pairs

gper_is_col_periodic(Grid, P):
  for all r in 0..H-1, c in 0..W-1 where c+P < W:
    assert Grid[r][c] == Grid[r][c+P]

gper_row_period(Grid, P):
  find smallest P in 1..H such that gper_is_row_periodic(Grid, P)

gper_col_period(Grid, P):
  find smallest P in 1..W such that gper_is_col_periodic(Grid, P)

gper_tile_dims(Grid, PH, PW):
  PH = gper_row_period(Grid)
  PW = gper_col_period(Grid)

gper_extract_tile(Grid, TH, TW, Tile):
  Tile = Grid[0..TH-1][0..TW-1]  // top-left TH x TW sub-grid

gper_tile_grid(Tile, H, W, Grid):
  for each (r,c) in 0..H-1 x 0..W-1:
    Grid[r][c] = Tile[r mod TH][c mod TW]

gper_extend_rows(Grid, TargetH, Extended):
  for each r in 0..TargetH-1:
    Extended[r] = Grid[r mod H]

gper_extend_cols(Grid, TargetW, Extended):
  for each r in 0..H-1, c in 0..TargetW-1:
    Extended[r][c] = Grid[r][c mod W]

gper_extend(Grid, TargetH, TargetW, Extended):
  for each (r,c) in 0..TargetH-1 x 0..TargetW-1:
    Extended[r][c] = Grid[r mod H][c mod W]

gper_autocorr_row(Grid, P, Score):
  Pairs = {(r,r+P) | 0 <= r, r+P < H}
  Score = |{(r,r+P) in Pairs | Grid[r]==Grid[r+P]}| / |Pairs|
          (1.0 if Pairs is empty)

gper_autocorr_col(Grid, P, Score):
  Pairs = {(c,c+P) | 0 <= c, c+P < W}
  Score = |{(c,c+P) in Pairs | Grid[*][c]==Grid[*][c+P]}| / |Pairs|
          (1.0 if Pairs is empty)

gper_shift_wrap_rows(Grid, N, Shifted):
  for each r in 0..H-1:
    Shifted[r] = Grid[(r-N) mod H]

gper_shift_wrap_cols(Grid, N, Shifted):
  for each (r,c) in 0..H-1 x 0..W-1:
    Shifted[r][c] = Grid[r][(c-N) mod W]


PART 213 - WORK PACKAGE 223: gridscale PACK (LAYER 202, gsc_*) PSEUDOCODE

gsc_upsample(Grid, N, Scaled):
  H, W = dims(Grid)
  for r in 0..H*N-1:
    for c in 0..W*N-1:
      Scaled[r][c] = Grid[r//N][c//N]

gsc_downsample(Grid, N, Small):
  fail unless gsc_all_uniform(Grid, N)
  BH = H//N, BW = W//N
  for BR in 0..BH-1:
    for BC in 0..BW-1:
      Small[BR][BC] = color of block (BR, BC)

gsc_block_majority(Grid, N, Small):
  BH = H//N, BW = W//N
  for BR in 0..BH-1:
    for BC in 0..BW-1:
      cells = flatten(block_at(Grid, N, BR, BC))
      Small[BR][BC] = most_frequent(cells)

gsc_scale_factor(GridA, GridB, N):
  N = H_B // H_A  (must equal W_B // W_A)
  fail unless gsc_is_scale_of(GridA, GridB, N)

gsc_is_scale_of(GridA, GridB, N):
  for all (r,c) in GridB:
    fail if GridB[r][c] != GridA[r//N][c//N]
  succeed

gsc_block_at(Grid, N, BR, BC, Block):
  SR = BR*N, SC = BC*N
  Block = subgrid(Grid, SR, SC, N, N)

gsc_block_uniform(Grid, N, BR, BC, Color):
  Block = block_at(Grid, N, BR, BC)
  cells = flatten(Block)
  Color = first(cells)
  fail if any cell != Color

gsc_all_uniform(Grid, N):
  BH = H//N, BW = W//N
  for all (BR, BC): fail if not block_uniform(BR, BC)
  succeed

gsc_infer_tile(Grid, Tile):
  Divs = [N | N divides H and W, N >= 2] sorted descending
  for N in Divs:
    if gsc_all_uniform(Grid, N): return gsc_downsample(Grid, N)
  fail

gsc_factors(Grid, Factors):
  Factors = [N | N divides H and W, N in 1..min(H,W)] sorted ascending

gsc_resize(Grid, TargetH, TargetW, Resized):
  for r in 0..TargetH-1:
    for c in 0..TargetW-1:
      Resized[r][c] = Grid[(r*H)//TargetH][(c*W)//TargetW]

gsc_subsample(Grid, N, Sub):
  BH = H//N, BW = W//N
  for BR in 0..BH-1:
    for BC in 0..BW-1:
      Sub[BR][BC] = Grid[BR*N][BC*N]

gsc_pad(Grid, N, Color, Padded):
  NewH = H+2N, NewW = W+2N
  for r in 0..NewH-1:
    for c in 0..NewW-1:
      GR = r-N, GC = c-N
      if 0 <= GR < H and 0 <= GC < W: Padded[r][c] = Grid[GR][GC]
      else: Padded[r][c] = Color

gsc_crop_to_factor(Grid, N, Cropped):
  CH = (H//N)*N, CW = (W//N)*N
  Cropped = subgrid(Grid, 0, 0, CH, CW)


PART 214 - WORK PACKAGE 224: gridrun PACK (LAYER 203, grl_*) PSEUDOCODE

grl_list_runs_(List, Runs):
  if List empty: Runs = []
  else: accumulate starting with head color, count consecutive equal values

grl_row_runs(Grid, R, Runs):
  Row = Grid[R]; Runs = grl_list_runs_(Row)

grl_col_runs(Grid, C, Runs):
  Col = [Grid[r][C] for r in 0..H-1]; Runs = grl_list_runs_(Col)

grl_all_row_runs(Grid, AllRuns):
  AllRuns = [grl_row_runs(Grid, R) for R in 0..H-1]

grl_all_col_runs(Grid, AllRuns):
  AllRuns = [grl_col_runs(Grid, C) for C in 0..W-1]

grl_decode(Runs, List):
  List = [Color repeated N times for each Color-N in Runs]

grl_run_count(Grid, R, N):
  N = length(grl_row_runs(Grid, R))

grl_uniform_row(Grid, R, Color):
  grl_row_runs(Grid, R, [Color-_])

grl_uniform_col(Grid, C, Color):
  grl_col_runs(Grid, C, [Color-_])

grl_is_striped_h(Grid):
  for all R in 0..H-1: fail if not grl_uniform_row(Grid, R)

grl_is_striped_v(Grid):
  for all C in 0..W-1: fail if not grl_uniform_col(Grid, C)

grl_stripe_colors_h(Grid, Colors):
  Colors = [Color | R in 0..H-1, grl_uniform_row(Grid, R, Color)]
  fail if length(Colors) != H

grl_stripe_colors_v(Grid, Colors):
  Colors = [Color | C in 0..W-1, grl_uniform_col(Grid, C, Color)]
  fail if length(Colors) != W

grl_max_run(Grid, R, Color, Len):
  Runs = grl_row_runs(Grid, R)
  (Color, Len) = run with maximum length; ties broken by term order on Color

grl_alternating(Grid, R):
  Runs = grl_row_runs(Grid, R)
  all runs have length 1
  exactly 2 distinct colors appear in Runs
  length(Runs) >= 2


Part 215 - Work Package 225: gridflood Pack (gf_*, Layer 204)

Purpose: BFS-based flood-fill, connected-region analysis, and component enumeration
for raw grids. 4-connected and 8-connected neighborhoods supported.

Helper gf_dims_(Grid, H, W):
  length(Grid, H)
  if H > 0: head(Grid) -> FR; length(FR, W)
  else: W = 0

Helper gf_cell_(Grid, R, C, V):
  nth0(R, Grid) -> Row; nth0(C, Row) -> V

Helper gf_bfs4_(Grid, H, W, Color, Queue, Visited, Result):
  if Queue = []: Result = Visited, cut
  dequeue R-C from Queue
  if memberchk(R-C, Visited): recurse with same Visited
  else:
    Visited1 = [R-C | Visited]
    Nbrs = all NR-NC where DR-DC in [(-1,0),(1,0),(0,-1),(0,1)],
           NR = R+DR, NC = C+DC, in-bounds, not in Visited1, cell color = Color
    Queue1 = Queue ++ Nbrs
    recurse with Visited1, Queue1

Helper gf_bfs8_: same as gf_bfs4_ but uses 8 directions including diagonals.

Helper gf_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, NewColor, Result):
  for each row R, for each col C:
    if R-C in Cells: V = NewColor
    else: V = original Grid[R][C]

Helper gf_keep_larger_(Region, Best, Winner):
  if length(Region) > length(Best): Winner = Region else Winner = Best

Helper gf_extract_components_(Grid, H, W, Color, [Seed|Rest], [Region|Comps]):
  BFS from Seed to get Region
  Remaining = Rest minus Region
  recurse with Remaining

gf_fill(Grid, R, C, NewColor, Result):
  SeedColor = Grid[R][C]
  if SeedColor = NewColor: Result = Grid
  else: BFS4 from R-C, set_cells to NewColor

gf_fill8(Grid, R, C, NewColor, Result):
  SeedColor = Grid[R][C]
  if SeedColor = NewColor: Result = Grid
  else: BFS8 from R-C, set_cells to NewColor

gf_recolor(Grid, OldColor, NewColor, Result):
  for each cell: if color = OldColor then NewColor else original

gf_isolate(Grid, R, C, BgColor, Result):
  BFS4 from R-C to get RegionCells
  for each cell: if in RegionCells keep original else BgColor

gf_region_cells(Grid, R, C, Cells):
  BFS4 from R-C collecting all same-color cells

gf_region_size(Grid, R, C, N):
  region_cells then length

gf_region_bbox(Grid, R, C, MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC):
  region_cells; extract row coords -> min/max; extract col coords -> min/max

gf_enclosed_cells(Grid, BgColor, Enclosed):
  BorderSeeds = BgColor cells on grid border
  Reachable = BFS4 from BorderSeeds
  Enclosed = all BgColor cells not in Reachable

gf_fill_enclosed(Grid, BgColor, FillColor, Result):
  enclosed_cells then set_cells to FillColor

gf_components(Grid, Color, Components):
  AllCells = all Color cell positions in row-major order
  repeatedly extract one region at a time via extract_components_

gf_n_components(Grid, Color, N):
  components then length

gf_largest(Grid, Color, Cells):
  components -> [First|Rest]
  foldl keep_larger_ over Rest starting at First

gf_is_connected(Grid, Color, 4):
  n_components <= 1

gf_is_connected(Grid, Color, 8):
  AllCells = all Color positions
  if empty: true
  else BFS8 from first cell; length(AllCells) = length(Region)

gf_boundary_fill(Grid, R, C, BoundaryColor, FillColor, Result):
  SeedColor = Grid[R][C]
  if SeedColor = BoundaryColor: Result = Grid
  else: BFS4 from R-C for SeedColor; set_cells to FillColor


Part 216 - Work Package 226: gridpath Pack (gpa_*, Layer 205)

Purpose: BFS-based pathfinding, distance maps, flood expansion, line-of-sight,
and region-to-region path finding for raw grids. ObsColor cells are impassable.

Helper gpa_dims_(Grid, H, W): length(Grid,H); first row length = W.
Helper gpa_cell_(Grid, R, C, V): nth0 lookup.

Helper gpa_path_bfs_(Grid, H, W, Obs, TR, TC, Queue, Vis, Path):
  If Queue head is node(TR,TC,RevPath): reverse([TR-TC|RevPath]) -> Path, cut
  Else dequeue node(R,C,RevPath):
    if R-C in Vis: recurse skipping
    else:
      Vis1 = [R-C|Vis]
      Nbrs = findall node(NR,NC,[R-C|RevPath]) for 4-neighbors not in Vis1 and not Obs
      append Rest Nbrs -> Q1; recurse with Vis1 Q1

Helper gpa_reach_bfs_(Grid, H, W, Obs, Queue, Acc, Result):
  Standard BFS collecting visited non-Obs cells in Acc.

Helper gpa_dist_bfs_(Grid, H, W, Obs, Queue, Acc, Map):
  BFS collecting R-C-Dist triples; queue entries are node(R,C,D).
  Skip if R-C-_ already in Acc; add R-C-D to Acc; expand neighbors with D+1.

gpa_shortest_path(Grid,R1,C1,R2,C2,Obs,Path):
  check both endpoints passable; call gpa_path_bfs_([node(R1,C1,[])],[])

gpa_path_length: shortest_path then length(Path)-1
gpa_reachable: shortest_path with _ for Path
gpa_all_reachable: reach_bfs from [R-C] with []
gpa_distance_map: dist_bfs from [node(R,C,0)] with []

gpa_nearest(Grid,R,C,TargetColor,Obs,NR-NC):
  distance_map; filter for TargetColor cells; msort on D; take first

gpa_flood_n: distance_map; filter D =< N
gpa_wavefront: distance_map; filter D = N

gpa_straight_h(R,C1,C2,Cells):
  if C1 =< C2: findall R-C for C in C1..C2
  else: findall for C2..C1 then reverse

gpa_straight_v(C,R1,R2,Cells): same pattern using rows

gpa_line_of_sight(Grid,R1,C1,R2,C2,Obs):
  if R1=R2: check no Obs strictly between C1,C2
  elif C1=C2: check no Obs strictly between R1,R2
  else fail

gpa_between_h(R,C1,C2,Cells): interior cells of row segment (exclusive)
gpa_between_v(R1,R2,C,Cells): interior cells of column segment (exclusive)

gpa_region_path(Grid,Color1,Color2,Obs,Path):
  Seeds1 = all Color1 cells; Seeds2 = all Color2 cells
  findall Len-P for each (S1,S2) pair where shortest_path succeeds
  msort -> take first (shortest)


Part 217 - Work Package 227: gridmask Pack (gm_*, Layer 206)

Purpose: Boolean mask operations on raw grids. All output grids are rebuilt
by gm_build_ which applies a lambda cell-by-cell in row-major order.

Helper gm_dims_(Grid, H, W): length and first-row length.
Helper gm_cell_(Grid, R, C, V): nth0 double lookup.
Helper gm_build_(H, W, Goal, Grid): findall rows by calling Goal(R,C,V) for each cell.

gm_overlay(GridA, GridB, BgColor, _FgColor, Result):
  Cell = VB if VB != BgColor else VA.

gm_union(GridA, GridB, BgColor, Result):
  Cell = VA if VA != BgColor, else VB if VB != BgColor, else BgColor.

gm_intersect(GridA, GridB, BgColor, FgColor, Result):
  Cell = FgColor if VA != BgColor AND VB != BgColor, else BgColor.

gm_difference(GridA, GridB, BgColor, BgOut, Result):
  Cell = VA if VB = BgColor, else BgOut.

gm_invert(Grid, BgColor, FgColor, Result):
  Cell = BgColor if V != BgColor, else FgColor.

gm_mask_apply(Grid, Mask, BgColor, FillColor, Result):
  Cell = Grid[R][C] if Mask[R][C] != BgColor, else FillColor.

gm_extract(Grid, Cells, BgColor, Result):
  Cell = Grid[R][C] if R-C in Cells, else BgColor.

gm_stamp(Grid, Stamp, OR, OC, Result):
  SR = R - OR, SC = C - OC.
  If SR/SC in-bounds for Stamp: cell = Stamp[SR][SC].
  Else: cell = Grid[R][C].

gm_compare(GridA, GridB, _BgColor, Diff):
  Diff = all R-C where GridA[R][C] != GridB[R][C].

gm_equal(GridA, GridB): GridA = GridB (unification).

gm_sub(Grid, R0, C0, Height, Width, Sub):
  Check R0+Height-1 < H, C0+Width-1 < W.
  Sub = Height x Width grid extracted from Grid at (R0,C0).

gm_paste(Grid, Patch, R0, C0, BgColor, Result):
  PR = R - R0, PC = C - C0.
  If PR/PC in-bounds for Patch AND Patch[PR][PC] != BgColor: cell = Patch[PR][PC].
  Else: cell = Grid[R][C].

gm_border_mask(Grid, N, Mask):
  Cell = border if R < N OR R >= H-N OR C < N OR C >= W-N, else interior.

gm_color_mask(Grid, Color, FgColor, Mask):
  Cell = FgColor if Grid[R][C] = Color, else bg.

Part 218 - Work Package 228: gridxform Pack (gx_*, Layer 207)

gx_rotate90(Grid, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid)
  build W x H result where result[R][C] = Grid[H-1-C][R].

gx_rotate180(Grid, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid)
  build H x W result where result[R][C] = Grid[H-1-R][W-1-C].

gx_rotate270(Grid, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid)
  build W x H result where result[R][C] = Grid[C][W-1-R].

gx_flip_h(Grid, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid)
  build H x W result where result[R][C] = Grid[R][W-1-C].

gx_flip_v(Grid, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid)
  build H x W result where result[R][C] = Grid[H-1-R][C].

gx_transpose(Grid, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid)
  build W x H result where result[R][C] = Grid[C][R].

gx_flip_d2(Grid, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid)
  build W x H result where result[R][C] = Grid[H-1-C][W-1-R].

gx_crop(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Result):
  NewH = R1 - R0 + 1, NewW = C1 - C0 + 1
  build NewH x NewW result where result[R][C] = Grid[R0+R][C0+C].

gx_crop_content(Grid, BgColor, Result):
  Cells = [(R,C) | Grid[R][C] != BgColor]
  if Cells empty: Result = Grid
  else: MinR,MaxR = min/max of row indices; MinC,MaxC = min/max of col indices
        Result = gx_crop(Grid, MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC).

gx_pad(Grid, Top, Bot, Left, Right, BgColor, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid); NewH = H+Top+Bot; NewW = W+Left+Right
  result[R][C] = Grid[R-Top][C-Left] if 0<=R-Top<H and 0<=C-Left<W
                 else BgColor.

gx_scale(Grid, N, Result):
  H,W = dims(Grid); NewH = H*N; NewW = W*N
  result[R][C] = Grid[R//N][C//N].

gx_tile(Grid, H, W, Result):
  TH,TW = dims(Grid)
  result[R][C] = Grid[R mod TH][C mod TW].

gx_d4_group(Grid, Transforms):
  Transforms = [Grid, rotate90, rotate180, rotate270, flip_h, flip_v,
                transpose, flip_d2] applied to Grid.

gx_normalize(Grid, Canon):
  Canon = minimum of gx_d4_group(Grid) under standard Prolog term order.

Part 219 - Work Package 229: gridsymm Pack (gsm_*, Layer 208)

gsm_sym_h(Grid):
  H,W = dims(Grid); MaxR = (H-2)//2
  succeed if \+ exists R in [0..MaxR], C in [0..W-1]: Grid[R][C] != Grid[H-1-R][C].

gsm_sym_v(Grid):
  H,W = dims(Grid); MaxC = (W-2)//2
  succeed if \+ exists R in [0..H-1], C in [0..MaxC]: Grid[R][C] != Grid[R][W-1-C].

gsm_sym_d1(Grid): fail if H != W; succeed if \+ exists R < C: Grid[R][C] != Grid[C][R].
gsm_sym_d2(Grid): fail if H != W; succeed if \+ exists R+C < H-1: Grid[R][C] != Grid[H-1-C][H-1-R].
gsm_sym_rot90(Grid): fail if H != W; succeed if \+ exists (R,C): Grid[R][C] != Grid[H-1-C][R].
gsm_sym_rot180(Grid): succeed if \+ exists Idx < H*W/2: Grid[R][C] != Grid[H-1-R][W-1-C].

gsm_symmetries(Grid, Syms):
  test each applicable symmetry; collect those that hold into Syms.

gsm_complete_h(Grid, Dir, Result):
  Dir=top: result[R][C] = Grid[min(R,H-1-R)][C].
  Dir=bottom: result[R][C] = Grid[max(R,H-1-R)][C].

gsm_complete_v(Grid, Dir, Result):
  Dir=left: result[R][C] = Grid[R][min(C,W-1-C)].
  Dir=right: result[R][C] = Grid[R][max(C,W-1-C)].

gsm_complete_rot180(Grid, BgColor, Result):
  result[R][C] = Grid[R][C] if Grid[R][C] != BgColor
               | Grid[H-1-R][W-1-C] if Grid[H-1-R][W-1-C] != BgColor
               | BgColor.

gsm_violations_h(Grid, Cells): findall R-C where R in [0..MaxR] and Grid[R][C] != Grid[H-1-R][C].
gsm_violations_v(Grid, Cells): findall R-C where C in [0..MaxC] and Grid[R][C] != Grid[R][W-1-C].
gsm_violations_rot180(Grid, Cells): findall R-C where Idx < H*W/2 and Grid[R][C] != Grid[H-1-R][W-1-C].

gsm_score(Grid, Type, Score):
  Type in {h, v, rot180}
  Score = float(matching pairs) / float(total pairs checked).

Part 220 - Work Package 230: gridcolor Pack (gc_*, Layer 209)

gc_all_cells_(Grid, Cells): flatten all cell values in row-major order.

gc_count(Grid, Color, N): findall matching Color from gc_all_cells_; N = length.
gc_histogram(Grid, Pairs): sort(gc_all_cells_) -> Colors; for each C count occurrences -> C-N pairs.
gc_most_frequent(Grid, Color): histogram -> NCPairs; msort -> last = _-Color.
gc_least_frequent(Grid, Color): histogram -> NCPairs; msort -> first = _-Color.
gc_unique_colors(Grid, Colors): sort(gc_all_cells_) = Colors.
gc_color_cells(Grid, Color, Cells): findall R-C where cell = Color.
gc_contains(Grid, Color): gc_all_cells_ then memberchk(Color, All).
gc_recolor(Grid, Old, New, Result): build H x W: cell = Old -> New, else cell.
gc_color_map(Grid, Map, Result): build H x W: member(cell-NV, Map) -> NV, else cell.
gc_threshold(Grid, Colors, Fg, Bg, Result): build H x W: memberchk(cell, Colors) -> Fg, else Bg.
gc_dominant(Grid, BgColor, Color): histogram filtered for != BgColor; max count color.
gc_fraction(Grid, Color, Frac): gc_count / H*W as float.
gc_count_colors(Grid, N): length(gc_unique_colors).
gc_sorted_by_freq(Grid, Colors): histogram; negate counts; msort ascending; extract colors.


Part 221 - Work Package 231: gridstitch Pack (gst_*, Layer 210)

gst_concat_h(GridA, GridB, Result):
  gst_dims_(GridA, H, _), gst_dims_(GridB, H, _).
  maplist([RA,RB,RC]>>(append(RA,RB,RC)), GridA, GridB, Result).

gst_concat_v(GridA, GridB, Result):
  gst_dims_(GridA, _, W), gst_dims_(GridB, _, W).
  append(GridA, GridB, Result).

gst_hstack([], []).
gst_hstack([G], G) :- !.
gst_hstack([G1,G2|Rest], Result): gst_concat_h(G1,G2,G12), gst_hstack([G12|Rest], Result).

gst_vstack([], []).
gst_vstack([G], G) :- !.
gst_vstack([G1,G2|Rest], Result): gst_concat_v(G1,G2,G12), gst_vstack([G12|Rest], Result).

gst_split_h(Grid, R, Top, Bottom): length(Top, R), append(Top, Bottom, Grid).

gst_split_v(Grid, C, Left, Right):
  maplist([Row,LRow,RRow]>>(length(LRow,C), append(LRow,RRow,Row)), Grid, Left, Right).

gst_halves_h(Grid, Top, Bottom): gst_dims_(Grid,H,_), Half is H//2, gst_split_h(Grid,Half,Top,Bottom).
gst_halves_v(Grid, Left, Right): gst_dims_(Grid,_,W), Half is W//2, gst_split_v(Grid,Half,Left,Right).

gst_quadrants(Grid, TL, TR, BL, BR):
  gst_halves_h(Grid, Top, Bottom).
  gst_halves_v(Top, TL, TR).
  gst_halves_v(Bottom, BL, BR).

gst_tile_grid(SubGrids, NR, NC, Result):
  NTotal is NR*NC, length(SubGrids, NTotal).
  findall(Band, (between(1,NR,RowIdx), Start is (RowIdx-1)*NC,
    findall(SG, (between(0,NC,Col), Col<NC, Pos is Start+Col, nth0(Pos,SubGrids,SG)), RowSubs),
    gst_hstack(RowSubs, Band)), Bands).
  gst_vstack(Bands, Result).

gst_add_border(Grid, N, Color, Result):
  gst_dims_(Grid,H,W), NewH is H+2*N, NewW is W+2*N.
  gst_build_(NewH, NewW, [R,C,V]>>(OR is R-N, OC is C-N,
    (OR>=0,OR<H,OC>=0,OC<W -> gst_cell_(Grid,OR,OC,V) ; V=Color)), Result).

gst_strip_border(Grid, N, Result):
  gst_dims_(Grid,H,W), NewH is H-2*N, NewW is W-2*N.
  gst_build_(NewH, NewW, [R,C,V]>>(OR is R+N, OC is C+N, gst_cell_(Grid,OR,OC,V)), Result).

gst_repeat_h(Grid, N, Result): findall(Grid, between(1,N,_), Copies), gst_hstack(Copies, Result).
gst_repeat_v(Grid, N, Result): findall(Grid, between(1,N,_), Copies), gst_vstack(Copies, Result).


Part 222 - Work Package 232: gridedge Pack (ge_*, Layer 211)

ge_edge_cells(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  ge_dims_(Grid,H,W); H1 is H-1; W1 is W-1.
  findall(R-C, (between(0,H1,R), between(0,W1,C),
    ge_cell_(Grid,R,C,FgColor),
    once((ge_nbr4_(R,C,NR,NC), ge_cell_(Grid,NR,NC,NV), NV\=FgColor))), Cells).

ge_edge_cells8(Grid, FgColor, Cells): same but ge_nbr8_.

ge_is_edge(Grid, R-C, Bool):
  ge_cell_(Grid,R,C,V).
  (once((ge_nbr4_(R,C,NR,NC), ge_cell_(Grid,NR,NC,NV), NV\=V)) -> Bool=yes ; Bool=no).

ge_boundary(Grid, Color1, Color2, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (between(0,H1,R), between(0,W1,C),
    ge_cell_(Grid,R,C,Color1),
    once((ge_nbr4_(R,C,NR,NC), ge_cell_(Grid,NR,NC,Color2)))), Cells).

ge_inner_border(Grid, BgColor, Cells): ge_boundary_to_nonbg_(Grid,BgColor,Cells).
  Private: BgColor cells with once((ge_nbr4_, ge_cell_!=BgColor)).

ge_outer_border(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell!=FgColor,
    once((ge_nbr4_, ge_cell_==FgColor))), Cells).

ge_edge_grid(Grid, FgColor, EdgeColor, Result):
  ge_edge_cells(Grid,FgColor,Edges).
  ge_build_(H,W, [R,C,V]>>(ge_cell_(Grid,R,C,GV),
    (memberchk(R-C,Edges)->V=EdgeColor;V=GV)), Result).

ge_edge_count(Grid, FgColor, N): ge_edge_cells(Grid,FgColor,Cells); length(Cells,N).

ge_neighbors_diff(Grid, R, C, Neighbors):
  ge_cell_(Grid,R,C,V).
  findall(NR-NC, (ge_nbr4_(R,C,NR,NC), ge_cell_(Grid,NR,NC,NV), NV\=V), Neighbors).

ge_corners(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell=FgColor,
    findall(1,(ge_nbr4_,cell!=FgColor),Diff), length(Diff,D), D>=2), Cells).

ge_endpoints(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell=FgColor,
    findall(1,(ge_nbr4_,cell=FgColor),Same), length(Same,1)), Cells).

ge_smooth_cells(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell=FgColor,
    \+(ge_nbr4_,cell!=FgColor)), Cells).

ge_transition_map(Grid, Result):
  ge_build_(H,W, [R,C,V]>>(ge_cell_(Grid,R,C,GV),
    findall(1,(ge_nbr4_,cell!=GV),Diffs), length(Diffs,V)), Result).

ge_edge_color_count(Grid, FgColor, BgColor, N):
  ge_boundary(Grid,FgColor,BgColor,Cells); length(Cells,N).


Part 223 - Work Package 233: gridmorph Pack (gmo_*, Layer 212)

gmo_dilate1(Grid, FgColor, Result):
  gmo_dims_(Grid, H, W)
  gmo_build_(H, W, [R,C,V]>>(
    gmo_cell_(Grid,R,C,GV),
    if GV=FgColor then V=FgColor
    else if once(nbr4 exists with FgColor) then V=FgColor
    else V=GV), Result).

gmo_erode1(Grid, FgColor, Result):
  gmo_bg_color_(Grid, FgColor, BgColor)
  gmo_dims_(Grid, H, W)
  gmo_build_(H, W, [R,C,V]>>(
    gmo_cell_(Grid,R,C,GV),
    if GV=FgColor then
      (if once(nbr4 exists with color!=FgColor) then V=BgColor else V=FgColor)
    else V=GV), Result).

gmo_dilate(Grid, FgColor, N, Result):
  iterate gmo_dilate1 N times starting from Grid.

gmo_erode(Grid, FgColor, N, Result):
  gmo_bg_color_(Grid, FgColor, BgColor) or BgColor=bg
  iterate gmo_erode1_step_(Grid, FgColor, BgColor) N times.

gmo_open(Grid, FgColor, N, Result):
  gmo_erode(Grid, FgColor, N, Eroded)
  gmo_dilate(Eroded, FgColor, N, Result).

gmo_close(Grid, FgColor, N, Result):
  gmo_dilate(Grid, FgColor, N, Dilated)
  gmo_erode(Dilated, FgColor, N, Result).

gmo_boundary_inner(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell=FgColor,
    once(nbr4 exists with color!=FgColor)), Cells).

gmo_boundary_outer(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell!=FgColor,
    once(nbr4 exists with color=FgColor)), Cells).

gmo_gradient_cells(Grid, FgColor, Cells):
  gmo_boundary_inner(Grid, FgColor, Inner)
  gmo_boundary_outer(Grid, FgColor, Outer)
  append(Inner, Outer, Cells).

gmo_top_hat(Grid, FgColor, N, Cells):
  gmo_open(Grid, FgColor, N, Opened)
  findall(R-C, (cell(Grid)=FgColor, cell(Opened)!=FgColor), Cells).

gmo_bottom_hat(Grid, FgColor, N, Cells):
  gmo_close(Grid, FgColor, N, Closed)
  findall(R-C, (cell(Closed)=FgColor, cell(Grid)!=FgColor), Cells).

gmo_fill_holes(Grid, FgColor, BgColor, Result):
  gmo_connected_border(Grid, BgColor, FgColor, OpenBg)
  gmo_build_(H, W, [R,C,V]>>(
    if cell=BgColor then
      (if R-C in OpenBg then V=BgColor else V=FgColor)
    else V=cell), Result).

gmo_connected_border(Grid, TargetColor, BlockColor, Cells):
  Seeds = border cells with TargetColor
  BFS from Seeds through TargetColor cells (BlockColor stops expansion).

gmo_remove_small(Grid, FgColor, BgColor, MinSize, Result):
  AllFg = all FgColor cells
  SmallCells = cells in FgColor components where length < MinSize
  build result replacing SmallCells with BgColor.


Part 224 - Work Package 234: gridconv Pack (gcv_*, Layer 213)

gcv_window(Grid, R, C, N, Fill, Window):
  Size = 2*N+1
  gcv_build_(Size, Size, [WRow,WCol,V]>>(
    GR = R-N+WRow, GC = C-N+WCol,
    gcv_cell_fill_(Grid, GR, GC, Fill, V)), Window).

gcv_count_in(Grid, R, C, N, Color, Count):
  RMin=R-N, RMax=R+N, CMin=C-N, CMax=C+N
  findall(1, (between(RMin,RMax,WR), between(CMin,CMax,WC),
              gcv_cell_(Grid,WR,WC,Color)), Ones)
  length(Ones, Count).

gcv_density_map(Grid, N, Color, DMap):
  gcv_build_(H, W, [R,C,Count]>>(gcv_count_in(Grid,R,C,N,Color,Count)), DMap).

gcv_majority(Grid, R, C, N, Color):
  gcv_inbounds_vals_(Grid, R, C, N, Vals)
  gcv_mode_(Vals, Color).  % mode = most frequent; ties by term order

gcv_majority_map(Grid, N, Result):
  gcv_build_(H, W, [R,C,Maj]>>(gcv_majority(Grid,R,C,N,Maj)), Result).

gcv_uniform_at(Grid, R, C, N, Bool):
  gcv_inbounds_vals_(Grid, R, C, N, Vals)
  if Vals != [] and gcv_all_eq_(Vals) then Bool=yes else Bool=no.

gcv_uniform_cells(Grid, N, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell, gcv_uniform_at(Grid,R,C,N,yes)), Cells).

gcv_find_pattern(Grid, Pattern, Positions):
  RMax=GH-PH, CMax=GW-PW
  findall(R-C, (between(0,RMax,R), between(0,CMax,C),
                gcv_match_at_(Grid,Pattern,R,C)), Positions).

gcv_count_pattern(Grid, Pattern, Count):
  gcv_find_pattern(Grid, Pattern, Positions); length(Positions, Count).

gcv_has_pattern(Grid, Pattern):
  once(gcv_match_at_(Grid, Pattern, _, _)).

gcv_hot_spots(Grid, N, Color, Threshold, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell, gcv_count_in(Grid,R,C,N,Color,Count), Count>=Threshold), Cells).

gcv_dilate_sq(Grid, FgColor, N, Result):
  gcv_build_(H, W, [R,C,V]>>(
    if cell=FgColor then V=FgColor
    else if gcv_count_in(Grid,R,C,N,FgColor,Count) > 0 then V=FgColor
    else V=cell), Result).

gcv_erode_sq(Grid, FgColor, N, Result):
  find BgColor (first non-FgColor cell)
  gcv_build_(H, W, [R,C,V]>>(
    if cell=FgColor then
      (if gcv_count_inbounds_ = gcv_count_in(FgColor) then V=FgColor else V=BgColor)
    else V=cell), Result).

gcv_replace_pattern(Grid, Pattern, Replacement, Result):
  find first (R0,C0) where gcv_match_at_(Grid,Pattern,R0,C0)
  build result: cells in [R0..R0+PH-1][C0..C0+PW-1] come from Replacement;
  all other cells from Grid. If no match, Result=Grid.


Part 225 - Work Package 235: gridgraph Pack (ggr_*, Layer 214)

ggr_adj_colors(Grid, Pairs):
  findall(P, (cell(Grid,R,C,V), nbr4 has NV, NV!=V,
              if V@<NV then P=V-NV else P=NV-V), Raw)
  list_to_set(Raw, Pairs).

ggr_adj_of(Grid, Color, Neighbors):
  findall(NV, (cell=Color, nbr4=NV, NV!=Color), Raw)
  list_to_set(Raw, Neighbors).

ggr_adj_graph(Grid, Graph):
  ggr_colors_(Grid, Colors)
  findall(C-Nbrs, (member(C,Colors), ggr_adj_of(Grid,C,Nbrs)), Graph).

ggr_are_adj(Grid, C1, C2):
  C1!=C2; once(cell=C1, nbr4=C2).

ggr_color_degree(Grid, Color, N):
  ggr_adj_of(Grid, Color, Nbrs); length(Nbrs, N).

ggr_shared_border(Grid, C1, C2, Cells):
  findall(R-C, (cell=C1, once(nbr4=C2)), Cells).

ggr_border_length(Grid, C1, C2, N):
  ggr_shared_border(Grid,C1,C2,Cells); length(Cells,N).

ggr_isolated_colors(Grid, Colors):
  ggr_colors_(Grid, All)
  findall(C, (member(C,All), ggr_color_degree(Grid,C,0)), Colors).

ggr_enclosed_colors(Grid, InnerColors, OuterColor):
  subtract(AllColors, [OuterColor], Candidates)
  findall(C, (member(C,Candidates),
    not(border cell has color C),
    not(C cell has non-C non-OuterColor 4-neighbor)), InnerColors).

ggr_spanning_h(Grid, Colors):
  findall(C, (color C exists in col 0 AND in last col), Raw)
  list_to_set(Raw, Colors).

ggr_spanning_v(Grid, Colors):
  findall(C, (color C exists in row 0 AND in last row), Raw)
  list_to_set(Raw, Colors).

ggr_merge_colors(Grid, From, To, Result):
  maplist([Row,NewRow]>>(maplist([V,NV]>>(V=From->NV=To;NV=V), Row, NewRow)),
          Grid, Result).

ggr_color_components(Grid, Color, N):
  find AllCells of Color; BFS from each unvisited cell; count iterations.

ggr_component_cells(Grid, Color, Components):
  find AllCells of Color; BFS from each unvisited cell; collect component lists.


Part 226 - Work Package 236: griddiag Pack (gdi_*, Layer 215)

gdi_main_diag(Grid, K, Vals):
  dims H, W; RMin=max(0,-K), RMax=min(H-1,W-1-K)
  findall(V, (between(RMin,RMax,R), C=R+K, cell(R,C,V)), Vals).

gdi_anti_diag(Grid, K, Vals):
  dims H, W; CMin=max(0,K-H+1), CMax=min(W-1,K)
  findall(V, (between(CMin,CMax,C), R=K-C, cell(R,C,V)), Vals).

gdi_trace(Grid, Vals): gdi_main_diag(Grid, 0, Vals).

gdi_all_main_diags(Grid, Diags):
  KMin=-(H-1), KMax=W-1
  findall(Vals, (between(KMin,KMax,K), gdi_main_diag(Grid,K,Vals)), Diags).

gdi_all_anti_diags(Grid, Diags):
  KMax=H+W-2
  findall(Vals, (between(0,KMax,K), gdi_anti_diag(Grid,K,Vals)), Diags).

gdi_main_count(Grid, K, Color, Count):
  gdi_main_diag(Grid, K, Vals)
  findall(1, member(Color,Vals), Ones); length(Ones, Count).

gdi_anti_count(Grid, K, Color, Count):
  gdi_anti_diag(Grid, K, Vals)
  findall(1, member(Color,Vals), Ones); length(Ones, Count).

gdi_main_uniform(Grid, K, Bool):
  gdi_main_diag(Grid,K,Vals); Vals != []
  if gdi_all_eq_(Vals) then yes else no.

gdi_anti_uniform(Grid, K, Bool):
  gdi_anti_diag(Grid,K,Vals); Vals != []
  if gdi_all_eq_(Vals) then yes else no.

gdi_set_main_diag(Grid, K, Color, Result):
  collect DiagCells
  gdi_build_(H,W, [R,C,V]>>(if R-C in DiagCells then V=Color else V=orig), Result).

gdi_set_anti_diag(Grid, K, Color, Result):
  collect DiagCells (anti-diagonal K)
  gdi_build_(H,W, [R,C,V]>>(if R-C in DiagCells then V=Color else V=orig), Result).

gdi_uniform_main_diags(Grid, Ks):
  findall(K, (between(KMin,KMax,K), gdi_main_uniform(Grid,K,yes)), Ks).

gdi_uniform_anti_diags(Grid, Ks):
  findall(K, (between(0,KMax,K), gdi_anti_uniform(Grid,K,yes)), Ks).

gdi_diag_length(Grid, K, Len):
  gdi_main_diag(Grid, K, Vals); length(Vals, Len).


Part 227 - Work Package 237: gridframe Pack (gfr_*, Layer 216)

gfr_cell_depth(Grid, R, C, D):
  dims H, W; D = min(min(R, H-1-R), min(C, W-1-C)).

gfr_frame(Grid, D, Cells):
  dims H, W; findall R-C: between(0..H-1,R), between(0..W-1,C), depth(H,W,R,C)=D.

gfr_max_depth(Grid, D):
  dims H, W; D = (min(H,W)-1)//2.

gfr_frame_count(Grid, N):
  gfr_max_depth(Grid, D); N = D+1.

gfr_peel(Grid, Inner):
  dims H, W; H>=3, W>=3; H1=H-2, W1=W-2
  build H1 x W1: V = cell(Grid, R+1, C+1).

gfr_all_frames(Grid, Frames):
  gfr_max_depth(Grid, MaxD)
  findall Cells: between(0,MaxD,D), gfr_frame(Grid,D,Cells).

gfr_frame_uniform(Grid, D, Bool):
  gfr_frame(Grid,D,Cells); Cells != []
  Vals = [V | R-C in Cells, cell(R,C,V)]
  if gfr_all_eq_(Vals) then yes else no.

gfr_frame_colors(Grid, D, Colors):
  gfr_frame(Grid,D,Cells)
  Vals = [V | R-C in Cells, cell(R,C,V)]
  list_to_set(Vals, Colors).

gfr_set_frame(Grid, D, Color, Result):
  build H x W: depth(R,C)=Dep; if Dep=D then Color else orig.

gfr_count_in_frame(Grid, D, Color, Count):
  gfr_frame(Grid,D,Cells)
  count 1 for R-C in Cells where cell(R,C)=Color.

gfr_uniform_frames(Grid, Ds):
  findall D: between(0,MaxD,D), gfr_frame_uniform(Grid,D,yes).

gfr_fill_frames(Grid, Colors, Result):
  build H x W: depth(R,C)=D; if nth0(D,Colors,FC) then FC else orig.

gfr_innermost(Grid, Cells):
  gfr_max_depth(Grid, MaxD); gfr_frame(Grid, MaxD, Cells).

gfr_onion_layers(Grid, Layers):
  findall D-Color: between(0,MaxD,D), gfr_frame uniform with Color.


Part 228 - Work Package 238: gridspiral Pack (gsp_*, Layer 217)

gsp_spiral(Grid, Cells):
  dims H, W; max_depth = (min(H,W)-1)//2
  for D in [0..max_depth]: gsp_frame_spiral_(H,W,D,FC); append all → Cells.

gsp_frame_spiral_(H, W, D, Cells):
  RowMin=D, RowMax=H-1-D, ColMin=D, ColMax=W-1-D
  Top: [(RowMin,C) | C in ColMin..ColMax]
  Right: [(R,ColMax) | R in RowMin+1..RowMax] if RowMax > RowMin
  Bot: reverse [(RowMax,C) | C in ColMin..ColMax-1] if RowMax > RowMin and ColMax > ColMin
  Left: reverse [(R,ColMin) | R in RowMin+1..RowMax-1] if both conditions hold
  Cells = Top ++ Right ++ Bot ++ Left.

gsp_read_spiral(Grid, Vals):
  gsp_spiral(Grid, Cells); [cell(R,C) | R-C in Cells].

gsp_write_spiral(Grid, Vals, Result):
  gsp_spiral(Grid, Cells); build H x W:
    for each (R,C): find Idx where Cells[Idx]=R-C;
    if nth0(Idx,Vals,V) then V else orig.

gsp_spiral_length(Grid, Len): Len = H*W.

gsp_spiral_index(Grid, R, C, Idx): nth0(Idx, spiral, R-C).

gsp_nth_spiral(Grid, N, R, C): nth0(N, spiral, R-C).

gsp_frame_spiral(Grid, D, Cells): gsp_frame_spiral_(H,W,D,Cells).

gsp_all_frame_spirals(Grid, Spirals): collect frame spirals D=0..max_depth.

gsp_spiral_uniform(Grid, Bool):
  read_spiral → Vals; if all equal then yes else no.

gsp_spiral_reversed(Grid, Rev): reverse(spiral, Rev).

gsp_spiral_count(Grid, Color, Count): count Color in read_spiral.

gsp_fill_spiral = gsp_write_spiral.

gsp_rotate_spiral(Grid, N, Result):
  read → Vals; Len=length(Vals); Shift = N mod Len
  Rotated = Vals[Shift..] ++ Vals[..Shift-1]
  gsp_write_spiral(Grid, Rotated, Result).

gsp_spiral_slice(Grid, Start, End, Slice):
  spiral → Cells; collect Cells[I] for I in [Start..End].


Part 229 - Work Package 239: griddelta Pack (gdt_*, Layer 218)

gdt_compatible(G1, G2): dims(G1)=dims(G2).

gdt_diff_cells(G1, G2, Cells):
  findall R-C: cell(G1,R,C,V1), cell(G2,R,C,V2), V1\=V2.

gdt_diff_count(G1, G2, Count): length(diff_cells, Count).

gdt_same_cells(G1, G2, Cells):
  findall R-C: cell(G1,R,C,V), cell(G2,R,C,V).

gdt_changed_pairs(G1, G2, Pairs):
  findall R-C-(V1->V2): cell(G1,R,C,V1), cell(G2,R,C,V2), V1\=V2.

gdt_color_changes(G1, G2, From, Count):
  count cells where G1(R,C)=From and G2(R,C)\=From.

gdt_changed_colors(G1, G2, Colors):
  new values from changed_pairs; list_to_set.

gdt_apply_delta(G1, G2, G3, Result):
  build H x W: V1=cell(G1,R,C), V2=cell(G2,R,C), V3=cell(G3,R,C)
  if V1\=V2 and V3=V1 then V=V2 else V=V3.

gdt_diff_rows(G1, G2, Rows):
  row indices R in diff_cells; list_to_set.

gdt_diff_cols(G1, G2, Cols):
  col indices C in diff_cells; list_to_set.

gdt_agree_region(G1, G2, R0, R1, C0, C1):
  \+ (between(R0,R1,R), between(C0,C1,C), cell(G1,R,C,V1), cell(G2,R,C,V2), V1\=V2).

gdt_overlay(G1, G2, Marker, Result):
  build H x W: if cell(G2,R,C,V2), V2\=Marker then V=V2 else V=cell(G1,R,C).

gdt_invert_delta(G1, G2, Inv):
  build H x W: if cell(G1)!=cell(G2) then V=cell(G1) else V=cell(G2).

gdt_is_identity(G1, G2): diff_count = 0.

Part 230 - WP 240 Pseudocode: gridrowcol Pack (grc_*, Layer 219)

grc_row(Grid, R, Row): nth0(R, Grid, Row).

grc_col(Grid, C, Col): Col = [V | V <- member(Row, Grid), nth0(C, Row, V)].

grc_row_uniform(Grid, R, Color):
  Row = grc_row(Grid, R).
  Row = [Color | Rest].
  forall V in Rest: V = Color.

grc_col_uniform(Grid, C, Color):
  Col = grc_col(Grid, C).
  Col = [Color | Rest].
  forall V in Rest: V = Color.

grc_equal_rows(Grid, R1, R2): nth0(R1, Grid, Row), nth0(R2, Grid, Row).

grc_equal_cols(Grid, C1, C2): grc_col(C1) = grc_col(C2).

grc_row_positions(Grid, Pattern, Positions):
  H = length(Grid).
  Positions = [R | between(0, H-1, R), nth0(R, Grid) = Pattern].

grc_col_positions(Grid, Pattern, Positions):
  W = col_count(Grid).
  Positions = [C | between(0, W-1, C), grc_col(C) = Pattern].

grc_matching_rows(Grid, Pairs):
  H = length(Grid).
  Pairs = [R1-R2 | 0 <= R1 < R2 < H, row(R1) = row(R2)].

grc_matching_cols(Grid, Pairs):
  W = col_count(Grid).
  Pairs = [C1-C2 | 0 <= C1 < C2 < W, col(C1) = col(C2)].

grc_unique_rows(Grid, Rows):
  H = length(Grid).
  Rows = [R | 0<=R<H, no R2 in 0..H-1 with R2!=R and row(R2)=row(R)].

grc_unique_cols(Grid, Cols):
  W = col_count(Grid).
  Cols = [C | 0<=C<W, no C2 in 0..W-1 with C2!=C and col(C2)=col(C)].

grc_row_sort(Grid, Sorted): msort(Grid, Sorted).

grc_col_sort(Grid, Sorted):
  Cols = [col(C) | C in 0..W-1].
  SortedCols = msort(Cols).
  Sorted[R][i] = SortedCols[i][R] for each row R, col-slot i.

Part 231 - WP 241 Pseudocode: gridseg Pack (gsg_*, Layer 220)

gsg_is_sep_row(Grid, R, Color):
  Row = Grid[R].
  Row = [Color | Rest].
  forall V in Rest: V = Color.

gsg_is_sep_col(Grid, C, Color):
  Col = column C of Grid.
  Col = [Color | Rest].
  forall V in Rest: V = Color.

gsg_sep_rows(Grid, Color, Rows):
  Rows = [R | 0<=R<H, gsg_is_sep_row(Grid, R, Color)].

gsg_sep_cols(Grid, Color, Cols):
  Cols = [C | 0<=C<W, gsg_is_sep_col(Grid, C, Color)].

gsg_split_h(Grid, Color, Segments):
  Walk rows top-to-bottom with accumulator Acc.
  If row is uniform Color: flush Acc as segment (if non-empty), reset Acc.
  Else: prepend row to Acc.
  At end: flush remaining Acc.

gsg_split_v(Grid, Color, Segments):
  Trans = transpose(Grid).
  TSegs = split_h(Trans, Color).
  Segments = [transpose(S) | S in TSegs].

gsg_segment_count_h(Grid, Color, N): N = length(split_h(Grid, Color)).
gsg_segment_count_v(Grid, Color, N): N = length(split_v(Grid, Color)).

gsg_panels(Grid, Color, Panels):
  RowSegs = split_h(Grid, Color).
  Panel2D = [split_v(Seg, Color) | Seg in RowSegs].
  Panels = flatten one level of Panel2D.

gsg_panel_count(Grid, Color, N): N = length(panels(Grid, Color)).

gsg_trim_h(Grid, Color, Trimmed):
  Front = drop_leading_sep(Grid, Color).
  Trimmed = reverse(drop_leading_sep(reverse(Front), Color)).

gsg_trim_v(Grid, Color, Trimmed):
  Trans = transpose(Grid).
  Trimmed = transpose(trim_h(Trans, Color)).

gsg_trim(Grid, Color, Trimmed): trim_v(trim_h(Grid, Color), Color).

gsg_sep_color(Grid, Color):
  RowColors = distinct colors used in uniform rows.
  ColColors = distinct colors used in uniform columns.
  AllColors = set_union(RowColors, ColColors).
  AllColors = [Color].  % exactly one color

Part 232 - WP 242 Pseudocode: gridhist Pack (ghst_*, Layer 221)

ghst_list_hist_(List, Hist):
  Sorted = msort(List).
  Walk Sorted, counting runs of equal elements.
  Hist = [Color-Count | for each distinct Color in sort order].

ghst_row_hist(Grid, R, Hist): Hist = list_hist(Grid[R]).
ghst_col_hist(Grid, C, Hist): Hist = list_hist(column C of Grid).

ghst_all_row_hists(Grid, AllHists): AllHists = [row_hist(R) | R in 0..H-1].
ghst_all_col_hists(Grid, AllHists): AllHists = [col_hist(C) | C in 0..W-1].

ghst_modal_(Hist, Color): Color is C where C-N in Hist with maximum N (tie: last sort).
ghst_modal_row(Grid, R, Color): Color = modal(row_hist(R)).
ghst_modal_col(Grid, C, Color): Color = modal(col_hist(C)).

ghst_row_count(Grid, R, Color, Count): Count = |{V in Grid[R] : V = Color}|.
ghst_col_count(Grid, C, Color, Count): Count = |{V in col(C) : V = Color}|.

ghst_row_entropy(Grid, R, N): N = length(row_hist(R)).
ghst_col_entropy(Grid, C, N): N = length(col_hist(C)).

ghst_max_row(Grid, Color, Row):
  Pairs = [(count(R,Color), R) | R in 0..H-1, count > 0].
  Fail if Pairs empty.
  Row = R from pair with max count (tie: max R).

ghst_min_row(Grid, Color, Row):
  Pairs = [(count(R,Color), R) | R in 0..H-1, count > 0].
  Fail if Pairs empty.
  Row = R from pair with min count (tie: min R).

ghst_rows_with(Grid, Color, N, Rows): Rows = [R | count(R,Color) >= N].
ghst_cols_with(Grid, Color, N, Cols): Cols = [C | count(C,Color) >= N].

Part 233 - Work Package 243: gridpos Pseudocode

gps_top_half(Grid, TopGrid):
  HMid = H // 2.
  If HMid = 0: TopGrid = [].
  Else: TopGrid = [Grid[R] | R in 0..HMid-1].

gps_bottom_half(Grid, BotGrid):
  HMid = H // 2.
  BotGrid = [Grid[R] | R in HMid..H-1].

gps_left_half(Grid, LeftGrid):
  WMid = W // 2.
  If WMid = 0: LeftGrid = [[] | each row].
  Else: LeftGrid = [row[0..WMid-1] | each row in Grid].

gps_right_half(Grid, RightGrid):
  WMid = W // 2.
  RightGrid = [row[WMid..W-1] | each row in Grid].

gps_quadrant(Grid, Quad, SubGrid):
  (R0,R1,C0,C1) = range for Quad.
  SubGrid = subgrid(Grid, R0, R1, C0, C1).

gps_even_rows(Grid, EvenGrid): EvenGrid = [Grid[R] | R in 0..H-1, R mod 2 = 0].
gps_odd_rows(Grid, OddGrid): OddGrid = [Grid[R] | R in 0..H-1, R mod 2 = 1].

gps_even_cols(Grid, EvenColGrid):
  EvenColGrid = [row[C for C in 0..W-1 if C mod 2 = 0] | row in Grid].

gps_odd_cols(Grid, OddColGrid):
  OddColGrid = [row[C for C in 0..W-1 if C mod 2 = 1] | row in Grid].

gps_checkerboard(Grid, Parity, Cells):
  Cells = [R-C | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, (R+C) mod 2 = Parity].

gps_center_cell(Grid, R, C): R = H//2, C = W//2.

gps_corners(Grid, Corners):
  Corners = [0-0-V00, 0-W1-V0W, H1-0-VH0, H1-W1-VHW].

gps_cross_h(Grid, R, Row): R = H//2, Row = Grid[R].
gps_cross_v(Grid, C, Col): C = W//2, Col = [Grid[R][C] | R in 0..H-1].

Part 234 - Work Package 244: gridgrav Pseudocode

gv_fall_down(Grid, BgColor, Fallen):
  For each column C: Col = col(Grid, C).
    NonBg = [V | V in Col, V != BgColor].
    BgN = len(Col) - len(NonBg).
    SettledCol = [BgColor * BgN] ++ NonBg.
  Fallen = reconstruct(H, W, SettledCols).

gv_fall_up(Grid, BgColor, Fallen):
  Same as fall_down but SettledCol = NonBg ++ [BgColor * BgN].

gv_fall_left(Grid, BgColor, Fallen):
  For each row Row: NonBg = [V | V in Row, V != BgColor].
    BgN = len(Row) - len(NonBg). Row' = NonBg ++ [BgColor * BgN].
  Fallen = [Row' | Row in Grid].

gv_fall_right(Grid, BgColor, Fallen):
  Same as fall_left but Row' = [BgColor * BgN] ++ NonBg.

gv_col_pile_h(Grid, C, BgColor, H):
  H = |{V in col(C) : V != BgColor}|.

gv_row_pile_w(Grid, R, BgColor, W):
  W = |{V in row(R) : V != BgColor}|.

gv_all_col_piles(Grid, BgColor, Piles):
  Piles = [col_pile_h(C) | C in 0..W-1].

gv_all_row_piles(Grid, BgColor, Piles):
  Piles = [row_pile_w(R) | R in 0..H-1].

gv_floating_cells(Grid, BgColor, Cells):
  Cells = [R-C | V=Grid[R][C], V!=BgColor, R+1<H, Grid[R+1][C]=BgColor].

gv_settled(Grid, BgColor): floating_cells(Grid, BgColor) = [].

gv_col_gap_above(Grid, C, BgColor, Gap):
  Count leading BgColor cells in col(C) from top.

gv_max_col_pile(Grid, BgColor, MaxC):
  BestH = max(col_pile_h(C) for all C).
  MaxC = min C where col_pile_h(C) = BestH.

gv_min_col_pile(Grid, BgColor, MinC):
  BestH = min(col_pile_h(C) for all C).
  MinC = min C where col_pile_h(C) = BestH.

gv_non_bg_count(Grid, BgColor, N):
  N = |{V : V in Grid, V != BgColor}|.

Part 235 - Work Package 245: gridtile Pseudocode

gti_h_period(Grid, P):
  Find smallest P dividing H where row R = row(R mod P) for all R.

gti_w_period(Grid, P):
  Find smallest P dividing W where col C = col(C mod P) for all C.

gti_tile_size(Grid, HP, WP):
  HP = h_period(Grid), WP = w_period(Grid).

gti_is_tiling(Grid, TH, TW):
  H mod TH = 0, W mod TW = 0,
  rows_have_period(Grid, TH), cols_have_period(Grid, TW).

gti_extract_tile(Grid, TH, TW, Tile):
  Tile = subgrid(Grid, 0, TH-1, 0, TW-1).

gti_tile_to_grid(Tile, H, W, Grid):
  Grid[R][C] = Tile[R mod TH][C mod TW] for all R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1.

gti_row_is_periodic(Row, P, Len):
  Len mod P = 0, Row[C] = Row[C mod P] for all C in 0..Len-1.

gti_col_is_periodic(Grid, C, P):
  H mod P = 0, col(C)[R] = col(C)[R mod P] for all R.

gti_tile_count_h(Grid, TH, Count): Count = H div TH.
gti_tile_count_w(Grid, TW, Count): Count = W div TW.

gti_matches_tile(Grid, Tile, R0, C0):
  subgrid(Grid, R0, R0+TH-1, C0, C0+TW-1) = Tile.

gti_tile_offset(TH, TW, R, C, TileR-TileC):
  TileR = R mod TH, TileC = C mod TW.

gti_all_tiles(Grid, TH, TW, Tiles):
  Tiles = [subgrid(TR*TH, TW*TC) | TR in 0..NH-1, TC in 0..NW-1].

gti_crop_to_tile(Grid, Tile):
  Tile = extract_tile(Grid, h_period(Grid), w_period(Grid)).

Part 236 - Work Package 246: gridmark Pseudocode

gmk_mark_cell(Grid, R, C, Mk, Marked): Marked = Grid with Grid[R][C] = Mk.
gmk_mark_cells(Grid, Cells, Mk, Marked): Marked = Grid with [R-C in Cells] -> Mk.
gmk_mark_row(Grid, R, Mk, Marked): Marked[R] = [Mk * W].
gmk_mark_col(Grid, C, Mk, Marked): Marked[R][C] = Mk for all R.
gmk_mark_rect(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Mk, Marked): Marked[R][C] = Mk for R in [R0,R1], C in [C0,C1].
gmk_mark_border(Grid, Mk, Marked): mark row 0, row H-1, col 0, col W-1.
gmk_mark_diagonal(Grid, Mk, Marked): mark (R,R) for R in 0..min(H,W)-1.
gmk_mark_anti_diagonal(Grid, Mk, Marked): mark (R,W-1-R) for R where W-1-R in [0,W).
