gmk_mark_corners(Grid, Mk, Marked): mark (0,0),(0,W-1),(H-1,0),(H-1,W-1).
gmk_mark_cross(Grid, Mk, Marked): mark row H//2 and col W//2.
gmk_marked_cells(Grid, Mk, Cells): Cells = [(R,C) | Grid[R][C] = Mk], row-major.
gmk_is_marked(Grid, R, C, Mk): Grid[R][C] = Mk.
gmk_mark_checkerboard(Grid, Mk, Marked): mark (R,C) where (R+C) mod 2 = 0.
gmk_erase(Grid, Mk, Bg, Erased): replace all Mk with Bg.

Part 237 - Work Package 247: gridcrop Pseudocode

gcr_bbox(Grid, Bg, R0-C0-R1-C1):
  Cells = [(R,C) | Grid[R][C] != Bg].
  R0 = min(R in Cells), R1 = max(R in Cells).
  C0 = min(C in Cells), C1 = max(C in Cells).

gcr_crop_bbox(Grid, Bg, Cropped): Cropped = Grid[R0..R1][C0..C1] from bbox.
gcr_trim(Grid, Bg, Trimmed): same as gcr_crop_bbox.
gcr_trim_rows(Grid, Bg, Trimmed): Grid[R0..R1][0..W-1] using bbox row range only.
gcr_trim_cols(Grid, Bg, Trimmed): Grid[0..H-1][C0..C1] using bbox col range only.
gcr_crop(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Cropped): sub-grid rows R0..R1, cols C0..C1.
gcr_pad_to(Grid, Bg, TH, TW, Padded):
  AddW = max(0, TW-W), AddH = max(0, TH-H).
  each row extended right by AddW Bg cells; AddH Bg rows appended at bottom.
gcr_center_in(Grid, Bg, TH, TW, Centered):
  TopPad = (TH-H)//2, LeftPad = (TW-W)//2.
  frame = TH*TW Bg grid; content placed at (TopPad, LeftPad).
gcr_add_border(Grid, N, Color, Bordered): N Color rows/cols on all four sides.
gcr_remove_border(Grid, N, _, Inner): crop away N rows/cols from all four sides.
gcr_expand_down(Grid, N, Color, Expanded): append N Color rows at bottom.
gcr_expand_right(Grid, N, Color, Expanded): append N Color cols on right.
gcr_content_h(Grid, Bg, H): H = R1 - R0 + 1 from bbox.
gcr_content_w(Grid, Bg, W): W = C1 - C0 + 1 from bbox.

Part 238 - Work Package 248: gridpatch Pseudocode

gpt_extract(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Patch): Patch = Grid[R0..R1][C0..C1].
gpt_place(Grid, Patch, R0, C0, Result): Result[R0+PR][C0+PC] = Patch[PR][PC] for all PR,PC.
gpt_overlay(Grid, Patch, R0, C0, Transp, Result):
  if Patch[PR][PC] = Transp: keep Grid cell; else overwrite with Patch cell.
gpt_match_at(Grid, Patch, R0, C0): no (PR,PC) where Grid[R0+PR][C0+PC] != Patch[PR][PC].
gpt_find_all(Grid, Patch, Positions): Positions = [R0-C0 | gpt_match_at succeeds].
gpt_count(Grid, Patch, N): N = |gpt_find_all(Grid, Patch)|.
gpt_replace_first(Grid, Old, New, Result): find first match, place New there.
gpt_scatter(Grid, Patch, [], Grid).
gpt_scatter(Grid, Patch, [R0-C0|Rest], Result):
  gpt_place(Grid, Patch, R0, C0, G2), gpt_scatter(G2, Patch, Rest, Result).
gpt_tile_fill(Patch, H, W, Grid): Grid[R][C] = Patch[R mod PH][C mod PW].
gpt_h(Patch, H): H = length(Patch).
gpt_w(Patch, W): W = length(Patch[0]).
gpt_size(Patch, H, W): H = length(Patch), W = length(Patch[0]).
gpt_eq(P1, P2): P1 = P2.
gpt_inpaint(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Color, Result):
  Result[R][C] = Color if R in [R0,R1] and C in [C0,C1]; else Grid[R][C].

Part 239 - Work Package 249: gridscan Pseudocode

gsn_scan_row(Grid, R, Bg, CVPairs): CVPairs = [(C,V) | Grid[R][C] != Bg].
gsn_scan_col(Grid, C, Bg, RVPairs): RVPairs = [(R,V) | Grid[R][C] != Bg].
gsn_first_right(Grid, R, C0, Bg, C-V): first C > C0 s.t. Grid[R][C] != Bg; cut.
gsn_first_left(Grid, R, C0, Bg, C-V): last C < C0 s.t. Grid[R][C] != Bg.
gsn_first_down(Grid, R0, C, Bg, R-V): first R > R0 s.t. Grid[R][C] != Bg; cut.
gsn_first_up(Grid, R0, C, Bg, R-V): last R < R0 s.t. Grid[R][C] != Bg.
gsn_dist_right(Grid, R, C0, Bg, D): D = C_hit - C0.
gsn_dist_left(Grid, R, C0, Bg, D): D = C0 - C_hit.
gsn_dist_down(Grid, R0, C, Bg, D): D = R_hit - R0.
gsn_dist_up(Grid, R0, C, Bg, D): D = R0 - R_hit.
gsn_blocked_right(Grid, R, C0, Bg): gsn_first_right succeeds.
gsn_blocked_left(Grid, R, C0, Bg): gsn_first_left succeeds.
gsn_blocked_down(Grid, R0, C, Bg): gsn_first_down succeeds.
gsn_blocked_up(Grid, R0, C, Bg): gsn_first_up succeeds.

Part 240 - Work Package 250: gridwave Pseudocode

gwv_step(Grid, Bg, Stepped):
  For each cell (R,C): if non-Bg, keep; else collect non-Bg neighbor colors Nbrs.
    If Nbrs=[]: stay Bg. If list_to_set(Nbrs)=[C]: take C. Else (conflict): stay Bg.
gwv_fill(Grid, Bg, Filled): apply gwv_step until fixed point (Stepped = Grid).
gwv_fill_n(Grid, N, Bg, Result): apply gwv_step N times.
gwv_frontier(Grid, Bg, Cells): Cells = [R-C | Grid[R][C]=Bg, any 4-nbr != Bg].
gwv_color_frontier(Grid, Bg, Color, Cells): Cells = [R-C | Grid[R][C]=Bg, any 4-nbr = Color].
gwv_equidistant_front(Grid, Bg, Cells): Cells = [R-C | Grid[R][C]=Bg, |{non-Bg nbr colors}| >= 2].
gwv_color_expand(Grid, Color, Bg, Expanded):
  For each cell (R,C): if non-Bg keep; else if any 4-nbr = Color then Color; else Bg.
gwv_color_expand_n(Grid, Color, N, Bg, Result): apply gwv_color_expand N times.
gwv_shadow_right(Grid, Bg, Shad, Shadow): per row, state machine; after first non-Bg,
  subsequent Bg cells -> Shad. Non-Bg cells keep value and reset state.
gwv_shadow_left(Grid, Bg, Shad, Shadow): reverse each row, shadow_right, reverse back.
gwv_shadow_down(Grid, Bg, Shad, Shadow): transpose, shadow_right, transpose back.
gwv_shadow_up(Grid, Bg, Shad, Shadow): transpose, shadow_left, transpose back.
gwv_contract(Grid, Bg, Contracted):
  For each non-Bg cell (R,C): if any in-bounds 4-nbr = Bg then Bg; else keep.
gwv_contract_n(Grid, N, Bg, Result): apply gwv_contract N times.

Part 241 - Work Package 251: gridshift Pseudocode

gsh_shift_right(Grid, N, Bg, Result): per row: Pad(N,Bg) ++ Take(Row, W-N).
gsh_shift_left(Grid, N, Bg, Result): per row: Drop(Row, N) ++ Pad(N,Bg).
gsh_shift_down(Grid, N, Bg, Result): Pad(N, BgRow) ++ Take(Grid, H-N rows).
gsh_shift_up(Grid, N, Bg, Result): Drop(Grid, N rows) ++ Pad(N, BgRow).
gsh_roll_right(Grid, N, Result): per row: last (N mod W) cells ++ first (W - N mod W) cells.
gsh_roll_left(Grid, N, Result): per row: roll_right by (W - N mod W) mod W.
gsh_roll_down(Grid, N, Result): roll the list of rows right by N mod H.
gsh_roll_up(Grid, N, Result): roll_down by (H - N mod H) mod H.
gsh_roll_row(Grid, R, N, Result): roll row R right by N; other rows unchanged.
gsh_roll_col(Grid, C, N, Result): transpose, roll_row C, transpose back.
gsh_shift_color(Grid, Color, DR, DC, Bg, Result):
  Result[R][C] = Color if Grid[R-DR][C-DC] = Color; else keep if Grid[R][C] != Color; else Bg.
gsh_offset(Grid, DR, DC, Bg, Result): Result[R][C] = Grid[R-DR][C-DC] if in bounds; else Bg.
gsh_shift_row(Grid, R, N, Bg, Result): shift row R by N (right if N>0, left if N<0); others unchanged.
gsh_shift_col(Grid, C, N, Bg, Result): transpose, shift_row C by N, transpose back.

Part 242 - Work Package 252: gridmap Pseudocode

gmp_remap(Grid, Mapping, Result):
  For each cell V: if (V-V2 in Mapping) then V2; else V.
gmp_swap(Grid, C1, C2, Result): gmp_remap(Grid, [C1-C2, C2-C1], Result).
gmp_replace(Grid, From, To, Result): gmp_remap(Grid, [From-To], Result).
gmp_merge(Grid, Colors, To, Result): Mapping = [(C-To) | C in Colors], gmp_remap.
gmp_normalize(Grid, Bg, Normalized):
  AllColors = [V | V in Grid, V != Bg]; Palette = unique_ordered(AllColors).
  Mapping = [(Palette[i] - i) | i in 1..|Palette|]; gmp_remap.
gmp_palette(Grid, Bg, Palette): Palette = unique_ordered([V | V in Grid, V != Bg]).
gmp_recolor_fg(Grid, Bg, Fg, Result): each cell: if V=Bg then Bg; else Fg.
gmp_mask_color(Grid, Color, Bg, Result): each cell: if V=Color then Color; else Bg.
gmp_invert(Grid, Palette, Result):
  N = |Palette|; Mapping = [(P[i] - P[N+1-i]) | i in 1..N]; gmp_remap.
gmp_cycle(Grid, Palette, N, Result):
  M = |Palette|; Mapping = [(P[i] - P[(i+N-1 mod M)+1]) | i in 1..M]; gmp_remap.
gmp_build_map(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, Mapping):
  AllPairs = [(V1-V2) | Grid1[R][C]=V1, Grid2[R][C]=V2, V1!=Bg, V2!=Bg, V1!=V2].
  Mapping = unique_ordered(AllPairs).
gmp_invert_map(Map, InvMap): InvMap = [(To-From) | (From-To) in Map].
gmp_compose_maps(Map1, Map2, Composed): Composed = [(From-To) | (From-Mid) in Map1, (Mid-To) in Map2].
gmp_map_count(Grid, Mapping, Count): Count = |[V | V in Grid, (V-_) in Mapping]|.

Part 243 - Work Package 253: gridrefl Pseudocode

grf_flip_h(Grid, Flipped): Flipped[R] = reverse(Grid[R]) for each row R.
grf_flip_v(Grid, Flipped): Flipped = reverse(Grid rows).
grf_rot90(Grid, Rotated): T = transpose(Grid); Rotated = flip_h(T).
grf_rot180(Grid, Rotated): V = flip_v(Grid); Rotated = flip_h(V).
grf_rot270(Grid, Rotated): FH = flip_h(Grid); Rotated = transpose(FH).
grf_transpose(Grid, Transposed): Transposed[R][C] = Grid[C][R].
grf_antidiag(Grid, AntiDiag): R180 = rot180(Grid); AntiDiag = transpose(R180).
  AntiDiag[R][C] = Grid[N-1-C][N-1-R] for square NxN grids.
grf_is_sym_h(Grid): flip_h(Grid) = Grid.
grf_is_sym_v(Grid): flip_v(Grid) = Grid.
grf_is_sym_d(Grid): transpose(Grid) = Grid.
grf_is_sym_a(Grid): antidiag(Grid) = Grid.
grf_sym_axes(Grid, Axes): Axes = [A | A in {h,v,d,a}, is_sym_A(Grid)].
grf_make_sym_h(Grid, Bg, Sym): Sym[R][C] = merge(Grid[R][C], Grid[R][W-1-C], Bg).
  merge(V1, V2, Bg) = V1 if V1!=Bg; V2 if V2!=Bg; else Bg.
grf_make_sym_v(Grid, Bg, Sym): Sym[R][C] = merge(Grid[R][C], Grid[H-1-R][C], Bg).

Part 244 - Work Package 254: gridlogic Pseudocode

ggl_and(G1, G2, Bg, R): R[r][c] = G1[r][c] if G1[r][c]!=Bg and G2[r][c]!=Bg; else Bg.
ggl_or(G1, G2, Bg, R): R[r][c] = G1 if G1!=Bg; else G2 if G2!=Bg; else Bg.
ggl_xor(G1, G2, Bg, R): R[r][c] = non-Bg value if exactly one of G1,G2 is non-Bg; else Bg.
ggl_not(Grid, Bg, Fg, R): R[r][c] = Fg if Grid[r][c]=Bg; else Bg.
ggl_subtract(G1, G2, Bg, R): R[r][c] = G1 if G1!=Bg and G2=Bg; else Bg.
ggl_common(G1, G2, Bg, R): R[r][c] = G1 if G1=G2 and G1!=Bg; else Bg.
ggl_differ(G1, G2, Bg, R): R[r][c] = G1 if G1!=Bg and G2!=Bg and G1!=G2; else Bg.
ggl_any(Grids, Bg, R): R[r][c] = first non-Bg value across Grids; else Bg. (fold or left-to-right)
ggl_all(Grids, Bg, R): R[r][c] = non-Bg value V if all grids agree G[r][c]=V; else Bg.
ggl_majority(Grids, Bg, R): R[r][c] = most frequent non-Bg value if count > |Grids|/2; else Bg.
ggl_unanimous(Grids, Bg, R): R[r][c] = V if all grids agree G[r][c]=V (any value); else Bg.
ggl_mask(Grid, Mask, MC, Bg, R): R[r][c] = Grid[r][c] if Mask[r][c]=MC; else Bg.
ggl_if(Cond, CC, Then, Else, R): R[r][c] = Then[r][c] if Cond[r][c]=CC; else Else[r][c].
ggl_filter(Grid, Colors, Bg, R): R[r][c] = Grid[r][c] if Grid[r][c] in Colors; else Bg.

Part 245 - WP-255: gridchain (gch_*, Layer 234)

gch_pairs(Grids, Pairs): if |Grids|>=2 then Pairs=[findall [G_i,G_{i+1}] for i in 0..N-2]; else Pairs=[].
gch_window(Grids, W, Windows): if W<=N then Windows=findall sublist(Grids,i,W) for i in 0..N-W; else [].
gch_zip([], _, []).  gch_zip(_, [], []).  gch_zip([G1|T1],[G2|T2],[[G1,G2]|R]) :- gch_zip(T1,T2,R).
gch_take(Grids, N, Taken): N2=min(N,|Grids|); length(Taken,N2); append(Taken,_,Grids).
gch_drop(Grids, N, Rest): N2=min(N,|Grids|); length(Prefix,N2); append(Prefix,Rest,Grids).
gch_nth(Grids, N, G): nth0(N, Grids, G).
gch_all_same([]). gch_all_same([_]). gch_all_same([G,G|R]) :- gch_all_same([G|R]).
gch_dedup(Grids, Unique): accumulator Seen; skip if member(H,Seen); else prepend H and recurse.
gch_cycle(Grid, N, Seq): Seq = findall(Grid, between(1,N,_), Seq).
gch_interleave([],_,[]). gch_interleave(_,[],[]). gch_interleave([G1|T1],[G2|T2],[G1,G2|R]).
gch_split_at(Grids, N, Before, After): length(Before,N); append(Before,After,Grids).
gch_reverse(Grids, Rev): reverse(Grids, Rev).
gch_diff_counts(Grids, _Bg, Counts): gch_pairs(Grids,Pairs); Counts=findall N per pair using cell-diff recursion.
gch_changes_mask([G],Bg,_,Mask): all-Bg mask same size as G.
gch_changes_mask([First|Rest],Bg,MC,Mask): last([First|Rest],Last); diff_mask_rows_(First,Last,Bg,MC,Mask).

Part 246 - WP-256: gridblend (gbld_*, Layer 235)

gbld_overlay(Top, Bottom, Bg, R): R[r][c] = Top[r][c] if /=Bg; else Bottom[r][c].
gbld_underlay(Top, Bottom, Bg, R): R[r][c] = Bottom[r][c] if /=Bg; else Top[r][c].
gbld_stencil(Source, Stencil, SC, R): R[r][c] = Source[r][c] if Stencil[r][c]=SC; else SC.
gbld_priority([G], _, G). gbld_priority([G1|Rest], Bg, R) :- priority(Rest,Bg,RR), overlay(G1,RR,Bg,R).
gbld_checker_blend(G1,G2,_Bg,Par,R): R[r][c] = G1[r][c] if (r+c) mod 2 = Par; else G2[r][c].
gbld_stripe_blend(G1,G2,Bg,SW,R): row r uses G1 on G2 if (r//SW) mod 2 = 0; else G2 on G1.
gbld_threshold_replace(Grid,T,RC,Bg,R): for each row: if count(non-bg)>=T replace non-bg with RC; else identity.
gbld_merge_many([G],_,G). gbld_merge_many([G1|Rest],Bg,R) :- merge_many(Rest,Bg,RR), overlay(Last,RR,Bg,R) where Last=last(Rest).
gbld_dominant(Grids,Bg,R): R[r][c] = mode of non-bg values across grids at (r,c); else Bg.
gbld_composite(Grids,Bg,overlay,R) :- gbld_priority(Grids,Bg,R).
gbld_composite(Grids,Bg,underlay,R) :- gbld_merge_many(Grids,Bg,R).
gbld_composite(Grids,Bg,dominant,R) :- gbld_dominant(Grids,Bg,R).

Part 247 - WP-257: gridextract (gxt_*, Layer 236)

gxt_nonbg_cells(Grid,Bg,Cells): Cells=[r(R,C,V) | R in 0..H-1, C in 0..W-1, Grid[R][C]/=Bg].
gxt_color_cells(Grid,Color,Cells): Cells=[r(R,C,Color) | Grid[R][C]=Color].
gxt_bbox(Grid,Bg,bb(MinR,MinC,MaxR,MaxC),Cells): Cells=gxt_nonbg_cells; Cells/=[]; bbox from min/max of R,C.
gxt_crop_bbox(Grid,_Bg,bb(R1,C1,R2,C2),Crop,off(R1,C1)): extract rows R1..R2, cols C1..C2.
gxt_object_at(Grid,R,C,_Bg,BBox): BFS flood fill from (R,C) with color Grid[R][C]; bbox of reachable cells.
gxt_all_colors(Grid,Bg,Colors): sorted unique non-bg values in Grid.
gxt_color_count(Grid,Color,_Bg,Count): count of Color occurrences in Grid.
gxt_largest_color(Grid,Bg,Color): non-bg color with highest count; last of msort(count-color pairs).
gxt_smallest_color(Grid,Bg,Color): non-bg color with lowest count; first of msort(count-color pairs).
gxt_centered_crop(Grid,Bg,CropH,CropW,Crop): centroid of non-bg cells → clamped crop window.
gxt_row_cells(Grid,R,Bg,Cells): non-bg cells in row R as r(R,C,V) triples.
gxt_col_cells(Grid,C,Bg,Cells): non-bg cells in column C as r(R,C,V) triples.
gxt_region_count(Grid,Color,_Bg,Count): count 4-connected regions; BFS subtract loop.
gxt_registry(Grid,Bg,Registry): [obj(Color,Count,BBox)] for each unique non-bg color; sorted by color.

Part 248 - WP-258: gridgrav (gra_*, Layer 237)

gra_col_nonbg(Grid,Col,Bg,Vals): Vals=[V | R in 0..H-1, Grid[R][Col]=V, V/=Bg].
gra_row_nonbg(Grid,Row,Bg,Vals): Vals=[V | C in 0..W-1, Grid[Row][C]=V, V/=Bg].
gra_fall_down(Grid,Bg,Result): per column, settle_segment(ColVals,Bg,down); transpose cols to grid.
gra_fall_up(Grid,Bg,Result): per column, settle_segment(ColVals,Bg,up); transpose.
gra_fall_left(Grid,Bg,Result): per row, settle_segment(Row,Bg,left).
gra_fall_right(Grid,Bg,Result): per row, settle_segment(Row,Bg,right).
gra_fall(Grid,Bg,Dir,Result): dispatch: Dir in {down,up,left,right}.
settle_segment(Seg,Bg,down/right,S): Vals=non-bg in Seg; S=BgPad++Vals (pack to end).
settle_segment(Seg,Bg,up/left,S): Vals=non-bg in Seg; S=Vals++BgPad (pack to start).
gra_set_col_bottom(Grid,Col,Vals,Bg,R): ColVals=BgTop++Vals; replace col in grid.
gra_set_col_top(Grid,Col,Vals,Bg,R): ColVals=Vals++BgBottom; replace col in grid.
gra_set_row_left(Grid,Row,Vals,Bg,R): NewRow=Vals++BgRight; replace row in grid.
gra_set_row_right(Grid,Row,Vals,Bg,R): NewRow=BgLeft++Vals; replace row in grid.
gra_blocked_fall(Grid,Bg,Block,Dir,R): split at Block; settle each segment; reassemble.
gra_is_settled(Grid,Bg): gra_fall_down(Grid,Bg,Grid) -- result unifies with original.
gra_gravity_score(Grid,Bg,Score): Score=count(positions where Grid/=fall_down(Grid,Bg)).

Part 249 - Work Package 259: gridstamp Pack Pseudocode (gst_*, Layer 238)

WP-259-PSEUDO-001: gst_canvas(H, W, Bg, Canvas)
  Canvas := [ [Bg * W] * H ]
  -- Build H rows; each row is W copies of Bg.

WP-259-PSEUDO-002: gst_stamp(Grid, Stamp, R0, C0, Bg, Result)
  Mods := { gr(R0+SR, C0+SC, V) |
              (SR,SC,V) in cells(Stamp), V != Bg,
              R0+SR in [0,GH-1], C0+SC in [0,GW-1] }
  Result[R][C] := if gr(R,C,MV) in Mods then MV else Grid[R][C]
  -- Only non-bg stamp cells overwrite; bg stamp cells are transparent.

WP-259-PSEUDO-003: gst_stamp_all(Grid, Stamp, Positions, Bg, Result)
  Acc := Grid
  for each r(R,C) in Positions:
    Acc := gst_stamp(Acc, Stamp, R, C, Bg)
  Result := Acc

WP-259-PSEUDO-004: gst_scatter(Grid, Color, Positions, Bg, Result)
  Result[R][C] := if r(R,C) in Positions then Color else Grid[R][C]
  -- Unconditionally overwrites (including Bg cells).

WP-259-PSEUDO-005: gst_find_matches(Grid, Pattern, Bg, Matches)
  Matches := { r(R,C) | R in [0, GH-PH], C in [0, GW-PW],
                 forall (PR,PC): Pattern[PR][PC] = Grid[R+PR][C+PC] }
  -- If Pattern does not fit in Grid, Matches := [].

WP-259-PSEUDO-006: gst_stamp_count(Grid, Pattern, Bg, Count)
  Count := |gst_find_matches(Grid, Pattern, Bg)|

WP-259-PSEUDO-007: gst_pad(Grid, H, W, Bg, Result)
  ExtraCols := max(0, W - GW)
  ExtraRows := max(0, H - GH)
  PaddedRows := [ Row ++ [Bg * ExtraCols] | Row in Grid ]
  Result := PaddedRows ++ [ [Bg * max(W,GW)] * ExtraRows ]

WP-259-PSEUDO-008: gst_unpad(Grid, Bg, Result)
  Rs := { R | exists C: Grid[R][C] != Bg }
  Cs := { C | exists R: Grid[R][C] != Bg }
  if Rs = {} then Result := []
  else Result := Grid[minRs..maxRs][minCs..maxCs]

WP-259-PSEUDO-009: gst_replicate_h(Grid, N, Bg, Result)
  Result[R] := Row * N  -- row R of Grid repeated N times end-to-end.

WP-259-PSEUDO-010: gst_replicate_v(Grid, N, Bg, Result)
  Result := Grid * N  -- all Grid rows stacked N times.

WP-259-PSEUDO-011: gst_border(Grid, BorderColor, T, Bg, Result)
  NewW := GW + 2*T
  TopRows := [ [BorderColor * NewW] * T ]
  MiddleRows := [ [BorderColor*T] ++ GRow ++ [BorderColor*T] | GRow in Grid ]
  BottomRows := [ [BorderColor * NewW] * T ]
  Result := TopRows ++ MiddleRows ++ BottomRows

WP-259-PSEUDO-012: gst_center(Grid, H, W, Bg, Result)
  R0 := (H - GH) // 2
  C0 := (W - GW) // 2
  Result[R][C] :=
    let SR := R - R0, SC := C - C0 in
    if SR in [0,GH-1] and SC in [0,GW-1] then Grid[SR][SC] else Bg

WP-259-PSEUDO-013: gst_extract(Grid, R0, C0, H, W, Subgrid)
  Subgrid := Grid[R0..R0+H-1][C0..C0+W-1]

WP-259-PSEUDO-014: gst_replace(Grid, R0, C0, Patch, Result)
  Result[R][C] :=
    let PR := R - R0, PC := C - C0 in
    if PR in [0,PH-1] and PC in [0,PW-1] then Patch[PR][PC] else Grid[R][C]
  -- Opaque: all Patch cells written regardless of color.

Part 250 - Work Package 260: gridalign Pack Pseudocode (gal_*, Layer 239)

WP-260-PSEUDO-001: gal_center_of_mass(Grid, Bg, r(R,C))
  S := { (r,c) | Grid[r][c] != Bg }
  R := floor(mean({ r | (r,c) in S }))
  C := floor(mean({ c | (r,c) in S }))

WP-260-PSEUDO-002: gal_nonbg_bbox(Grid, Bg, BBox)
  S := { (r,c) | Grid[r][c] != Bg }
  if S = {} then BBox := none
  else BBox := r0(min_r(S), min_c(S), max_r(S), max_c(S))

WP-260-PSEUDO-003: gal_bbox_center(Grid, Bg, Center)
  BBox := gal_nonbg_bbox(Grid, Bg)
  if BBox = none then Center := none
  else Center := r((R0+R1)//2, (C0+C1)//2)

WP-260-PSEUDO-004: gal_translate(Grid, DR, DC, Bg, Result)
  Result[r][c] :=
    let sr := r - DR, sc := c - DC in
    if sr in [0, H-1] and sc in [0, W-1] and Grid[sr][sc] != Bg
    then Grid[sr][sc] else Bg

WP-260-PSEUDO-005: gal_overlap_count(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, Count)
  Count := |{ (r,c) | Grid1[r][c] != Bg and Grid2[r][c] != Bg }|

WP-260-PSEUDO-006: gal_overlap_score(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, Score)
  N1 := |{ (r,c) | Grid1[r][c] != Bg }|
  if N1 = 0 then Score := 0.0
  else Score := gal_overlap_count(Grid1, Grid2) / N1

WP-260-PSEUDO-007: gal_iou(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, IoU)
  Inter := |{ (r,c) | Grid1[r][c] != Bg and Grid2[r][c] != Bg }|
  Union := |{ (r,c) | Grid1[r][c] != Bg or Grid2[r][c] != Bg }|
  -- Use negation \+(V1=Bg, V2=Bg) to avoid double-counting disjunction.
  if Union = 0 then IoU := 0.0 else IoU := Inter / Union

WP-260-PSEUDO-008: gal_find_offset(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, SearchR, o(DR,DC))
  S1 := { (r,c) | Grid1[r][c] != Bg }
  S2 := { (r,c) | Grid2[r][c] != Bg }
  BestOv := 0, BestDR := 0, BestDC := 0
  for each (dr,dc) in [-SearchR,SearchR]^2:
    Ov := |{ (r,c) in S2 | (r+dr, c+dc) in S1 }|
    if Ov > BestOv or (Ov = BestOv and |dr|+|dc| < |BestDR|+|BestDC|):
      BestOv := Ov, BestDR := dr, BestDC := dc
  (DR, DC) := (BestDR, BestDC)

WP-260-PSEUDO-009: gal_align_centers(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, Aligned)
  r(R1,C1) := gal_center_of_mass(Grid1, Bg)
  r(R2,C2) := gal_center_of_mass(Grid2, Bg)
  Aligned := gal_translate(Grid2, R1-R2, C1-C2, Bg)
  -- If either grid has no non-bg cells, Aligned := Grid2.

WP-260-PSEUDO-010: gal_align_bbox_centers(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, Aligned)
  r(R1,C1) := gal_bbox_center(Grid1, Bg)
  r(R2,C2) := gal_bbox_center(Grid2, Bg)
  Aligned := gal_translate(Grid2, R1-R2, C1-C2, Bg)

WP-260-PSEUDO-011: gal_nonbg_offset(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, o(DR,DC))
  r(R1,C1) := gal_center_of_mass(Grid1, Bg)
  r(R2,C2) := gal_center_of_mass(Grid2, Bg)
  (DR, DC) := (R2-R1, C2-C1)

WP-260-PSEUDO-012: gal_place_at(Canvas, Grid2, R0, C0, Bg, Result)
  Mods := { (R0+sr, C0+sc, v) | Grid2[sr][sc] = v != Bg, in bounds }
  Result[r][c] := if (r,c,mv) in Mods then mv else Canvas[r][c]

WP-260-PSEUDO-013: gal_anchor_to(Canvas, Grid2, PR, PC, QR, QC, Bg, Result)
  R0 := QR - PR, C0 := QC - PC
  Result := gal_place_at(Canvas, Grid2, R0, C0, Bg)

WP-260-PSEUDO-014: gal_match_any_offset(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, Offsets)
  S1 := { (r,c) | Grid1[r][c] != Bg }
  S2 := { (r,c) | Grid2[r][c] != Bg }
  Offsets := deduplicate { o(dr,dc) | (r2,c2) in S2, (r2+dr, c2+dc) in S1 }


Part 251: Work Package 261 - gridcolorop Pack (gco_*, Layer 240)

WP-261-PSEUDO-001: gco_color_counts(Grid, Bg, Counts)
  Colors := { V | Grid[r][c] = V, V != Bg }
  Distinct := set(Colors)
  Pairs := [ cc(V, count(V, Colors)) | V in Distinct ]
  Counts := sort_by_count_desc(Pairs)

WP-261-PSEUDO-002: gco_distinct_colors(Grid, Bg, Colors)
  Counts := gco_color_counts(Grid, Bg)
  Colors := [ V | cc(V,_) in Counts ]

WP-261-PSEUDO-003: gco_nth_color(Grid, Bg, N, Color)
  Colors := gco_distinct_colors(Grid, Bg)
  Color := Colors[N]

WP-261-PSEUDO-004: gco_count_distinct(Grid, Bg, Count)
  Colors := gco_distinct_colors(Grid, Bg)
  Count := length(Colors)

WP-261-PSEUDO-005: gco_swap(Grid, C1, C2, Bg, Result)
  Result[r][c] := if Grid[r][c]=C1 then C2
                  else if Grid[r][c]=C2 then C1
                  else Grid[r][c]

WP-261-PSEUDO-006: gco_replace(Grid, Old, New, Bg, Result)
  Result[r][c] := if Grid[r][c]=Old then New else Grid[r][c]

WP-261-PSEUDO-007: gco_apply_map(Grid, Map, Bg, Result)
  Result[r][c] := if (Grid[r][c] -> MV) in Map then MV else Grid[r][c]

WP-261-PSEUDO-008: gco_keep_only(Grid, Color, Bg, Result)
  Result[r][c] := if Grid[r][c]=Color then Color else Bg

WP-261-PSEUDO-009: gco_remove_color(Grid, Color, Bg, Result)
  Result[r][c] := if Grid[r][c]=Color then Bg else Grid[r][c]

WP-261-PSEUDO-010: gco_cycle(Grid, Palette, N, Bg, Result)
  PLen := length(Palette)
  Result[r][c] := if Palette[Idx]=Grid[r][c] then
                    Palette[((Idx+N) mod PLen + PLen) mod PLen]
                  else Grid[r][c]

WP-261-PSEUDO-011: gco_rank_grid(Grid, Bg, Result)
  ByFreq := gco_distinct_colors(Grid, Bg)
  Result[r][c] := if Grid[r][c]=Bg then Bg else index_of(ByFreq, Grid[r][c])

WP-261-PSEUDO-012: gco_apply_palette(Grid, Bg, Palette, Result)
  ByFreq := gco_distinct_colors(Grid, Bg)
  Map := [ ByFreq[K] -> Palette[K] | K in 0..min(|Palette|,|ByFreq|)-1 ]
  Result := gco_apply_map(Grid, Map, Bg)

WP-261-PSEUDO-013: gco_most_least(Grid, Bg, Most, Least)
  Counts := gco_color_counts(Grid, Bg)  (non-empty)
  Most := first(Counts).color
  Least := last(Counts).color

WP-261-PSEUDO-014: gco_invert(Grid, Bg, FgColor, Result)
  Result[r][c] := if Grid[r][c]=Bg then FgColor else Bg

Private helper: gco_sort_by_count_desc_(Pairs, Sorted)
  Keyed := [ neg(Neg, cc(V,N)) | cc(V,N) in Pairs, Neg is -N ]
  KeyedSorted := msort(Keyed)
  Sorted := [ cc(V,N) | neg(_,cc(V,N)) in KeyedSorted ]
  Note: Neg is -N evaluates arithmetic; -N as a term creates compound -(N)
  which compares by functor and arity, not numeric value.


Part 252: Work Package 262 - gridresize Pack (grs_*, Layer 241)

WP-262-PSEUDO-001: grs_scale_up(Grid, F, Result)
  H, W := dims(Grid)
  NewH := H*F, NewW := W*F
  Result[r][c] := Grid[r // F][c // F]  for r in [0,NewH), c in [0,NewW)

WP-262-PSEUDO-002: grs_scale_down(Grid, F, Bg, Result)
  NewH := H // F, NewW := W // F
  if NewH=0 or NewW=0: Result := []
  else: Result[r][c] := Grid[r*F][c*F]  for r in [0,NewH), c in [0,NewW)

WP-262-PSEUDO-003: grs_scale_down_mode(Grid, F, Bg, Result)
  NewH := H // F, NewW := W // F
  if NewH=0 or NewW=0: Result := []
  else: Block(r,c) := { Grid[sr][sc] | sr in [r*F, r*F+F-1], sc in [c*F, c*F+F-1], in bounds }
        Result[r][c] := mode(Block(r,c))

WP-262-PSEUDO-004: grs_double(Grid, Result)
  Result := grs_scale_up(Grid, 2)

WP-262-PSEUDO-005: grs_halve(Grid, Bg, Result)
  Result := grs_scale_down(Grid, 2, Bg)

WP-262-PSEUDO-006: grs_resize(Grid, NewH, NewW, Bg, Result)
  if NewH=0 or NewW=0: Result := []
  elif H=0 or W=0: Result := NewH x NewW canvas of Bg
  else: Result[r][c] := Grid[floor(r*H/NewH)][floor(c*W/NewW)]

WP-262-PSEUDO-007: grs_tile_to(Grid, H, W, Result)
  H0, W0 := dims(Grid)
  if H=0 or W=0 or H0=0 or W0=0: Result := []
  else: Result[r][c] := Grid[r mod H0][c mod W0]

WP-262-PSEUDO-008: grs_crop(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1, Result)
  ClR0 := max(R0,0), ClC0 := max(C0,0)
  ClR1 := min(R1, H-1), ClC1 := min(C1, W-1)
  if ClR0 > ClR1 or ClC0 > ClC1: Result := []
  else: Result[r][c] := Grid[ClR0+r][ClC0+c]

WP-262-PSEUDO-009: grs_border_crop(Grid, N, Bg, Result)
  R0:=N, C0:=N, R1:=H-N-1, C1:=W-N-1
  if R1 >= R0 and C1 >= C0: Result := grs_crop(Grid, R0, C0, R1, C1)
  else: Result := []

WP-262-PSEUDO-010: grs_fit_in(Grid, H, W, Bg, Result)
  H0, W0 := dims(Grid)
  if H0=0 or W0=0: Result := grs_embed_in(Grid, H, W, Bg)
  else:
    Scale := min(H/H0, W/W0)
    NewH := max(1, round(H0*Scale)), NewW := max(1, round(W0*Scale))
    Scaled := grs_resize(Grid, NewH, NewW, Bg)
    Result := grs_embed_in(Scaled, H, W, Bg)

WP-262-PSEUDO-011: grs_embed_in(Grid, H, W, Bg, Result)
  H0, W0 := dims(Grid)
  OffR := (H-H0) // 2, OffC := (W-W0) // 2
  Result[r][c] := if (r-OffR) in [0,H0) and (c-OffC) in [0,W0):
                    Grid[r-OffR][c-OffC]
                  else: Bg

WP-262-PSEUDO-012: grs_grid_size(Grid, H, W)
  H, W := dims(Grid)

WP-262-PSEUDO-013: grs_aspect_ratio(Grid, H, W, Ratio)
  H, W := dims(Grid)
  Ratio := if H=0: 0.0 else W/H

WP-262-PSEUDO-014: grs_is_square(Grid)
  H, W := dims(Grid)
  succeed iff H = W

Private helper: grs_mode_(List, Mode)
  Vals := sort(List)
  Keyed := [ neg(Neg,V) | V in Vals, N := count(V,List), Neg is -N ]
  Mode := first value from msort(Keyed)
  Note: Neg is -N (arithmetic) ensures numeric sort order.


Part 253: Work Package 263 - gridobj Pack (gob_*, Layer 242)

WP-263-PSEUDO-001: gob_object_cells(Grid, R, C, Cells)
  Color := Grid[R][C]
  Cells := BFS(start={r(R,C)}, visited={r(R,C)}, match=Color)

WP-263-PSEUDO-002: gob_object_color(Grid, R, C, Color)
  Color := Grid[R][C]

WP-263-PSEUDO-003: gob_object_size(Grid, R, C, Size)
  Cells := gob_object_cells(Grid, R, C)
  Size := length(Cells)

WP-263-PSEUDO-004: gob_object_bbox(Grid, R, C, BBox)
  Cells := gob_object_cells(Grid, R, C)
  BBox := r0(min_R, min_C, max_R, max_C) over Cells

WP-263-PSEUDO-005: gob_object_mask(Grid, R, C, Bg, Mask)
  Cells := gob_object_cells(Grid, R, C); Color := Grid[R][C]
  Mask[r][c] := if r(r,c) in Cells then Color else Bg

WP-263-PSEUDO-006: gob_extract_object(Grid, R, C, Bg, Extracted)
  Cells := gob_object_cells; Color := Grid[R][C]
  r0(R0,C0,R1,C1) := bbox(Cells)
  Extracted[dr][dc] := if r(R0+dr,C0+dc) in Cells then Color else Bg

WP-263-PSEUDO-007: gob_all_objects(Grid, Bg, Objects)
  NonBg := scan all non-Bg cells in row-major order
  Objects := collect_components(NonBg, Grid, already_seen={})
  Each component: ob(Color, Cells, BBox)

WP-263-PSEUDO-008: gob_object_count(Grid, Bg, Count)
  Count := length(gob_all_objects(Grid, Bg))

WP-263-PSEUDO-009: gob_largest_object(Grid, Bg, Cells)
  Cells := cells of ob with max length in gob_all_objects
  Key for msort: neg(Neg, Cs) where Neg is -(length(Cs))

WP-263-PSEUDO-010: gob_smallest_object(Grid, Bg, Cells)
  Cells := cells of ob with min length in gob_all_objects
  Key for msort: pos(Len, Cs) where Len = length(Cs)

WP-263-PSEUDO-011: gob_flood_fill(Grid, R, C, NewColor, Result)
  Cells := gob_object_cells(Grid, R, C)
  Result[r][c] := if r(r,c) in Cells then NewColor else Grid[r][c]

WP-263-PSEUDO-012: gob_fill_enclosed(Grid, Bg, FgColor, Result)
  BorderBg := all Bg cells at row=0, row=H-1, col=0, or col=W-1
  Reachable := BFS(start=BorderBg, match=Bg)
  Result[r][c] := if Grid[r][c]=Bg and r(r,c) not in Reachable: FgColor
                  else Grid[r][c]

WP-263-PSEUDO-013: gob_remove_object(Grid, R, C, Bg, Result)
  Cells := gob_object_cells(Grid, R, C)
  Result[r][c] := if r(r,c) in Cells then Bg else Grid[r][c]

WP-263-PSEUDO-014: gob_move_object(Grid, R, C, NewR, NewC, Bg, Result)
  Cells := gob_object_cells; Color := Grid[R][C]
  r0(OldR0,OldC0,_,_) := bbox(Cells)
  DR := NewR - OldR0, DC := NewC - OldC0
  Base := gob_remove_object(Grid, R, C, Bg)
  Moved := { r(OR+DR, OC+DC, Color) | r(OR,OC) in Cells, in bounds }
  Result[r][c] := if r(r,c,Color) in Moved then Color else Base[r][c]

BFS subroutine: gob_bfs_(Frontier, Visited, Color, H, W, Grid, Result)
  if Frontier = []: Result = Visited
  else:
    [r(R,C)|Rest] = Frontier
    NewCells = { r(NR,NC) | (NR,NC) is 4-neighbor of (R,C), in bounds,
                 not in Visited, not in Rest, Grid[NR][NC]=Color }
    recurse with Frontier=Rest+NewCells, Visited=Visited+NewCells


Part 254: Work Package 264 - gridgroupby Pack (ggb_*, Layer 243)

WP-264-PSEUDO-001: ggb_group_by_color(Objects, Groups):
  Collect k(Color, Obj) pairs for all Obj in Objects where Color is Obj's color.
  msort the pairs by key.
  Collect consecutive same-key runs into grp(Color, ObjList) terms.
  Return list of grp terms.

WP-264-PSEUDO-002: ggb_group_by_size(Objects, Groups):
  Collect k(Size, Obj) pairs where Size = length(Obj.Cells).
  msort and collect runs as above. Return grp(Size, ObjList) list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-003: ggb_group_by_row(Objects, Groups):
  Collect k(R0, Obj) pairs where R0 is the top row from Obj's BBox.
  msort and collect runs. Return grp(R0, ObjList) list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-004: ggb_group_by_col(Objects, Groups):
  Collect k(C0, Obj) pairs where C0 is the left col from Obj's BBox.
  msort and collect runs. Return grp(C0, ObjList) list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-005: ggb_filter_by_color(Objects, Color, Filtered):
  Collect Obj from Objects where Obj = ob(Color,_,_). Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-006: ggb_filter_by_size(Objects, Size, Filtered):
  Collect Obj from Objects where length(Obj.Cells) = Size. Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-007: ggb_filter_larger(Objects, N, Filtered):
  Collect Obj from Objects where length(Obj.Cells) > N. Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-008: ggb_filter_smaller(Objects, N, Filtered):
  Collect Obj from Objects where length(Obj.Cells) < N. Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-009: ggb_sort_by_size_asc(Objects, Sorted):
  Collect k(Size, Obj) pairs. msort. Extract Obj in key order. Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-010: ggb_sort_by_size_desc(Objects, Sorted):
  Collect neg(Neg, Obj) pairs where Neg is -Size. msort. Extract Obj. Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-011: ggb_sort_by_row(Objects, Sorted):
  Collect k(R0, Obj) pairs. msort. Extract Obj. Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-012: ggb_sort_by_col(Objects, Sorted):
  Collect k(C0, Obj) pairs. msort. Extract Obj. Return list.

WP-264-PSEUDO-013: ggb_pair_by_color(Objects, Pairs):
  Call ggb_group_by_color to get Groups.
  For each grp(Color, [Obj1, Obj2]) (exactly two members), emit pair(Color,Obj1,Obj2).
  Return list of pairs.

WP-264-PSEUDO-014: ggb_count_per_color(Objects, Counts):
  Call ggb_group_by_color to get Groups.
  For each grp(Color, ObjList), compute N = length(ObjList).
  Collect neg(Neg, Color, N) with Neg is -N.
  msort. Extract cnt(Color, N) terms. Return list.


Part 255: Work Package 265 - gridrelation Pack (grl_*, Layer 244)

WP-265-PSEUDO-001: grl_touching(ObjA, ObjB):
  Get CellsA, CellsB. For any r(RA,CA) in CellsA and r(RB,CB) in CellsB:
  succeed if (RA=RB and |CA-CB|=1) or (CA=CB and |RA-RB|=1). Cut on first match.

WP-265-PSEUDO-002: grl_adjacent(ObjA, ObjB, N):
  Call grl_min_distance(ObjA, ObjB, D). Succeed if D =< N.

WP-265-PSEUDO-003: grl_min_distance(ObjA, ObjB, D):
  Collect Manhattan(CA, CB) for all CA in CellsA, CB in CellsB.
  D = min of that list.

WP-265-PSEUDO-004: grl_above(ObjA, ObjB):
  Get R1A from ObjA's bbox, R0B from ObjB's bbox. Succeed if R1A < R0B.

WP-265-PSEUDO-005: grl_below(ObjA, ObjB):
  Get R0A from ObjA's bbox, R1B from ObjB's bbox. Succeed if R0A > R1B.

WP-265-PSEUDO-006: grl_left_of(ObjA, ObjB):
  Get C1A from ObjA's bbox, C0B from ObjB's bbox. Succeed if C1A < C0B.

WP-265-PSEUDO-007: grl_right_of(ObjA, ObjB):
  Get C0A from ObjA's bbox, C1B from ObjB's bbox. Succeed if C0A > C1B.

WP-265-PSEUDO-008: grl_bbox_contains(ObjA, ObjB):
  Get r0(R0A,C0A,R1A,C1A) and r0(R0B,C0B,R1B,C1B).
  Succeed if R0A =< R0B, C0A =< C0B, R1A >= R1B, C1A >= C1B.

WP-265-PSEUDO-009: grl_bbox_overlap(ObjA, ObjB):
  Succeed if R0A =< R1B and R0B =< R1A and C0A =< C1B and C0B =< C1A.

WP-265-PSEUDO-010: grl_cells_overlap(ObjA, ObjB):
  For any Cell in CellsA, succeed if Cell in CellsB. Cut on first match.

WP-265-PSEUDO-011: grl_same_rows(ObjA, ObjB):
  Succeed if R0A =< R1B and R0B =< R1A.

WP-265-PSEUDO-012: grl_same_cols(ObjA, ObjB):
  Succeed if C0A =< C1B and C0B =< C1A.

WP-265-PSEUDO-013: grl_direction(ObjA, ObjB, Dir):
  CRA = R0A + R1A, CCA = C0A + C1A (doubled centroid).
  CRB = R0B + R1B, CCB = C0B + C1B.
  DR = CRB - CRA, DC = CCB - CCA.
  If DR=0 and DC=0: Dir = overlap.
  If abs(DR) >= abs(DC): Dir = below (DR>0) or above (DR<0).
  Else: Dir = right (DC>0) or left (DC<0).

WP-265-PSEUDO-014: grl_all_relations(ObjA, ObjB, Relations):
  For each (Rel-Goal) in the 10-element association list, call Goal.
  Collect Rel for each Goal that succeeds. Return list.


Part 256: Work Package 266 - gridtransform Pack (gtr_*, Layer 245)

WP-266-PSEUDO-001: gtr_color_map(GridA, GridB, Map):
  Collect cm(VA,VB) for all (R,C) pairs. Sort to dedup (sort/2).
  Fail if any cm(VA,VB1) and cm(VA,VB2) exist with VB1 \= VB2.

WP-266-PSEUDO-002: gtr_apply_color_map(Grid, Map, Result):
  For each cell V: if cm(V,NV) in Map use NV else keep V.

WP-266-PSEUDO-003: gtr_diff_cells(GridA, GridB, Cells):
  Collect r(R,C) for all positions where VA \= VB.

WP-266-PSEUDO-004: gtr_diff_count(GridA, GridB, N):
  Call gtr_diff_cells, N = length.

WP-266-PSEUDO-005: gtr_same_cells(GridA, GridB, Cells):
  Collect r(R,C) for all positions where VA = VB.

WP-266-PSEUDO-006: gtr_changed_colors(GridA, GridB, Changes):
  Collect chg(R,C,VA,VB) for all positions where VA \= VB.

WP-266-PSEUDO-007: gtr_invert_map(Map, InvMap):
  Collect cm(VB,VA) for each cm(VA,VB). Sort. Fail if non-injective.

WP-266-PSEUDO-008: gtr_compose_maps(MapAtoB, MapBtoC, MapAtoC):
  Collect cm(VA,VC) for each cm(VA,VB) in MapAtoB with matching cm(VB,VC) in MapBtoC.
  Sort.

WP-266-PSEUDO-009: gtr_is_identity_map(Map):
  Fail if any cm(VA,VB) with VA \= VB exists.

WP-266-PSEUDO-010: gtr_apply_changes(Grid, Changes, Result):
  For each cell: if chg(R,C,_,NV) in Changes use NV else keep original.

WP-266-PSEUDO-011: gtr_delta_grid(GridA, GridB, Bg, Delta):
  For each cell: if VA \= VB use VB else use Bg.

WP-266-PSEUDO-012: gtr_overlay(BaseGrid, DeltaGrid, Bg, Result):
  For each cell: if DV \= Bg use DV else use BV from BaseGrid.

WP-266-PSEUDO-013: gtr_common_grid(GridA, GridB, Bg, Common):
  For each cell: if VA = VB use VA else use Bg.

WP-266-PSEUDO-014: gtr_is_color_permutation(GridA, GridB):
  Call gtr_color_map. Fail if any two sources map to same target.


Part 257: Work Package 267 - gridobjmatch Pack (gom_*, Layer 246)

WP-267-PSEUDO-001: gom_match_color(Objs1, Objs2, Pairs):
  Base case: Objs1=[] -> Pairs=[].
  Take O1 from Objs1; get its Color.
  If gom_select_color_(Objs2, Color, O2, Objs2Rem) ->
    Pairs = [match(O1,O2)|More], recurse with Objs2Rem.
  Else recurse with Objs2 unchanged.

WP-267-PSEUDO-002: gom_match_nearest(Objs1, Objs2, Pairs):
  Base cases: Objs1=[] or Objs2=[] -> Pairs=[].
  Take O1 from Objs1.
  Call gom_find_nearest_(O1, Objs2, Best): collect D-O2 pairs by
    doubled-centroid Manhattan distance; msort, take first element.
  Remove Best from Objs2 once (gom_remove_once_).
  Pairs = [match(O1,Best)|More], recurse.

WP-267-PSEUDO-003: gom_match_size(Objs1, Objs2, Pairs):
  Same structure as gom_match_color but uses gom_select_size_.
  Size = length of Cells list.

WP-267-PSEUDO-004: gom_unmatched_a(Pairs, Objs1, Unmatched):
  Matched = findall(O1, member(match(O1,_), Pairs)).
  Unmatched = subtract(Objs1, Matched).

WP-267-PSEUDO-005: gom_unmatched_b(Pairs, Objs2, Unmatched):
  Matched = findall(O2, member(match(_,O2), Pairs)).
  Unmatched = subtract(Objs2, Matched).

WP-267-PSEUDO-006: gom_color_diff(Pairs, Same, Diff):
  Recurse over Pairs.
  For match(O1,O2): if gom_color_(O1)=gom_color_(O2) -> add to Same else to Diff.

WP-267-PSEUDO-007: gom_move_vector(match(O1,O2), mv(DR,DC)):
  gom_top_left_(O1, R1, C1); gom_top_left_(O2, R2, C2).
  DR = R2-R1, DC = C2-C1.

WP-267-PSEUDO-008: gom_move_vectors(Pairs, Vectors):
  maplist(gom_move_vector, Pairs, Vectors).

WP-267-PSEUDO-009: gom_constant_move([P|Rest], V):
  V = gom_move_vector(P).
  maplist(gom_has_vector_(V), Rest).
  Fails for empty list.

WP-267-PSEUDO-010: gom_infer_color_map(Pairs, Map):
  findall(cm(C1,C2), (member(match(O1,O2),Pairs), C1=color(O1), C2=color(O2), C1\=C2)).
  sort to dedup -> Map.

WP-267-PSEUDO-011: gom_appeared(Objs1, Objs2, Appeared):
  Cs1 = all colors in Objs1.
  include(not_in(Cs1), Objs2, Appeared).

WP-267-PSEUDO-012: gom_disappeared(Objs1, Objs2, Disappeared):
  Cs2 = all colors in Objs2.
  include(not_in(Cs2), Objs1, Disappeared).

WP-267-PSEUDO-013: gom_same_structure(Objs1, Objs2):
  msort(colors(Objs1), S1); msort(colors(Objs2), S2).
  Succeed if S1 = S2.

WP-267-PSEUDO-014: gom_count_change(Objs1, Objs2, N):
  N = length(Objs2) - length(Objs1).


Part 258: Work Package 268 - symtab Pack (st_*, Layer 247)

WP-268-PSEUDO-001: st_build_table(Pairs, SymbolTable):
  Call st_contrastive_learn(Pairs, Candidates).
  If Candidates=[]: SymbolTable=[].
  Else: st_best_table(Candidates, Pairs, SymbolTable).

WP-268-PSEUDO-002: st_identify_symbols(Pairs, Symbols):
  findall(sym(Feature, OutColor),
    (member(pair(InObjs,OutObjs), Pairs),
     member(InObj, InObjs), member(OutObj, OutObjs),
     colors differ,
     Feature from st_color_feature or st_size_feature or holes(H)).
  sort -> Symbols.

WP-268-PSEUDO-003: st_contrastive_learn([], []).
  st_contrastive_learn([Pair|Rest], Findings):
    Extract PairSet from Pair via findall over all features.
    Recurse on Rest -> RestFindings.
    include(st_entry_consistent_(RestFindings), PairSet, Findings).

WP-268-PSEUDO-004: st_apply_table(SymbolTable, InObjs, ColorMap):
  findall(cm(Color,Value),
    (member(InObj, InObjs), st_ob_color_(InObj, Color),
     member(Sym, SymbolTable), st_apply_sym_(Sym, InObj, cm(Color, Value)))).
  sort -> ColorMap.

WP-268-PSEUDO-005: st_hole_count(ob(_, Cells, r0(R0,C0,R1,C1)), N):
  BboxArea = (R1-R0+1)*(C1-C0+1). CellCount = length(Cells).
  HoleArea = BboxArea - CellCount. N = max(0, HoleArea).

WP-268-PSEUDO-006: st_lookup([sym(F,V)|_], F, V) :- cut.
  st_lookup([_|Rest], F, V) :- st_lookup(Rest, F, V).

WP-268-PSEUDO-007: st_entry_consistent(sym(F,V), Table):
  \+ (member(sym(F,V2), Table), V2 \= V).

WP-268-PSEUDO-008: st_color_feature(ob(Color,_,_), color(Color)).

WP-268-PSEUDO-009: st_size_feature(ob(_,Cells,_), size(N)) :- length(Cells, N).

WP-268-PSEUDO-010: st_position_feature(ob(_,_,r0(R0,C0,_,_)), dims(Rows,Cols), pos(Q)):
  Compute quadrant by comparing R0 to Rows/2 and C0 to Cols/2.

WP-268-PSEUDO-011: st_is_symbol(Obj, ContentObjs):
  size(Obj) < max(sizes(ContentObjs)), OR unique color not in ContentObjs.

WP-268-PSEUDO-012: st_candidate_symbols(InObjs, Candidates):
  Sort by size ascending. Take first len/4 objects. Return as Candidates.

WP-268-PSEUDO-013: st_score_table(SymbolTable, Pairs, Score):
  For each pair: apply table -> ColorMap. Verify ColorMap transforms InObjs to OutObjs.
  Score = count of verified pairs.

WP-268-PSEUDO-014: st_best_table(Tables, Pairs, Best):
  Score each table. msort -> take last (highest). Return Best.


Part 259: Work Package 269 - invariant Pack (iv_*, Layer 248)

WP-269-PSEUDO-001: iv_grid_invariants(Pairs, Invariants):
  Extract inputs. Find dims(R,C) such that all inputs have those dims.
  Return [inv(dims(R,C))] or [].

WP-269-PSEUDO-002: iv_output_invariants(Pairs, Invariants):
  Same as iv_grid_invariants but over outputs.

WP-269-PSEUDO-003: iv_object_invariants(Pairs, Invariants):
  Extract inputs. Get color set of first input.
  If all inputs have same color set: [inv(stable_color_set(Cs))].
  Else: [].

WP-269-PSEUDO-004: iv_variant_features(Pairs, Features):
  Extract inputs. Check dims: if vary -> [feature(dims)].
  Check color set: if vary -> [feature(color_set)].
  Append results.

WP-269-PSEUDO-005: iv_consistent_delta(Pairs, Delta):
  If all pairs preserve dims -> [inv(dims_preserved)].
  If all pairs preserve color set -> [inv(color_set_preserved)].
  Append results.

WP-269-PSEUDO-006: iv_all_grids(Grids, Goal):
  maplist(Goal, Grids).

WP-269-PSEUDO-007: iv_no_grids([], _).
  iv_no_grids([G|Rest], Goal) :- \+ call(Goal, G), recurse.

WP-269-PSEUDO-008: iv_color_set(Grid, BgColor, Colors):
  Collect all non-BgColor values. Sort.

WP-269-PSEUDO-009: iv_same_color_sets(Grids, BgColor):
  Get color set of first. maplist check all have same.

WP-269-PSEUDO-010: iv_same_dims(Grids):
  Get dims of first. maplist check all have same dims.

WP-269-PSEUDO-011: iv_preserves_dims(Pairs):
  maplist(pair_preserves_dims, Pairs).

WP-269-PSEUDO-012: iv_preserves_colors(Pairs):
  maplist(pair_preserves_color_set, Pairs).

WP-269-PSEUDO-013: iv_preserves_count(Pairs, BgColor):
  For each pair: count distinct colors in In and Out. Succeed if equal.

WP-269-PSEUDO-014: iv_stable_color_map(Pairs, Map):
  For each pair: extract per-cell cm(InV,OutV) where InV\=OutV. Sort.
  Intersect across all pairs. Return common entries.


WP-270: contrast Pack (ca_*, Layer 249)

WP-270-PSEUDO-001: ca_pairwise_delta(Pairs, Deltas):
  numlist(1, N, Idxs). maplist(delta_for_pair, Idxs, Pairs, Deltas).
  delta_for_pair(I, pair(In,Out), delta(I, Changes)):
    find all chg(R,C,IV,OV) where cell at R,C differs.

WP-270-PSEUDO-002: ca_feature_profile(Grid, Profile):
  Get dims (Rows-Cols). Get non-bg colors. Count colors.
  Find dominant (most frequent non-0) color.
  sort [feat(dims,Rows-Cols), feat(color_count,N), feat(dominant_color,C)].

WP-270-PSEUDO-003: ca_profile_diff(Profile1, Profile2, Changed):
  include(not_in_profile2, Profile1, Changed).
  not_in_profile2(feat(N,V)): \+ member(feat(N,V), Profile2).

WP-270-PSEUDO-004: ca_stable_features(Pairs, Features):
  maplist(input_profile, Pairs, Profiles). ca_common_features(Profiles, Features).
  common_features: intersect all profiles.

WP-270-PSEUDO-005: ca_unstable_features(Pairs, Features):
  Union all input profiles. Subtract stable. Return remainder.

WP-270-PSEUDO-006: ca_covarying_features(Pairs, Features):
  Partition Pairs into ChangingPairs and StablePairs.
  Get features common to ALL ChangingPairs.
  Subtract features present in any StablePair.

WP-270-PSEUDO-007: ca_change_count(Pairs, Feature, N):
  include(pair_changes, Pairs, Changing).
  include(has_feature(Feature), Changing, Matching). length(Matching, N).

WP-270-PSEUDO-008: ca_rank_features(Pairs, RankedFeatures):
  Get all input features (union). For each: compute change_count / total_changing.
  msort descending by score. Return feature list in order.

WP-270-PSEUDO-009: ca_context_gate(Pairs, Gate):
  ca_rank_features(Pairs, [feat(N,V)|_]) -> Gate = feat(N,V).
  Empty rank -> Gate = feat(none, none).

WP-270-PSEUDO-010: ca_separates(Pairs, Feature, PositivePairs, Result):
  TP = pairs with Feature in PositivePairs.
  FP = pairs with Feature not in PositivePairs.
  Result is TPN / (TPN + FPN). 0.0 if none.

WP-270-PSEUDO-011: ca_correlated_features(Pairs, OutputChange, Features):
  Filter Pairs to those containing OutputChange pattern.
  Get common input features of matching pairs.

WP-270-PSEUDO-012: ca_common_context(Pairs, OutputChange, Context):
  Same as ca_correlated_features.

WP-270-PSEUDO-013: ca_discriminating_pair(Pairs, Hyp1, Hyp2, DiscPair):
  Find first pair where applying Hyp1 explains changes but Hyp2 does not (or vice versa).

WP-270-PSEUDO-014: ca_minimal_features(Pairs, Features):
  Greedy: rank by correlation. Return ranked list.


WP-271: legend Pack (lg_*, Layer 250)

WP-271-PSEUDO-001: lg_all_regions(Grid, BgColor, Regions):
  Find all non-bg cells. BFS flood-fill each unvisited seed.
  Each connected component is one region (list of r(R,C)).

WP-271-PSEUDO-002: lg_detect_legend(Grid, BgColor, LegendRegion):
  Get all_regions. Filter to small (area <= TotalArea/4).
  From small: prefer isolated (not touching other regions). Return first.

WP-271-PSEUDO-003: lg_is_legend(Region, ContentRegions):
  Area of Region <= MaxContentArea/2. Not touching any ContentRegion.

WP-271-PSEUDO-004: lg_legend_entries(LegendRegion, Entries):
  Find unique rows in region. Each row is one entry band.
  Return entry(BandIdx, BandIdx) for each.

WP-271-PSEUDO-005: lg_color_map(LegendRegion, Grid, ColorMap):
  For each row band: get first cell in row, look up color in Grid.
  Return sorted [cm(Color, BandIdx)] list.

WP-271-PSEUDO-006: lg_consistent_legend(Pairs, Legend):
  Get small regions from first pair input. Find one that has same-area
  match in all other pair inputs. Return legend_entries of that region.

WP-271-PSEUDO-007: lg_same_shape(R1, R2):
  Normalize both regions to origin. Compare sorted cell lists.

WP-271-PSEUDO-008: lg_position(Region, Grid, Position):
  Center = (MinR+MaxR)/2, (MinC+MaxC)/2.
  top if CenterR < Rows/3. bottom if >= Rows - Rows/3.
  left/right similarly. else center.


WP-272: multipair Pack (mp_*, Layer 251)

WP-272-PSEUDO-001: mp_all_input_objects(Pairs, AllObjects):
  numlist(1, N). For each Idx and pair: get non-bg colors. Yield po(Idx, Color).

WP-272-PSEUDO-002: mp_track_objects(Pairs, TrackedObjects):
  All unique colors across all pair inputs. For each color: find which pair
  indices contain it. Return tracked(Idx, Color, PairIdxList).

WP-272-PSEUDO-003: mp_invariant_objects(Tracked, Objects):
  Filter to tracked entries where length(PairList) = NPairs (all pairs).

WP-272-PSEUDO-004: mp_universal_colors(Pairs, Colors):
  Get color list for each pair input. Intersect all lists.

WP-272-PSEUDO-005: mp_variable_colors(Pairs, Colors):
  Union all input color lists. Subtract universal. Return remainder.

WP-272-PSEUDO-006: mp_cross_pair_match(Pairs, Matrix):
  For all (I, J) with I < J: get CI from pair I input, CJ from pair J input.
  Common = intersection(CI, CJ). Return match(I, J, Common).

WP-272-PSEUDO-007: mp_disappeared_objects(Pairs, Colors):
  Universal colors not present in ANY output.

WP-272-PSEUDO-008: mp_appeared_objects(Pairs, Colors):
  Colors in any output not present in any input.


WP-273: taskcat Pack (tc_*, Layer 252)

WP-273-PSEUDO-001: tc_categorize(Pairs, Category):
  Chain: is_single_rule? → single_rule.
         is_multi_step? → multi_step.
         has_context_gate? → context_gated.
         else → symbol_table.

WP-273-PSEUDO-002: tc_is_single_rule(Pairs):
  preserves_dims AND consistent_change_count AND distinct_patterns = 1.

WP-273-PSEUDO-003: tc_is_multi_step(Pairs):
  MaxN >= 4 AND (MaxN > Avg*1.5 OR distinct_patterns >= 2).

WP-273-PSEUDO-004: tc_has_context_gate(Pairs):
  Some input color C separates pairs into two groups with different change counts.

WP-273-PSEUDO-005: tc_suggest_strategies(Category, Strategies):
  single_rule → [simple_rule_search, seqinfer_2step].
  multi_step → [seqinfer_2step, seqinfer_3step, simple_rule_search].
  context_gated → [context_gate_search, seqinfer_2step, simple_rule_search].
  symbol_table → [symbol_table_learning, context_gate_search, seqinfer_2step].

WP-273-PSEUDO-006: tc_confidence(Pairs, Score):
  dims_preserved (+1) + consistent_count (+1) + distinct_patterns=1 (+1) else 0.
  Score = sum/3, clamped to [0.0, 1.0].


WP-274: seqinfer Enhancement - sq_arc2_candidates/1

sq_arc2_candidates(-Rules):
  Rules is the flat list of 66 scene-level rule terms for ARC-AGI-2 search.
  Begins with identity.
  Includes recolor(Old, New) for all integer-color pairs (1-6).
  Includes recolor_all(C) for colors 1-6.
  Includes shift(DR, DC) for deltas -3 to 3 in each axis (12 variants).
  Includes to_origin, reflect_h, reflect_v.
  Includes remove_color(C) and keep_color(C) for colors 1-6.
  Includes sort_size_desc, sort_size_asc, top_n(1), top_n(2), top_n(3).


WP-275: hyp Enhancement - hy_spatial_hyp/3, hy_structural_hyp/3, hy_sequence_hyp/4

hy_spatial_hyp(+Pairs, +Moves, -Hyp):
  For each DR-DC in Moves:
    If forall pair(In, Out) in Pairs:
      Shifted = {(R+DR, C+DC, V) | cell(R,C,V) in In, V != 0,
                                    R+DR in bounds, C+DC in bounds}
      OutCells = {(R, C, V) | cell(R,C,V) in Out, V != 0}
      msort(Shifted) = msort(OutCells)
    Return shift(DR, DC).
  Fail if no move works.

hy_structural_hyp(+Pairs, +Patterns, -Hyp):
  For each Pattern in Patterns:
    If forall pair(In, Out) in Pairs:
      hy_struct_check_(Pattern, In, Out) succeeds
    Return structural(Pattern).
  Patterns supported: dims_preserved, colors_preserved, total_nonzero_preserved,
    monotone_output, output_subset_of_input, input_subset_of_output.

hy_sequence_hyp(+Pairs, +Maps1, +Maps2, -Hyp):
  For each Map1 in Maps1, Map2 in Maps2:
    If forall pair(In, Out) in Pairs:
      hy_color_sub(Map1, In, Mid), hy_color_sub(Map2, Mid, Out)
    Return seq(Map1, Map2).
  Fail if no combination works.


WP-276: condxf Enhancement - xc_infer_gate/3

xc_infer_gate(+Pairs, +_Variants, -Gate):
  Collect all colors C from all pair inputs.
  Sort colors to get UniqColors.
  For each GateColor in UniqColors:
    WithGate = pairs where GateColor appears in SceneIn.
    WithoutGate = pairs where GateColor does NOT appear in SceneIn.
    If WithGate != [] and WithoutGate != []:
      SigsW = [change_sig(SI, SO) for pair in WithGate]
      SigsWO = [change_sig(SI, SO) for pair in WithoutGate]
      If sort(SigsW) != sort(SigsWO):
        Return gate_color(GateColor).
  Fail if no gate found.

xc_change_sig_(+SceneIn, +SceneOut, -Sig):
  CIn = colors in SceneIn.
  COut = colors in SceneOut.
  Lost = sort(CIn) - sort(COut).
  Gained = sort(COut) - sort(CIn).
  Sig = lost(Lost)-gained(Gained).


WP-277: induction Enhancement - id_cross_pair_invariants/2, id_cross_pair_variants/2

id_cross_pair_invariants(+Pairs, -Invariants):
  AllProps = [dims_preserved, colors_preserved, total_nonzero_preserved,
              monotone_input, monotone_output, bg_preserved, scale_preserved].
  Filter AllProps to those where id_pair_prop_(Prop, In, Out) holds
  for every pair(In, Out) in Pairs.
  Return the filtered list as Invariants.

id_cross_pair_variants(+Pairs, -Variants):
  Compute Invariants via id_cross_pair_invariants.
  Compute HoldsSome = props that hold for at least ONE pair.
  Variants = HoldsSome - Invariants.


ARC-AGI-2 Wave 5: stub_rank_fill - PSEUDOCODE

arc2_transform(stub_rank_fill, +Grid, -Result):
  Bg = background color (most common value in Grid).
  H = number of rows, W = number of columns.
  Stubs = all stub(V, N) terms found by scanning each column C:
    V = Grid[0][C] (must differ from Bg).
    N = length of top run of V starting at row 0.
    If N >= 1 and (N >= H or Grid[N][C] = Bg): stub exists.
  VBars = all vbar(C, TR, BR, V, K) terms found by scanning each column C:
    TR = any row where Grid[TR][C] = V (non-bg), Grid[TR-1][C] = Bg (or TR=0).
    B = Grid[TR+1][C] (must differ from V and Bg).
    BR = first row > TR+1 where Grid[BR][C] = V and all rows TR+1..BR-1 equal B.
    K = BR - TR - 1 (body length).
  Fills = for each stub(V, N):
    Cands = [(K, C, TR, BR) | vbar(C, TR, BR, V, K) in VBars].
    Sort Cands descending by K (msort then reverse).
    Select Nth entry: fill(C, TR, BR, V).
  Result = grid reconstructed row by row, cell by cell:
    If (R, C) is strictly between TR and BR for fill(C, TR, BR, FillV):
      Cell = FillV.
    Else: Cell = Grid[R][C].

arc2_induce_rule(+TrainingPairs, stub_rank_fill):
  Guard: all pairs have equal input/output dimensions.
  Guard: first row of first input has at least one non-background cell.
  Verify: arc2_transform(stub_rank_fill, In, Out) holds for every pair(In, Out).


WAVE 6: band_wrap - CONCENTRIC RECTANGULAR RINGS FROM ROW-COLOR BANDS


arc2_transform(band_wrap, Grid, Result):
  Guard: forall Row in Grid: all cells of Row equal Row[0].
  Colors = [Row[0] | Row in Grid]   (first cell of each row).
  Bands = run_length_encode(Colors)  -> [(C1,T1), (C2,T2), ..., (Cn,Tn)].
  Guard: length(Bands) >= 2.
  TotalT = sum of all Ti.
  TLast = Tn (count of last band).
  S = 2 * TotalT - TLast.
  Result = [
    [color_for_ring(min(R,C,S-1-R,S-1-C), Bands) | C in 0..S-1]
    | R in 0..S-1
  ].

color_for_ring(Ring, [(C, T) | _]):
  if Ring < T: return C.
color_for_ring(Ring, [(_, T) | Rest]):
  return color_for_ring(Ring - T, Rest).

run_length_encode([]):
  return [].
run_length_encode([C | Cs]):
  (N, Tail) = count_run(Cs, C, 1).
  return [(C, N)] ++ run_length_encode(Tail).

count_run([], _, N):
  return (N, []).
count_run([C | Cs], C, Acc):
  return count_run(Cs, C, Acc+1).
count_run([D | Cs], C, N) where D != C:
  return (N, [D | Cs]).

arc2_induce_rule(TrainingPairs, band_wrap):
  Guard: forall pair(In,_) in TrainingPairs:
           forall Row in In: all cells of Row equal Row[0].
  First pair In0 = TrainingPairs[0].In.
  Colors0 = [Row[0] | Row in In0].
  Bands0 = run_length_encode(Colors0).
  Guard: length(Bands0) >= 2.
  Guard: forall pair(In,Out) in TrainingPairs:
           arc2_transform(band_wrap, In, Out) succeeds and matches Out.


PART 270: ARC-AGI-2 WAVE 7 PSEUDOCODE - STAIRCASE LIFT


staircase_height(Grid, OddCol) ->
  H = 0
  Row = 5
  while Row >= 1 and Grid[Row][OddCol] == 5:
    H += 1
    Row -= 1
  return H

find_bar_color_and_length(Grid, Col) ->
  for Row in 1..4:
    if Grid[Row][Col] not in {0, 5}:
      Color = Grid[Row][Col]
      Length = 0
      R = Row
      while R <= 4 and Grid[R][Col] == Color:
        Length += 1
        R += 1
      return (Color, Length)
  return (0, 0)  % no bar found

compute_output_bar(H, Color, InLen) ->
  MaxEnd = max(0, 5 - H)
  OutHeight = min(InLen, MaxEnd)
  OutEnd = MaxEnd
  OutStart = OutEnd - OutHeight + 1
  return bar(Color, OutStart, OutEnd)

output_cell(R, C, OutBars) ->
  if C < 9:              return 0  % left half cleared
  if C == 9:             return 5 if R in {0,1,2,3,6,7} else 0
  if C == 19:            return 5
  if R == 0 or R == 7:   return 5
  if C is even:
    return 5 if R == 5 and 11 <= C <= 17 else 0
  if 11 <= C <= 17:      % odd bar column
    i = (C - 11) // 2
    bar = OutBars[i]
    if R == 5:                       return 5
    if 1 <= R <= 4:
      if bar.OutStart <= R <= bar.OutEnd:  return bar.Color
      else:                               return 5
    else:                            return 0
  return 0

arc2_transform staircase_lift(Grid) ->
  assert length(Grid) == 8 and length(Grid[0]) == 20
  H = [staircase_height(Grid, c) for c in {1, 3, 5, 7}]
  Bars = [find_bar_color_and_length(Grid, c) for c in {11, 13, 15, 17}]
  OutBars = [compute_output_bar(H[i], Bars[i].Color, Bars[i].Length) for i in 0..3]
  Result[R][C] = output_cell(R, C, OutBars) for all R in 0..7, C in 0..19
  return Result

arc2_induce_rule(TrainingPairs, staircase_lift) ->
  In0 = TrainingPairs[0].input
  Guard: length(In0) == 8 and length(In0[0]) == 20
  Guard: In0[0][0] == 0 and In0[0][9] == 5
  Guard: In0[7][9] == 5
  Guard: forall pair(In,Out) in TrainingPairs:
           arc2_transform(staircase_lift, In, Out) succeeds and matches Out.


PART 271: ARC-AGI-2 WAVE 13 PSEUDOCODE - ODD COL RULE

% Solve task 38007db0.  The grid is a tiling of N row sections by M col
% sections separated by uniform-value rows and cols.  One col section per
% row section has a unique interior pattern.  Output that one col section
% per row section, giving a single-column-section output with the same
% row structure as the input.

% Helper: all_same(List) - true when every element of List is equal.
all_same([]) -> true
all_same([_]) -> true
all_same([H, H | T]) -> all_same([H | T])

% Helper: strip(Row, C0, C1) - return Row[C0..C1] inclusive.
strip(Row, C0, C1) -> Row[C0 .. C1]

% Helper: majority(Values) - return the most frequent value.
majority(Values) -> mode(sort(Values))

% Step 1 - find separator rows and cols.
sep_rows(Grid) -> [R | all cells in Grid[R] are equal]
sep_cols(Grid) -> [C | all cells in column C of Grid are equal]

% Step 2 - build row sections and col sections (adjacent-pair intervals).
row_sections(SepRows) -> [(SepRows[i], SepRows[i+1]) | i in 0..len-2]
col_sections(SepCols) -> [(SepCols[j], SepCols[j+1]) | j in 0..len-2]

% Step 3 - for each row section, vote for the unique col section.
vote_unique_col(R0, R1, Grid, ColSecs) ->
  votes = empty_counter
  for R in R0+1 .. R1-1:                  % content rows only
    Strips = [strip(Grid[R], C0, C1) | (C0,C1) in ColSecs]
    MajStrip = [majority(Strips[*][i]) | i in 0..len(Strips[0])-1]
    DiffIdxs = [j | Strips[j] != MajStrip]
    if len(DiffIdxs) == 1:
      votes[DiffIdxs[0]] += 1
  if votes is non-empty:
    return argmax(votes)
  else:
    return 0                              % all identical; use first

% Step 4 - build output.
arc2_transform odd_col(Grid) ->
  SepRows = sep_rows(Grid)
  SepCols = sep_cols(Grid)
  ColSecs = col_sections(SepCols)
  RowSecs = row_sections(SepRows)
  UniqueJs = [vote_unique_col(R0, R1, Grid, ColSecs) | (R0,R1) in RowSecs]
  (C0First, C1First) = ColSecs[0]
  Result = []
  for (i, (R0, R1)) in enumerate(RowSecs):
    J = UniqueJs[i]
    (C0, C1) = ColSecs[J]
    for R in R0 .. R1-1:
      Result.append(strip(Grid[R], C0, C1))
  Result.append(strip(Grid[SepRows[-1]], C0First, C1First))
  return Result

arc2_induce_rule(TrainingPairs, odd_col) ->
  Guard: TrainingPairs is non-empty
  Guard: forall pair(In, Out) in TrainingPairs:
           arc2_transform(odd_col, In, Out) succeeds and matches Out.

-- WAVE 14: reflect_axis (task 7ed72f31) --

arc2_transform reflect_axis(Grid) ->
  NR := number of rows in Grid
  NC := number of cols in first row of Grid
  Bg := mode of all values in flatten(Grid)
  Twos := all (R,C) where Grid[R][C] = 2
  TwoClusters := 4-connected components of Twos
  ShapeComps := 4-connected components of {(R,C,V) | Grid[R][C] != Bg and Grid[R][C] != 2}
  Output := Grid
  for each comp(V, Pts) in ShapeComps:
    NearCluster := cluster in TwoClusters minimising min-manhattan-distance(Pts, cluster)
    Axis := axis_type(NearCluster)
    for each (R,C) in Pts:
      (R2,C2) := reflect(R, C, Axis)
      if (R2,C2) is within bounds: Output[R2][C2] := V
  return Output

axis_type(Cluster) ->
  if |Cluster| = 1: return point(R0, C0) where Cluster = [(R0,C0)]
  Rows := {R | (R,C) in Cluster}
  if |Rows| = 1: return h(R0) where R0 is the unique row
  Cols := {C | (R,C) in Cluster}
  if |Cols| = 1: return v(C0) where C0 is the unique col
  return point(R0,C0) where (R0,C0) is the first cell of Cluster

reflect(R, C, h(R0)) -> (2*R0 - R, C)
reflect(R, C, v(C0)) -> (R, 2*C0 - C)
reflect(R, C, point(R0,C0)) -> (2*R0 - R, 2*C0 - C)

arc2_induce_rule(TrainingPairs, reflect_axis) ->
  Guard: TrainingPairs is non-empty
  Guard: forall pair(In, Out) in TrainingPairs:
           arc2_transform(reflect_axis, In, Out) succeeds and matches Out.

% ARC-AGI-2 Wave 15 pseudocode - period_repair rule

arc2_transform(period_repair, Grid, Out):
  Bg := mode of all cells in Grid
  Grid1 := maplist(pr2_repair_row_(Bg), Grid)  % row repair
  GridT := transpose(Grid1)
  GridT2 := maplist(pr2_repair_row_(Bg), GridT)  % column repair via transpose
  Out := transpose(GridT2)

pr2_repair_row_(Bg, Row, Fixed):
  Wall := first V in Row where V != Bg  (or none)
  if Wall = none: Fixed = Row
  else:
    WallPositions := [i | Row[i] = Wall]
    if |WallPositions| < 2: Fixed = Row
    else: Fixed := pr2_fix_segs_(Row, WallPositions)

pr2_fix_segs_(Row, [W1, W2 | Rest], Fixed):
  InLen := W2 - W1 - 1
  if InLen >= 5:
    Inner := Row[W1+1 .. W2-1]
    (P, Errs) := pr2_best_period_(Inner)
    if Errs != []: Row1 := apply_fixes(Row, W1+1, Errs)
    else: Row1 := Row
  else: Row1 := Row
  Fixed := pr2_fix_segs_(Row1, [W2 | Rest])

pr2_best_period_(Seq):
  N := |Seq|; MaxP := N // 2
  Candidates := [(|Errs|, P, Errs) |
    P in 2..MaxP,
    Base := pr2_majority_base_(Seq, P),
    MinSupp := pr2_min_support_(Seq, P, Base),
    MinSupp >= 0.75,
    Errs := pr2_errors_(Seq, P, Base),
    1 <= |Errs| <= 3]
  if Candidates = []: return (none, [])
  sort Candidates by (|Errs| ASC, P ASC)
  return first candidate

pr2_majority_base_(Seq, P):
  for r in 0..P-1:
    Vals := [Seq[i] | i in 0..|Seq|-1, i mod P = r]
    Base[r] := mode(Vals)
  return Base

pr2_min_support_(Seq, P, Base):
  for r in 0..P-1:
    Vals := [Seq[i] | i in 0..|Seq|-1, i mod P = r]
    Supp[r] := count(v in Vals where v = Base[r]) / |Vals|
  return min(Supp)

pr2_errors_(Seq, P, Base):
  return [err(i, Seq[i], Base[i mod P]) |
    i in 0..|Seq|-1, Seq[i] != Base[i mod P]]

arc2_induce_rule(Pairs, period_repair):
  Guard: Pairs non-empty; all pairs preserve grid dimensions.
  Guard: first training input has a non-background element in row 1 (wall marker).
  Verify: forall pair(In, Out) in Pairs: arc2_transform(period_repair, In, Out).

Score impact: 14/120 = 11.67% -> 15/120 = 12.50% (+1 task, +0.83%).

% ARC-AGI-2 Wave 16 pseudocode - legend_fill rule
arc2_transform(legend_fill, Grid, Out):
  Bg = mode(flatten(Grid)).
  (Keys, Vals) = lf_legend_(Grid, Bg).
  KVPairs = zip(Keys, Vals).
  Out = foldl([K-V, G -> lf_apply_fill_(G, Bg, K, V)], KVPairs, Grid).

lf_legend_(Grid, Bg) -> (Keys, Vals):
  Candidates = all valid 2xN row-blocks + all valid Nx2 col-blocks.
    A block (Raw1, Raw2, Len) is valid if:
      ALL cells in both rows (or cols) are non-Bg,
      the sub-rows (or sub-cols) are not identical (Raw1 != Raw2),
      Len >= 2.
  (Raw1, Raw2) = candidate with maximum Len.
  FC = frame_colors(Grid, Bg).
    Frame color = non-Bg color C with at least one enclosed Bg neighbor.
  N1 = |{x in Raw1 : x in FC}|, N2 = |{x in Raw2 : x in FC}|.
  if N1 >= N2: Keys=Raw1, Vals=Raw2. else: Keys=Raw2, Vals=Raw1.

lf_apply_fill_(Grid, Bg, K, V) -> Grid':
  Enclosed = enclosed_bg(Grid, Bg).
  KCells = {R-C in Enclosed : sort(non_bg_neighbors(Grid, R, C)) = [K]}.
  Grid' = Grid with all KCells set to V.

enclosed_bg(Grid, Bg):
  Exterior = BFS from all boundary Bg cells through Bg-only 4-neighbors.
  return all_bg(Grid) minus Exterior.

arc2_induce_rule(Pairs, legend_fill):
  Guard: Pairs non-empty.
  Guard: lf_legend_(In0, Bg0, _, _) succeeds for first training input.
  Verify: forall pair(In, Out) in Pairs: arc2_transform(legend_fill, In, Out).

Score impact: 15/120 = 12.50% -> 16/120 = 13.33% (+1 task, +0.83%).

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 17: frame_target pseudocode (2026-06-28)
INDUCE frame_target(TrainingPairs):
  Get background Bg from mode of first grid.
  Build DirMap = ft_build_dir_map(Grid, Bg):
    For each non-Bg non-4 color C: find legend rectangle for C; derive (Dr, Dc).
  Require DirMap non-empty.
  Verify forall pair(In, Out): arc2_transform(frame_target, In, Out).

TRANSFORM frame_target(Grid):
  Rebuild DirMap and DirColors (set of frame colors).
  Find all dot-4 positions: Fours.
  For each dot at (R, C):
    FColor = ft_enclosing_color(Grid, DirColors, R, C):
      Ray-shoot in 4 directions; unique DirColors member hit = FColor.
    (Dr, Dc) = DirMap[FColor].
    (NR, NC) = ft_shoot(Grid, FColor, R, C, Dr, Dc):
      Repeat: next = (R+Dr, C+Dc).
      Stop if diagonal: any of (R+Dr,C), (R,C+Dc), (R+Dr,C+Dc) = FColor.
      Stop if cardinal: next cell = FColor.
  Build output: clear source positions to Bg; place 4 at destination.

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 18: tip_escape pseudocode (2026-06-28)
tip_escape(Grid) ->
  AllComps <- bfs8_components(Grid, background=0)      // 8-connected
  Pairs    <- [(S,M) : S in AllComps, M in AllComps,
               S.color != M.color,
               |M.cells| < |S.cells|,
               bb(M.cells) inside bb(S.cells)]
  assert Pairs != []
  for each (Shape, Marker) in Pairs do
    Tips <- [dir, (r,c) : dir in {left,right,up,down},
             exactly one Shape.cell at extreme(dir)]
    EscDir, TipR, TipC <-
      first apex in Tips            // perpendicular diverging arms
      else argmax_tip projection    // escape_vec = shape_cen - marker_cen
    EscZone <- ordered cells from (TipR,TipC)+dir to grid edge
    N       <- |Marker.cells|
    Grid    <- clear(Grid, Marker.cells)
    Grid    <- set(Grid, EscZone[0 .. min(N,|EscZone|)-1], Marker.color)
  return Grid

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 19: segment_ext pseudocode (2026-06-28)
segment_ext(Grid) ->
  // Phase 1: process each 4-corner junction cell (value 4)
  Prio <- compute_fill_priority(Grid)   // none | h | v
  for each (R,C) with Grid[R][C]=4 do
    StubDir <- stub_direction(Grid, R, C)   // dir of longest same-color run or adjacent 2-corner
    ArmColor <- arm_color(Grid, R, C, StubDir)  // first non-bg/non-junction color in StubDir
    KeptJunction <- (R,C) + StubDir
    FirstStub <- KeptJunction + StubDir
    IStub <- contiguous_nonbg(Grid, FirstStub, StubDir)
    CasStub <- bfs_from_2corner_neighbors(Grid, IStub, blocked={4-corner,KeptJunction}+IStub)
    FarRem <- far_segments_no_perp(Grid, FirstStub, StubDir, ArmColor, blocked=...)
    ToRemove <- IStub + CasStub + FarRem
    Grid <- set(Grid, ToRemove, 0)
    Grid <- set(Grid, (R,C), ArmColor)
    ExtDir <- -StubDir
    Grid <- extend_to_boundary(Grid, (R,C)+ExtDir, ExtDir, ArmColor)
  // Phase 2: convert remaining 2-corner cells
  for each (R,C) with Grid[R][C]=2 do
    Grid[R][C] <- first non-bg non-junction neighbor color
  // Phase 3: gap fill
  for each (R,C) do
    Vpp <- Grid[R][C]; Vin <- OrigGrid[R][C]
    H <- hfill(Grid, R, C)     // left=right=Color and Color != 0
    V <- vfill(Grid, R, C)     // above=below=Color and Color != 0
                                // AND at least one neighbor is pure-vertical
                                //   (pure-vertical: no same-color horizontal neighbor)
    Out[R][C] <- fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H, V)
  return Out

fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H=none, V=none) = Vpp
fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H=none, V)      = V if V!=Vin else Vpp
fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H, V=none)      = H if H!=Vin else Vpp
fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H, V) where H=V = H if H!=Vin else Vpp
fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H, V) where H!=Vin and V=Vin =
  H if (Vin=0 or Prio=none) else Vpp  // protect existing arm cells in 4-corner grids
fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H, V) where V!=Vin and H=Vin = V
fill_rule(Prio, Vpp, Vin, H, V) // true conflict: H!=Vin, V!=Vin, H!=V
  = H if Prio=h else V           // extension direction decides

compute_fill_priority(Grid):
  C4s <- all (R,C) with Grid[R][C]=4
  if C4s = []: return none
  ExtDirs <- [(-DR,-DC) : (R,C) in C4s, (DR,DC) = stub_direction(Grid,R,C)]
  if any (DR,DC) in ExtDirs with DR!=0: return v
  return h

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 20: section_tile pseudocode (2026-06-29)
section_tile(Grid) ->
  // Step 1: find all-1 rows and all-1 cols
  DivRows <- {R | all cells in Grid[R] == 1}
  DivCols <- {C | all cells in Grid[*][C] == 1}
  // Step 2: extract non-trivial sections
  RowRanges <- ranges(0..NRows, DivRows)   // intervals between dividers
  ColRanges <- ranges(0..NCols, DivCols)
  Sections  <- {slice(Grid, Rows, Cols) | Rows in RowRanges, Cols in ColRanges,
                section is non-trivial}
  // Step 3: classify sections
  Shape1 <- section with (any 0 cell) and (>= 2 distinct non-zero values)
  Solids <- Sections - {Shape1}
  // Step 4: derive tile count from shape2
  Shape2 <- first solid section
  TotalNZ <- count of non-zero cells in Shape2
  N <- TotalNZ // 2
  // Step 5: derive color mapping
  ColorSolids <- Solids - {Shape2}   // remaining solid sections in order
  Colors <- [uniform_value(S) | S in ColorSolids]
  // Step 6: find inner bbox of shape1
  BboxRows, BboxCols <- min/max rows and cols of non-zero cells in Shape1
  InnerPattern <- slice(Shape1, BboxRows, BboxCols)
  // Step 7: build tiled output
  Copies <- []
  for I in 1..N do
    Copy <- apply_color_map(InnerPattern, Colors)
    Copies <- Copies ++ [Copy]
    if I < N: Copies <- Copies ++ [separator_cols_of_2(BboxCols)]   // 2-cell separator
  return stack_vertically(Copies)   // or horizontally depending on layout axis
